Ukusakamana kwa Bashicilye ba Buteko bwa calo ca Wales (AMs) pa ‘kumoneka nga abashikwete mano’
Pali ukusakamana kumo pakati ka Bashicilye ba Buteko pe langulushi lyakuti ishina lya cifulo cabo lifwile ukucinja ukuba MWPs (Member of the Welsh Parliament).
Ili langulushi lishile pamulandu wafilepekanishiwa ifyakucinja ishina lya ici cilye ukuti cileitwa Welsh Parliament.
Bashicilye ba Buteko mu fipani fyonse ifya mitekele nabasakamana ukutila ici kuti caleta ukusekwa.
Shichilye umo uwakuciputulwa ca Labour atile ibumba lyakwe nalisakamana ukutila “cileumfwika kwati ni Twp na Pwp."
Kuli ba kabelenga abali kunse ya calo ca Wales: Muchi Welsh twp ipilibula ubupuba elyo pwp ipilibula ubusaali.
Membala umo uwa cipani ca Plaid atile icipani conse “tacitemenwe” kabili nacilandako na ifyakupyanikishapo fimbi.
Umo uwamu cipani ca Welsh Conservative atile icipani cakwe "cilefwaya ukwishibilapo nafimbi” pakucinja kwe shina, lelo atile uyu musango uwamubwipi uwakutolokelamo mumilandile ukufuma kuli MWP ukuya kwisiwi lya Bupuba.
Muli uyu musango icilembo caci Welsh ica w cilandwa mukupalana ne filandwa icilembo ca u mu Cingeleshi caku Yorkshire.
Ba Assembly Commission, abalepanga ifunde lyakuleta uku kucinja kwe shina, batile: "Ubusalo bwakulekelesha pa bulondoloshi bonse ubo ba Membala ba Cilye ca Buteeko betwa bukabafye kuli ba membala abene."
Ifunde lyamu 2017 ilya Buteeko bwa calo ca Wales lyalipeele amaka kuli bashicilye ba calo ca Wales ukucinja ishina lya cilye.
Mu mweshi wa Kapepo-Kakalamba, Akabungwe ka uyu mulimo kalilembele insebo shakufwailisha kwa cintubwingi pafyo abantu balefwaya umo umwasangilwe ukuti abantu abengi balefwaya ukuti icilye cileitwa Welsh Parliament.
Pa mulandu we shina lya cifulo caba AMs, Akabungwe kasalilepo ishina lya Welsh Parliament Members nangu WMPs, lelo ubusalo bwa MWP ebwatungililwe sana mu kufwailisha kwa cintubwingi.
Ba AM pali ino nshita balefwaya amashina yakusalapo nayambi, lelo ubwafya bwakufika pa kusuminishanya kuti bwaba cakukalifya umutwe ku Uuletungulula uyu Mulandu Elin Jones, uulecetekelwa ukupeela ubwanshiko bwe funde pali uku kucinja kwe shina mu milungu iinono.
Mwifunde lya uku kucinja mukasangwa ukucinja kumbi pafyo ici cilye cibomba, ukubikapo na mafunde pakufumyapo kwaba AM elyo nemipangilwe ya mibombele ya komiti.
Ba AM bakakwata ukuvota kwakushalikisha palipusho lyafyo balingile ukwitwa ilyo bakalalanshanya pali ili ifunde.
Abena Macedonia balekwata ukusala kwa cinkumbawile pakucinja kwe shina lya calo cabo
Bakasala bakalasala pa Sande pakumona ngacakuti bengacinja ishina lya calo cabo ukuti lileitwa "Republic of North Macedonia."
Uku kusala kwapekanishiwe mukufwaya ukupwisha ukulwishanya kwa myaka ukwabapo necalo icinamupalamano ica Greece, icakwata pulovinsi imo iitwa Macedonia.
Icalo ca Athens panshita iitali calilanda ukutila ishina lya calo icina mupalamano icaku kapinda kakukuso lyaba kwati lilafwaya ukupoka amaka ku mpanga yabo elyo kabili panshita iitali balakana ukuti ici calo cibe nicimembala camu EU na NATO.
Kateeka wa calo ca Macedonia, Gjorge Ivanov, uukanya kuli uku kusala kwa cinkumbawile ukwa kucinja kwe shina, atile takasumine kuli uku kusala.
Nangu cibefyo, abaletungilila uku kusala, ukubikapo na Prime Minister Zoran Zaev, baletila ukucinja kwe shina emutengofye wakulipila pakusuminshiwa ukwingila mu EU na NATO.
Inyenjele shamu St. Martin Shaikala Tondolo ilyo Ifilonganino fyamu Harlem Filelwishanya
"Ukulingana ne milumbe yakale, abantu abakalamba abo nalandapo nabo batila paali akabale ne cilonganino pali cila cinshoko," efyalandile ba Adams.
"Ilelo, ifi fyonse takuli."
Batile ukuluba kwa tubale kwalyumfwikike.
Batile, "Abantu nomba beshisha mu misango iyaibelako" shino nshiku.
"Utubale nomba tatuli nincende shakwishamo umo abantu baya cila nshita."
Lelo ku filonganino fyena, nabasakamana ukutila indalama ishilefuma kukushitisha ifipe tashakakokole ngefyo intungulushi shileenekela, "elyo mukwangufyanyafye fikabwelela kuntu fyatendekele."
Balundilepo nokutila, ifilonganino kuti fyapyanikishiwapo nefikulwa fyakwikalamo umukalaikala imisango ya bantu abashakafwilishe ukutila ishi ncende shingaba incende ishamutende.
"Abantu abengi abakalashita imiputule muli ifi fikulwa bakaba basungu," efyo balandile, "neci cikalenga ubushiku bwakwisalilila kwa filonganino ukufika bwangu pantu limbi tacakacitike icakutila abantu bonse abakalaingila muli iyi miputule bakasanguka bamembala ba ifi filonganino."
Ifilonganino fyonse fyakulilwe naba mapepo ya basungu ilyo incende ya Harlem tailasanguka incende ya bantu bafita - Metropolitan Community mu mwaka wa 1870 elyo nokwisaba St. Martin panuma ya myaka ikumi.
Ababalilepo ukulonganinamo muli iyi ncende ba Methodist abasungu bafuminemo mu myaka yamuma 1930.
Icilonganino ca bafita abalelonganina mupepi ebaishilepyana muli ici cikuulwa.
Icilonganino ca St. Martin caishilesendwa no lukuta lwa mapepo ulwaletungululwa naba Rev. John Howard Johnson, uwatungulwile ukukanya kwaba shimakwebo mu Musebo 125, umusebo uwakulisha mu Harlem, abalekanya ukubomfya nangu ukusumbula abantu bafita.
Umulilo uwaliko mu mwaka wa 1939 washile icikuulwa icaonaika sana, lelo ilyo abasambi baba Father Johnson balepanga amanshiko ya kukuula cipyacipya, bapangile inyenjele ishitwa carillon.
Ba Rev. David Johnson, abana baba Father Johnson abapyene pa St. Martin, mucilumba baitile inyenjele sha carillon nga "inyenjele sha bapina."
Incenshi iyalelisha inyenjele ya carilllon mu mweshi wa Chikungu-lupepo yena yaleita ishi nynjele ishina limbi: "Ubutala bwa lutambi" na "icilimba ca myaka icishingapyanikishiwapo."
Iyi ncenshi, iyeshina lya Tiffany Ng iyapa University of Michigan, kabili yatile iyi enyenjele yakubalilapo ukulishiwa na kalisha wafilimba uwafita mwisonde lyonse, uweshina lya Dionisio A. Lind, uwakukile ku nyenjele iikulu iyapa Riverside Church apo apapita nomba imyaka 18.
Ba Merriweather batile icilonganino ca St. Martin tacafwailepo uwakumupyana.
Ifyacitika pa St. Martin panshita ya myeshi iyapitapo lyashi ilyakosa ilya bakapanga na bakakuula, bamo abaletelwe no butungulushi bwa cilonganino, bambi nabo baletelwe na Episcopal diocese.
Akabungwe kaletungulula parishi - aketwa vestry - umusangwa intungulushi sha cilonganino - kalilembele inkalata kuli ba diocese mu mweshi wa Cikungu-lupepo namasakamiko yakutila ba diocese "balefwaya ukutambikisha ifya malipilo" ku kabungwe ka vestry, nangu cakuti aka kabungwe takaibimbilemo mukwingisha bakapanga na bakakuula abo ba diocese batumine.
Bamembala bamo abamucilonganino baliilishenye pa mulandu wa kubulisha icishinka kulubali lwaba diocese.
Ci Shaki cacena umulemendo wa myaka 13 uwaleikata isabi lya lobster mu California
Icilisabi ci Shaki calisansa no kucena umulumendo wa myaka 13 ilyo aleikata isabi lya lobster mu California pa bushiku bwa kwiswila inshita ya kwikata isabi lya lobster, efyalandile abakalamba bancende.
Ubusanso bwacitike ilyo tacilafika pa 7 a.m. mupepi na Beacon's Beach mu Encinitas.
Ba Chad Hammel baebele umulabasa wa KSWB-TV mu musumba wa San Diego ukutila aleowa pamo nabanankwe mupepi ne nsa imo pa Chibelushi ulucelo ilyo aumfwile umulumendo alapuundilila abakumupususha elyo baileko pamo ne bumba ukuyamwafwilisha ukumufumya mu menshi.
Ba Hammel pakubala baletontonkanya ukuti limbi kusamwafye kwa mulandu wa kwikata isabi lya lobster, lelo panuma “aishileumfwa umulumendo alepunda ati, ‘Nasumwa!
Nasumwa!'
Ifupa lyapa mabeya lyonse lyalifumishiwa," Ba Hammel batile bailemona ifi ilyo bafilkile pa mulumendo.
"Natendeke ukupundilila bonse ukuti bafume mu menshi: 'Muli ci Shaki mu menshi!'" Efyo ba Hammel balundilepo.
Umulumendo alisendelwe ne ndeke ukutwalwa ku Chipatala ca Baice ica Rady mu San Diego umo alembelwe pa butantiko bwa bali mubusanso sana.
Umutundu wa ci shaki icamusanshile tawaishibikwe bwino.
Umukalamba uulolesha mu kupususha kwa bantu Capt. Larry Giles alandile ilyo alelanda ku calo ukutila icisabi ci shaki calimoneke muli iyi ncende imilungu inono iyapitilepo, lelo calemoneka kwati te musango wa shaki uwingaleta ubusanso.
Ba Giles balundilepo nokutila uyu mulumendo alikwete ifilonda ifibi nganshi ku mubili wa pamulu wa musana.
Abakalamba ba ncende baliisala inshila yakuila ku Ponto Beach mu Casablad ku Swami mu Ecinitas pa nsa ishili 48 pakuti bengafwailisha ifyacitike elyo nokubikapo ubucingo.
Ba Giles batile mwaliba imisango yama shaki ukufika kuli 135 muli iyi ncende, lelo imisango iingi tayakwata ubusanso.
Amanshiko yaba Sainsbury yaingila mu mushiika wa mafuta yakuwamya imibili iyamu UK
Ba Sainsbury baleingila mu Boots, Superdrug na Debenhams ne fiputulwa fya mafuta yakuwamya inkanda umusangwa ababomfi abakanshiwa.
Pamo nga ulubali lwakwingila mu mushiika wa mafuta yakuwamya imibili iyaku UK iyakwata icipendo ca £2.8bn, iilekulikakofye ilyo ifyakufwala nefya mumayanda filebwelela panuma, incende umushitishiwa amafuta yakuwamya imibili ikalaeishiwa mu mashitolo ayali 11 mu calo conse elyo nokutwalwa ku mashitolo nayambi uyu mwaka.
Ukubika kwa lupiya mu mafuta yakuwamya imibili kwaisa pakuti amashitolo ayengi yesushishe amashelufu umwali kale ama TV, ama microwave elyo nefipe fimbi ifyamu mayanda.
Ba Sainsbury batile balundako ubukulu bwa mafuta yakuwamya imibili ukufika kumisango iili 3,000, ukubikapo na Revlon, Essie, Tweezerman elyo na Dr. PawPaw pamuku wakubalilapo.
Amashitolo nayambi ayabako nakale pamo nga L'Oreal, Maybelline na Burt's Bees nayo yakakwatamo incende mu miputule iyalembwapo iyapalana nailya iisangwa mu mashitolo ayali nga Boots.
Ili shitolo likalamba kabili liletendeka cipyacipya amakwebo ya Boutique pakuti ifipe ifingi fibe fyakubomfya nabantu abashibomfya ifyanama-nama pantu abengi efyo balefwaisha makama imisepela.
Mukulunda pali ico, ishitolo ilishitisha amafuta ayanunkila ilya Fragrance nabo bakalaeshamo amafuta yabo mu mashitolo ya Sainsbury ilyakubalilapo ilyaiswike mu Croydon, south London, umulungu wapwile elyo ilyabubili lileisulwa mukutendeka kwa uyu mwaka mu Selly Oak, Birmingham.
Ukushita kwa fipe pa intaneti elyo nokusela ukuya kukushita ifyakulya cilabushiku ifyampendwa iinono pa mashitolo ayali mupepi cilepilibula ukuti amashitolo ayakulu yalingile ukubombesha sana pakupatikisha abantu ukalaya mukushita muli aya mashitolo.
Ba Mike Coupe, intungulushi nkalamba iye shitolo lya Sainsbury, batile amashitolo ayashitisha ifipe fyabo yalatendeka ukumoneka nga matuuka yamufiputulwa ilyo ili shitolo likalamba lilefwaya ukulwisha ba Aldi naba Lidl abalebwesha imitengo ku milimo iyingi nefipe ifishili fyakulya.
Ishitolo lya Sainsbury lyatendeka kale ukusalanganya umwakushitishisha Argos mumatuuka ayengi nokupanga impendwa shama Habitat ukutendeka ilyo lyashitile amatuuka yonse yabili apo apapita nomba ne myaka ibili, ayo eyo batile yalilenga ukuti ukushitisha kwa fipe fyabo kuye pamulu nokukwatilapo icibwesha nacimbi.
Ukwesha kwa ili ishitolo ukwa kunuma ukwakubukulusha ifiputululwa fya mafuta yakusuba ne miti yalifilikwe.
Ba Sainsbury's balyeseshepo ukubombela pamo naba Boots mu kutendeka kwa mwaka wa 2000, lelo ubwafya bwaishileima panuma yakulwishanya mumyakanishishe ya ndalama ishalepangwa mumatuuka ya miti aya ili shitolo.
Ubu bwanshiko ubupya bwaisa panuma ishitolo lya Sainsbury lyashitishe ituuka lya 281 ilya makwebo ya miti kuli ba Celesio, abene ba Lloyds Pharmacy chain, pa mutengo wa £125m, apo apapita nomba imyaka itatu.
Batile ituuka lya Lloyds kuti lyabomba umulimo uukalamba muli ubu bwanshiko, ukupitila mukulundako imisango naimbi iya mafuta yakuwamya inkanda ukubikapo na mafuta ya La Roche-Posay na Vichy mu matuuka yane.
Ba Paul Mills-Hicks, abakondenkanya amakwebo mwi shitolo lya Sainsbury, batile: "Twalyalula imimonekele nemyumfwikile ya ncende sha mafuta yakuwamya inkanda pakulunda ubusuma bwa ncende kuli ba kasitoma besu.
Kabili twalibikamo indalama shakukansha ababomfi abakalasangwa lyonse nokupeela bumpandamano.
Imisango ya fipe fyesu yapangwa mumusango uwakukwanisha ubukabilo bonse elyo nencende ishayemba kabili ishisangwa konsekonse shilepilibula ukuti nomba tuli pamulu mukuba ishitolo ilyakwita abantu bonse mukupusanako ne misango yakale iya mishitile yafintu."
Ba Peter Jones 'nabafulwa' panuma ba Holly Willoughby bafuma mu makwebo ya £11 million
Kanyekanye we bumba lya Dragons Den uweshina lya Peter Jones 'nafulwa sana' panuma umubomfi waku mulabasa wa fikope Holly Willoughby afuma mu makwebo ya ndalama £11 million na makwebo yakwe ayapa mikalile pakuti engaposa amano ku bwampano bwa makwebo ayapya naba Marks and Spencer naba ITV
Willoughby takwete inshita yakubombela pafipe fyamu mayanda nefibombelo fimbi ifitwa Truly.
Amakwebo ya aba bantu babili yapashanishiwe ku fipe fya Goop ifyakwa Gwyneth Paltrow's.
Kasabankanya wa pulogilamu iitwa This Morning, uuli ne myaka 37, aile pa Instagram nokubilisha ukuti alefumamo.
Ukufuma kwakwa Holly Willoughby mu Dragons" Den nakulenga ukuti Peter Jones afulwe sana pantu Holly nafuma mu makwebo ya fipe fya mikalile ayalebapela sana indalama mukashita akanono - ukuti abike amano kubwampano bwa makwebo ayapya naba Marks & Spencer na ITV.
Abatupeelako ilyashi batile Jones "alifulwa sana" ilyo umukashana uwalumbuka sana pa TV asumine pa kukumana ukwakakata nganshi pali Cibili pe ofeshi lyabo ilikalamba mu Marlow, Buckinghamshire, ukutila amakwebo yakwe ayapya - ayakwete indalama £1.5 million - yalepilibula ukuti takwete nomba inshita iyakwakanya ku makwebo yabo aya fipe fya mung’anda nefibombelo fimbi aya Truly.
Aya makwebo yalipashanishiwe ku fipe fya Goop ifyaba Gwyneth Paltrow elyo yalemoneka ukuti kuti yakula ukufika ku miku ibili iya cuma cakwa Willoughby's ica £11 million.
Ilyo Willoughby, uuli ne myaka 37, aile pa Instagram ukubilisha ukuti alefumamo mu Truly, Jones alifuma mu Britain nokuya kung’anda imo pang’anda shintu aya mukutushishako cuti.
Abatupeelako ilyashi batile: "Amakwebo ya Truly eyaba pamulu sana pali fintu Holly atemwisha.
Yali nokuba makwebo yakwe ayasuma ayali nokumutwala pa ntanshi mu myaka iingi iileisa kuntanshi .
Ubusalo bwakwe ubwakufumamo nabupapusha bonse abakwatamo ulubali.
Tapali nangu umo uwasumine kufyacitike pali Cibili, fyalipalamisha sana ku kwisula kwa aya makwebo.
Pali icikulwa cafipe icaisula pa Marlow HQ ifyo ifilelolelwa ukushitishiwa."
Abafikukile insakwe baletila ukufumamo kwakwa kasambankanya wa pulogilamu ya This Morning, uwaba umo pabekashi bamu Britain abakwatisha indalama, kuti kwalufyanya imibombele ya ili tuuka iliboomba mu fintu ifingi apali ama kushoni nama kandulo pamo nefyakufwala elyo nefipe fyamu mayanda, pamofye nokucelwisha kwa kwisula kwa ili tuuka.
Elyo kabili kuti capilibulu impela ya bucibusa ubwabapo pa nshita iitali.
Umufyashi wa bana batatu Willoughby no mukashi wakwe Dan Baldwin baliba pa bwampano na Jones no mukashi wakwe Tara Capp pa myaka ikumi.
Willoughby atampile amakwebo ya Truly pamo na Capp mu mwaka wa 2016 elyo Jones, uuli ne myaka 52, ailundileko mu mweshi wa Machi.
Cuti wa aba bantu babili pamo na Jones yalikwata icipendo ca 40 pesenti mu makwebo ya TV ayakwa Baldwin.
Willoughby ewalaba umwiminishi wa makwebo yaba M&S elyo alapyana pali Ant McPartlin nga uwakulaletako pulogilamu ya ITV iitwa I'm A Celebrity.
Abatupeelako ilyashi abapalama kuli Jones mailo ubushiku batile "Tekuti tulandepo ifili fyonse pali ubu bwampano bwa makwebo."
Ukusosa ukwakosa ‘napanuma twatemwana’
Alesekesha pa mashiwi yakususha ayo engasenda mu lyashi pamulandu nokulandapo utumashiwi tumo uto bamo bengatila “tatulingile kuli kateeka” elyo nokutungilila sana kateeka wa calo ca North Korea.
Nichisnhi icalengele Kateeka Trump afuminwemo sana?
Trump atile mwishiwi lyakwe ilya mitumfya "nga mukusabankanya kwe lyashi".
"Nshasulileko kufili fyonse."
Alishibe ukuti Kim alefwaisha ukukumana nakabili panuma yakukumana kwakubalilapo ukwacitike mu Singapore mu mweshi wa Juni uko Trump atile lutampulo ulukulu ulwakulola mukupokolola iminshinga ya nyukiliya ku calo ca North Korea.
Lelo ukulanshanya pakupokolola iminshinga ya nyukiliya nakwiminina.
Ukucila pa myeshi itatu ukufuma pa kulanshanya ukwali ku Singapore Umukalamba umo mu buteeko bwa calo ca North Korea Ri Yong Ho aebele intungulushi sha calo pa U.N. General Assembly pa Cibelushi ukutila incende yaku Kapinda kaku Kuso tailemonapo "ubwasuko ubwayana" ukufuma ku calo ca U.S. ukuya ku kupwisha bwangu ukwa maka ya minshinga mu calo ca North Korea.
Nakuba, bamwene ukuti, icalo ca U.S. cilekonkanyapo ifibindo pakuti fye cibikepo umutitikisha uukulu.
Ba Trump bena mukulanda kwabo bacimwenene mukwanguka nokwenekela ukuti fyonse fyalabafye bwino.
Batile "Tulebombafye bwino necalo ca North Korea,"
"Twali nokuya ku nkondo naba North Korea.
Imintapendwa ya bantu nga yalipaiwe.
Nomba natukwata ubwampano ubu ubusuma."
Batile ukubomba kwabo ukwakuleta ubwampano naba Kim nakuleta insebo ishisuma - ukupwisha ukwesha kwa minshinga yama roketi, ukwafwilisha ukupususha abaiketwe nokuleta ifitumbi fyabashilika ku calo cabo.
Balecingilila ukulanda kwabo ukwaibelako mukulanda pa bwampano bwabo naba Kim.
"Caliba icayanguka ukuba nga kateeka, lelo munshita yakukwata abantu 10,000 panse abalekabila ukwingila muli iyi ncende iyaisula, ngatwacikwata abantu ukufika kuli 200 abeminine palya," efyasosele ba Trump, ninshi balesonta pa bantu abaiminine ukulungatana nabena.
Amabimbi ne Cinkukuma ifyaku Indonesia fyaonaula Icilila, nokwipaya Imyanda ya Bantu
Panuma ya busanso bwa cinkukuma caku Lombok, kucakumwenako, utubungwe utushili twabuteeko utwakunse ya calo twalyebelwe ukuti tatulefwaikwa.
Nangu cakuti ukucila pali 10 pesenti yabantu mu Lombok bashele ukwabula apakwikala, icalo tacabilishepo ukuti kuli ubusanso bwa calo, ico icingalenga ukuti kufumeko ubwafwilisho bwe sonde lyonse.
"Inshita ishingi, ku cabulanda, balilandafye apabuuta tutu ukuti tabalekabila ubwafwilisho ubuli bonse, kanshi caliba icayafyako,” efyasosele ba Ms. Sumbung.
Panshita iyo akabungwe ka Save Children kalepekanya ubulendo bwakuya ku Palu, tabeshibe bwino ngacakuti ababomfi ukufuma ku fyalo fimbi kuti babomba muli ilya ncende.
Ba Sutopo, abalandilako akabungwe kalolesha ku masanso, batile abakalamba ba buteeko bwa Indonesia bacili balececeta ubukulu bwa busanso ku Palu nokumona ngacakuti utubungwe ukufuma kunse ya calo kuti twasuminishiwa ukulundako ku milimo ya bwafwilisho.
Ukulingana nokusunkana kwa mushili uko icalo ca Indonesia cipitamo inshita ishingi, ici calo cili pabusanso ubukulu ubwakuti taciipekenye bwino ifyakupusuka ku cipyu ca bubumbo.
Nangu cakuti incende shakuubamo amabimbi nashikuulwa mu ncende ya Aceh, incende shimbi ishamumbali ya bemba tashikwete.
Ubwafya bwakukanakwata inyenjele yakusoka abantu kuli aya mabimbi mu ncende a palu, nangu cakuti ubusoko bwena eko bwali, ecilengele sana ukuti abantu abengi bafwe.
Panshita ishingi, ukwenda pakati ka filila fya calo ca Indonesia ifingi kwalibako ukwayafya.
Amasanso ya bubumbo eyakoseshako ne myendele.
Icombo ca cipatala icali mu Lombok umwakundapila abasanshilwe ku cinkukuma cili pabulendo bwakuya ku Palu, lelo kuti casenda ne nshiku shitatu pakuti cingafika ku ncende ukubelele ubusanso ubupya.
Ba kateeka ba Joko Widodo baposele sana amano mukuwamya ifikuulwa ne misebo ifyaonaike sana mu Indonesia ngomusango wakongwelamo bakasala, elyo kabili baliposa sana indalama ishingi ku misebo naku nyanji.
Lelo nomba ukwakufumya indalama nakubula mu butungulushi bwaba Joko ilyo nomba cilepalamina mukusala nakabili uyu mwaka.
Ba Joko bali nobwafya bumbi ubwa mpasase sha mapepo ubulecitika mu Indonesia, umo bamembala ba ci Isilamu abengi nabengila mu mapepo ayakushintilila pali cila muntu ukubomba umulimo.
Abantu ukucila pali 1,000 ebafwile elyo bambi amakumi ya makana ebashele ukwabula apakwikala ilyo amabumba ya bena Kristu naba ci Isilamu balelwa mu misebo, ukubomfya amapanga, imifwi, amafumo, elyo nefyanso fimbi ifyayafya.
Tambeniko: Daniel Sturridge uwe bumba lyaba Liverpool aingisha akakato kakulinganya mukucimfyanya naba Chelsea
Daniel Sturridge ewapuswishe ba Liverpool ku kucimfiwa kwa Premier League kuli ba Chelsea ilyo aingishe akakato kamo pali mineti yalenga 89 pa Cibelushi mu cibansa ca Stamford Bridge mu London.
Sturridge apokelele umupila ukufuma kuli Xherdan Shaqiri ilyo pashelefye amayadi 30 ukufika mu cipanda caba Chelsea ninshi ibumba lyakwe nalishalilako na 1-0.
Abweseshe umupila kukuso ilyo talapantila mupepi napamulu wa cipanda.
Uyu mupila waliya apatali elyo waishiletelemuka ukuya lwapa cifutu cakukulyo ice sumbu.
Kulipelepele umupila waishilepita pamulu wakwa Kepa Arrizabalaga uwatolweke nokwingila mwisumbu.
"Walefwaishafye ukwingila muli ilya ncende, ukuba pa mupila elyo nabakateya pamo nga Shaq lyonse balalwisha ukuteya ukuya kuntanshi, kanshi naine nalelwisha ukuipangila inshita ukufika pantu ningapela," efyo Sturridge aebele ba LiverpoolFC.com.
"Namwene Kante aleisa nokwisakumyamo lelo nshaposeleko amano kuli wena naine nauminefye."
Ba Chelsea ebali pantanshi na 1-0 pa nshita ya kutusha panuma yakwingisha akakato kamo pali mineti yalenga 25 nowaingishe ni Eden Hazard uuteya muli ba Belgian.
Kengisha wa mupila uwaba Buluu aumine umupila ukupeela Mateo Kovacic muli kulya kuteya, ilyo talashingulukila pakati ka cibansa nokubutukisha ukuya kulubali lwacibansa ulwaba Liverpool.
Kovacic aliisa panta umupila wakupeela nokuya pakati ka cibansa.
Napanuma aishile uma umupila uwakupisha, nokutwala Hazard mu mushilwa wa cipanda.
Hazard alibutukisha ukusha abacingilila umupila bonse nokuya pwisha ilyashi pamulu wa cifutu ca cipanda nokuma kwaku kuso ukupita pali Alisson Becker uwaba Liverpool.
Ba Liverpool bakalashokana naba Napoli mukuteya kwamabumba ya Champions League ne nshita ya 3 p.m. pali Citatu mu cibansa ca San Paolo mu Naples, ku Italy.
Ba Chelsea nabo bakalashokana naba Videoton mu kuteya kwa UEFA Europa League ne nshita ya 3 p.m. pali Cine ku London.
Imfwa sha bantu ukufuma ku mabimbi yaku Indonesia shafika pali 832
Abantu abafwile ukufuma ku mabimbi ne cinkukuma ifyaku Indonesia nomba nabafika pali 832, efyalandile akabungwe akabombela ku masanso pa Sande ulucelo.
Cashimikwe ukuti abantu abengi balishikilishiwa mu fimabwe fya fikulwa ifyawile pa mulandu wa cinkukuma icafikile pa bukulu bwa 7.5 icacitike pali Cisano nokwimya amabimbi ayalepele ukufika pali 20 feet, efyo abalandilako aka kabungwe ba Sutopo Purwo Nugroho baebele abakolonganika ilyashi.
Umusumba wa Palu, uwakwata abantu ukufika kuli 380,000, waiswilemofye ifipimfya ifyaleputaulwa ku fikulwa ifyalebongoloka.
Bakapokola baikata umwaume, uwamyaka 32, uuletunganishiwa ukuti ewaipeye namayo uwalasawilwe imyele mpaka afwa.
Ukufwailisha ekulecitwa panuma umubili wakwa namayo wacisangwa mu Birkenhead, Merseyside lelo ulucelo.
Namayo uwamyaka 44 eusangilwe pa nshita ya 7.55am ne filonda fya myele pa Grayson Mews mu John Street, elyo no mwaume uwamyaka 32 ewiketwe mukukonkana neyi mfwa.
Bakapokola nabepusha abantu muli iyi ncende abamwene nangu ukumfwa ifilifyonse ukuti bese balondolole.
Ababombela ku Fyakufwailisha Imilandu ba Brian O'Hagan batile: 'Ukufwailisha elyo kutendekefye lelo ndelomba kuli abo bonse abasangwa mupepi na John Street mu Birkenhead abamwene nangu ukumfwako ifili fyonse ifyo baletunganya ukuti bengalanda naifwe.
Kuti natemwa nokulomba kubali bonse, makamaka bakensha bama taxi, abo limbi kuti bakopako fimo pama kamera yama motoka yabo ukuti bengalanda naifwe pantu kuti limbi nabakwatako ilyashi ilingafwilishako ukufwailisha kwesu.'
Abalandilako impuka yaba kapokola ebashininkishe ukuti namayo untu umubili wakwe usangilwe mwikashi wamu Birkenhead kabili umubili wakwe usangilwe mu cikuulwa.
Munshita ya cungulo kasuba ifibusa ifyaishibe uyu namayo fyaciya pa ncende ya busanso kukwipusha amepusho pamulandu ne ncende iyo uyu mubili wacisangwalo ulucelo.
Ukufwailisha kucili kulecitika ngefilandile ba kapokola ukuti balepekanya ukweba balupwa bakwa uyu namayo.
Kensha wa taxi uwikala mu Grayson Mews alefwaya ukwingila mu muputule wakwe lelo ba kapokola bamulesha pantu tapali uulesuminishiwa ukwingila nangu ukufuma muli ici cikulwa.
Camupesha sana amano pakumfwa ificitike.
Abekashi bakuli iyi ncende nomba baleebwa ukuti limbi kuti papita insa ishinono pakuti bengasuminishiwa ukubwelela mumayanda yabo.
Umubomfi waba kapokola ewo cumfwikilwe aleeba umuntu umo ukutila incende yonse iyi nomba iletunganishiwa nga incende ya misoka.
Namayo umo acimoneka pali iyi ncende ninshi alelila.
Alebwekeshapofye amashiwi ayakuti 'cabipa sana'.
Panshita ya 2pm Bakapokola babili baciba mukati ka cordon na motoka imbi panse.
Bakapokola bamo baciminina mu cordon nokuceceta amayanda ayatantama.

Icimumbwa capa Ng'anda ya Mafunde icaba Cromwell casanguka ecibukisho capali ino nshita ica 'kulembulula kwa lyashi lyakale'
Ukubindwa kwa ciko kuti kwaba ngo bupingushi bwa mumishikakulo pamulandu wa bonaushi bwakwe ubwapalana nobwa ba Taliban ubwa fintu ifingi ifya ntambi na mapepo ifyamu England ukwacitilwe nabantu bakwe aba Puritan.
Lelo incende ya Cromwell Society yalondolwele ukulanda kwaba Crick nga "ubuwelewele" kabili "nga ukufwaya ukulembuluka ilyashi lyakale."
Ba John Goldsmith, abakumupando mu Cromwell Society, batile: "Cali icabula ukutwishika mukulanshanya ukulipo pamulandu wakufumya ifimumbwa ukuti icimumbwa cakwa Oliver Cromwell panse ya Palace of Westminster kuti caba nicimo pafyalelolekeshiwapo.
Ukupekanya kwa nkondo shamu ncende sha Basungu takwatendeke nangu ukubomba na Cromwell.
Nakuba, limbi Cromwell kuti aculilamofye mu ficitwa fyakwa Thomas icikolwe cakwe mu myaka umwanda umo iyakunuma.
Ubulondoloshi ubwafikapo ubwakwa Cromwell ukulondolola ba Sir William Hamo Thorneycroft kushininkisha kwe langulushi lyamu sencari yalenga 19 elyo ne milembele yama lyashi yakale iya muntu uwingamoneka ukuti naclinga ukumusefya.
Ba Goldsmith baebele ipepala lye lyashi ilya Sunday Telegraph: "Cromwell amonwa nabantu abengi, makamaka mu kupwa kwa sencari yalenga 19 ukucila ilelo, nga kacingilila wa ng'anda ya mafunde ku mafya ayakufuma kunse, mukumona kwakwe icingaba buteeko bwa muntu umo.
Ngacakuti ici cintu capwililika mukwimininwa kwa ciko kuti lyaba ilyashi ilyakutwalilila ukulanshanyapo mu milumbe ya calo.
Icishinka icakwishiba cakutila impasase ishacitike pakati ka cencary yalenga 17 shalilenga ukuti ubuyantanshi ubwakonkapo bube fintu buli mu calo cesu, elyo Cromwell muntu umo uwaishibikwa uwimininako ulubali lumo ulwa uku kupatukana.
Imilimo yakwe iyabukacimyfa nga Kacingilila wa Mfumu nayo yalilinga ukusefiwa nokucindikwa."
Inkumba Iikali Yasumaula Shibulimi waku China mpaka Afwa
Shibulimi ewasanshilwe nokwipaiwa ne nkumba mu mushiika wa muncende iyabela lwaku kapinda kaku kuso aka calo ca China, ukulingana nefilandile imilabasa yakuli ilya ncende.
Uyu mwaume, uwishibikwefye neshina lyabubili ilya "Yuan," asangilwe ninshi nafwa ninshi no mushipa wakumutima nauputuka, ninshi alifye nomulopa mupepi ne cinka lya nkumba mu Liupanshui mu Guizhou province, efyalandile ipepala lya South China Morning Post pa bushiku bwapa Sande.
Shibulimi wa nkumba apekanya ukulasa inshindano ku nkumba shakwe pe cinka pa bushiku bwapa 30 Akapepo-Kanono, 2005 mu Xining iyamu Qinghai Province, ku China.
Ashimikwe ukutila aendele no mufyala wakwe ukufuma ku provinsi iyapalaminako iya Yunnan pa bushiku bwapali Citatu ukuyashitisha inkumba shakwe ishili 15 pa mushiika.
Ulucelo ulwakonkelepo, umufyala wakwe amusangile nafwa, nokusanga ukuti iciibi ce cinka ilyapalemeko nacisuka.
Alandile ukuti mwi cinka mwine umu mwali inkumba iikulu ninshi naikwata no mulopa kukanwa.
Ukupima kwa mubili kwasangile ukuti inkumba imo ine iyafinine 550 poundi eyasumawile nokwipaya uyu shibulimi, ukulingana ne nsebo ishapelwe.
"Amolu ya mufyala wandi yali nomulopa elyo ayafunaika, efyalandile umufyala wakwe uweshina lya "Wu," ukulingana nefyabelengelwe mu Lyashi lya Cungulo ilya mulabasa wa Guiyang.
Ifikope fyama kamera yakucecetelako fyalangile uko Yuan alaeingila mu mushiika panshita ya 4.40 am pali Cine ukuya mukuliisha inkumba shakwe.
Umubili wakwe waishilesangwa panuma ya nsa imo.
Inama iyaipeye uyu muntu tayali yakwa Yuan nangu umufyala wakwe.
Umukalamba uubombela pa mushiika aebele umulabasa we Lyashi lya Cungulo ukutila inkumba yalisalilwe pakuicincintila ukusansa umuntu uuli onse, panshita iyo bakapokola balefwailisha ifishinka fye lyashi.
Ulupwa lwakwa Yuan nabakalamba ba mushiika balelanshanya pamulandu wa cishinka mukofu pa mfwa yabo.
Nangu cakuti taficitika lyonse, imilandu ya nkumba ukusansa abantu shalicitikapo kunshiku shakunuma.
Mu mwaka wa 2016, inkumba yalisanshile umulume no mukashi wakwe pe bala lyabo mu Massachusetts, ukusha umwaume ne filonda ifibi sana.
Imyaka ikumi iyafumineko kunuma, inkumba iyafinine amapaundi 650 yatininkishe umulimi waku calo ca Wales kuli talakita yakwe mpaka umukashi wakwe atamfishe iyi nkumba nokupusha umulume.
Panuma shibulimi waku Oregon bamulile ku nkumba shakwe mu mwaka wa 2012, shibulimi umo uwaku Manitoba aebele ba CBC News ukutila inkumba tashaba no bwafya inshita ishingi, nomba ngashanunshafye ukuli umulopa kuti shaleta "ubwafya"
"Inkumba ilingi line shangalafye.
Shakwata amano ya bwaice, ukufwailisha.... tashakwata na lubuli.
Lelo ulingilefye ukushipela umucinshi uwalinga," efyo basosele.
Ifisheleko ku cimwela ca Huricane Rosa fileenekelwa ukuleta imfula iyacitalawe ku masamba ya calo ca US
Ukulingana nokuceceta kwa miceele, icimwela ca Hurricane Rosa cile cilecepako amaka ilyo cileselela ku cishi caku kapinda kaku kuso akaku Mexico.
Nangu cibefyo, icimwela ca Rosa cileleta imfula ya lyeshi ku northern Mexico elyo na southwest U.S. panshiku ishilekonkapo.
Icimwela ca Rosa cali ne cipupu ca mwela ukufika pali 85 mph, icamu Category 1 Hurricane, ilyo inshita yafikile pa 5 a.m. Eastern Time pa Sande, elyo caleendela apali imilundu 385 ku masamba ya Punta Eugenia, Mexico.
Icimwela ca Rosa cileeneklwa ukuselela ku kapinda kaku kuso pa bushiku bwapa Sande.
Pali ino nshita, amakumbi nayatendeka ukwengelela pamulu wa Pacific Ocean nokwenda ukuya ku kabanga mupepi ne Cishi caku Masamba ica calo ca U.S. Ilyo icimwela ca Rosa cilepalamina ku Baja California peninsula pabushiku bwa pali Cimo nge mfula iikalamba, cikatendeka ukusunkila umwela uwatikama ku kapinda kaku kuso ukutwala lwaku masamba ya calo ca U.S.
Icimwela ca Rosa cikaleta imfula iifikile pama inchi 10 mu ncende shimo ishaku Mexico pali Cimo.
Panuma, umwela uwamutonshi mukuuminkana na makumbi ayaleisa fikaleta imfula iingi mu ncende ya mupepi naku Masamba munshiku ishileisa.
Muli iyi ncende, imfula pakati kama inchi 1 na 4 ikaleta ukubunda, ifimabwe, elyo limbi nokutentemuka kwa mushili mu fiswebebe.
Umutonshi uwatikama uwakuli iyi ncende ukaleta imfula ukufika pama inchi 2 na 3, makamaka muncende shaku kapinda kakukulyo aka Nevada na Arizona.
Ukufikafye nakuma inchi 2 na 4 aya mfula eileenekelwa ukuloka mu ncende ishingi ishaku kapinda ka Kukuso, makamaka muncende iikulu iya Arizona.
Fimulamba fya lyeshi kuti fyabako ukukonkana nefyo imiceele ile ilelubana pamulandu wakusalangana kwa mfula iishikalika.
Kuti caba icalubana sana ukuya mu ciswebebe na makasa pamulandu wa kutiinya kwa iyi mfula.
Imfula iyamaka kuti yalenga utumilonga twamu mikonko namumpili ukuba mimana iikali nokupuupa kwa cimwela kukaleta icipuupu icikali nolukungu ulwingi.
Amakumbi ayalepalamina yakaleta imfula mu ncende shaku cishi ca Southern California.
Ukufula bwa mfula yonse pamo ukufika kuli citika wa inchi kuti kwacitika, ico icingalenga ukuleta kwafisoso elyo nokutelela kwa misebo.
Iyi kuti yaba nimfula yakubalilapo iya mainsa yabo.
Ukumiima kwa mfula iyasalangana kukatendeka ukuya ku Arizona mu cungulo capa Sande no lucelo lwa pali Cimo, ilyo imfula tailasalangana sana pali Cimo icungulo elyo napali Cibili.
Imfula iyamaka ikasalangana mu Fifutu Fine pali Cibili elyo nokuloka ukufika pali Citatu.
Mu mweshi wa Lusuba Lukalamba mulaba ukukaba mu calo ca U.S. ilyo incende ya Arctic yena ninshi iletalalisha, lelo incende sha tropic shena shibafye ishakabilila.
Inshita shimo ici cilalenga ukuti kube ukucinja kwa kukaba pantamfu iinonofye.
Kuliko icilangililo ca kupusana kwa kukaba ukupita mu ncende ya pakati iya calo ca U.S. pa Sande.
Palipo ukupusana kwa kukaba ukufika pama digili 20 pakati ka Musumba wa Kansas City, Missouri, na Omaha, Nebraska, elyo napakati ka St. Louis na Des Moines, Iowa.
Panshiku ishakonkapo, ukukabilila kwa lusuba kukatendeka ukupangika nokukulilako nakabili.
Incende iikulu iya pakati naku kabanga aka calo ca U.S. iileenekelwa ukutendeka ukukaba kwa mweshi wa Lusuba-lukalamba nokukaba ukufika pali 80 ukufuma ku Nika shaku Kapinda kaku Kulyo ukufika lwaku Kabanga.
Umusumba wa New York kuti wafika pama digili 80 pali Cibili ico icingacilako ama digili 10 pa kukaba ukwalyonse.
Ukuceceta kwa miceele ukwapa nshita iitali kulelanga ukuti kuti kwaba ukukaba ukucila pa cipimo ku kabanga ka calo ca U.S. muli citika wakubalilapo uwa mweshi wa Lusuba-lukalamba.
Abantu ukucila pali 20 milyoni ebatambileko ukulubulula kwa milandu yakwa Brett Kavanaugh
Abantu ukucila pali 20 milyoni ebatambile ubunte bwacishinka pa milabasa yacalo iili mutanda, mu milandu yapali Cine iyakwa Brett Kavanaugh uuli mukusalwa ku Supreme Court elyo na namayo uweshina lya Christine Blasey Ford, uwamulumbwile ukuti alefwaya ukumucenda ku maka ico icashimikwe ukuti cacitike mu myaka yamuma 1980.
Pali iyi nshita, ukwiminina kwe lyashi lya mashiwi ya mitekele nakukonkanyapo, ilyo imilabasa ilefulunganya amapulogilamu yabo pakuti bengasabankanya ili lyashi lya pali Cisano ilyakupumikisha: ukukonkana nokupekanya kwaba Arozona Sen. ba Jeff Flake ukwimininako ba FBI ukuti bengabika umulungu umo uwakufwailisha uyu mulandu.
Ba mayo ba Ford baebele Akabungwe ka Senate Judiciary Committee ukuti bali abashininkisha 100 pesenti ukutila ba Kavanaugh balibekete ku fyamfwalo ninshi nabakolwa nokwesha ukubafuula ifyakufwala ilyo kwali ukusefya kwa malila pa sukulu.
Ba Kavanaugh, muli bunte bwabo ubwacishinka nabo batile bali abashininkisha 100 pesenti ukutila ico tacacitike.
Ukulingana nefyo cilemoneka cipalile ukuti abantu ukucila pali 20.4 milyoni ebatambile uku kulubulula pali Cisano ukulingana ne nsebo ishapeelwe naba Nilesen
Aka kampani kalependa abaletamba iyi milandu pa milabasa ya CBS, ABC, NBC, CNN, Fox News Channel elyo na MSNBC.
Ifipendo fyabatambileko tafyaishibikwe bwangu ukufuma ku milabasa imbi iyatambishe, ukubikapo na PBS, C-SPAN elyo na Fox Business Network.
Elyo inshita shimo akampani ka Nielsen kalakwatako ubwafya pakupenda bwino abantu abatambila mu ma ofeshi yabo.
Ukucibika mucingomfwika bwino, iyi mpendwa kuti yapashanishiwa ku bantu abaletamba umupila mu cibansa nangu abalesangwa pa kulongana kwa Filambu fya Masambililo.
Umulabasa wa Fox News Channel, uyo amalangushi yauko yalitungilila sana ukusontwa kwakwa Kavanaugh, ewacilike ku bwingi bwa bantu ukufika ku cipendo ca 5.69 milyoni mu nshita yakulubulula konse, efyasosele ba Nielsen.
Umulabasa wa ABC ewali uwacibili uwakwete abaletamba abali 3.26 milyoni.
Umulabasa wa CBS wakwete 3.1 milyoni, NBC yakwete 2.94 milyoni, MSNBC yakwete 2.89 milyoni elyo CNN yakwete 2.52 milyoni, efyo ba Nielsen balandile.
Ukukonka kwelyashi kwashelefye pamulu napanuma ya kulubulula.
Ba Flake ebalekonkwa sana mu lyashi lyacitike pali Cisano.
Panuma umukalamba uwamu ofeshi lyama Republican alandile amashiwi ukuti akavota mukutungilila Kavanaugh, alikopelwe nama kamera yaba CNN naba CBS pali Cisano ulucelo ninshi balemupundilila ku bantu abafulilwe nganshi ilyo alenina icikwepe ukuya ku kulubulula kwa Judiciary Committee.
Aiminine namenso panshi ayansoni ilyo balemushoba ifyo ifyalangilwe pa mulabasa wa CNN.
"Ninjiminina pano pantanshi yobe,” efyalandile namayo umo.
"Bushe uletontonkanya ukuti alelanda icishinka ku calo?
Bamwebele ukuti, "uli namaka ilyo banamayo abengi bali ukwabula amaka.""
Ba Flake batile iofeshi lyabo nalilandapo kale pali uyu mulandu, ilyo icikwepe tacilaisalika, ukuti balekwata ifingi ifyakulanda ku kabungwe panuma ya kulubulula.
Imilabasa ya nsale neya pamwela yonse yaletambisha fyonse ifyalecitika ukufikafye naku nsa nashimbi ishakonkelepo, ilyo akabungwe ka Judiciary Committee kalingile ukuvota ukutwala ukusalwa kwaba Kavanaugh ku kuvota ukukulu ukwaba Senate.
Lelo ba Flake batile alecitafye ifyo mukumfwikisha kwakuti ba FBI bali nokulolesha mu mitunganya yakwa uyu kasalwa wa uyu mulungu uwakonkapo icintu ico impendwa iinono iyama Democrat balekaana.
Ba Flake bali abashininkisha lubalifye ukupitila mukulanshanya kwabo nabanabo, ba Senator bama Democrat ba Chris Coons.
Panuma yakulanshanya naba Coons elyo nama senators bambi, ba Flake balipanga ubusalo.
Ubusalo bwaba Flake nabukwata amaka pantu cilepilibula ukuti ama Republicans tekuti bakwate amavoti ayakusuminisha ba Kavanaugh ukwabula ukubafwailisha.
Ba kateeka ba Trump nabesula ukufwailisha kwa FBI mu milandu yonse iitunganishiwemo ba Kavanaugh.
Prime Minister waku Britain May atunganya abasusha imilimo yakwe ukuti 'baleingishamo ifikansa fya mitekele' mulyashi lya Brexit
Ba Prime Minister ba Theresa May ebatungenye abasusha amanshiko yabo ayakufuma mu European Union ukuti "baleingishamo ifikansa fya mitekele" mu buyo bwa calo ca Britain nokonaula ubukabilo bwa calo neci cali nimukulanshanya ne pepala lyelyashi ilya Sunday Times.
Ba Prime Minister baku Britain ba Theresa May ebaleya ku kulongana kwa Conservative Party Conference mu Birmingham, Britain, pa 29 Sepitemba, 2018.
Mukulanshanya kumbi ukupalamine nokulanshanya pe buula lyakubalilapo ilye pepala lye lyashi, uwali kale Foreigh Minister Boris Johnson eubikilepo ukusansa kwa lyashi lyakwa May ilileitwa ubwanshiko bwa Chequers ubwa Brexit, nokutila ilangulushi lyakuti ba Britain naba EU balingile ukulapoka imisonko yacilaumo "talilolemo nakalya."
Ukulasa kwakwa Wayde Sims: Bakapokola nabekata Dyteon Simpson uuletunganishiwa mukukonkana nemfwa yakwa kateya wamu LSU
Bakapokola nabekatako uuletunganishiwa mukulasaula nokwipaya kwakwa Wayde Sims, uuli ne myaka 20 kabili kateya wa basketball mwibumba lya LSU.
Dyteon Simpson, uuli ne myaka 20, ewiketwe nokusungilwa muli bu citente pamulandu wakwipaya ukwacipimo ca bubili, efilandile impuka ya bakapokola iyaku Baton Rouge Police Department
Abakalamba ba bakapokola balilangisha vidyo iyo Sims na Simpson balelwa, elyo kabili batile Sims alilufya amagilasi yakwe ilyo balelwa.
Bakapokola baishiletola amagilasi pancende yalubuli elyo batile umulopa wa DNA yakwa Simpson walisangwa kuli aya magilasi, efilandile ba WAFB ababombelako ba CBS.
Panuma yakwipusha Simpson, bakopokola batile alisumina ukuti ewalasawile Sims icabipisha.
Ukufuma kwakwe ukwa bondi kubikilwe pali $350,000, efilandile ba Advocate.
Iofeshi lyaba Coroner baku East Baton Rouge Parish ebafumishe insebo shakubalilapo pali Cisano, ukutila intuntuko ya iyi mfwa cilonda ca lupolopolo lwa mfuti ukufuma ku mutwe ukwingila mu mukoshi.
Iciputulwa ca bakapokola ciletasha sana ba Louisiana State Police fugitive task force, ba state police crime lab, ba Southern University police elyo nabekashi bakuli iyi ncende pakwafwilshako mukwikata kwa uyu muntu.
Abatungulula ibumba lya LSU ba Joe Alleva balitasha sana iciputulwa cisopa amafunde kuli iyi ncende "pakubombesha kwabo nokufwaya umulinganya."
Sims akwetefye imyaka 20.
Umulumendo uwali no mushinku wa 6-foot-6 kuntanshi akulile mu Baton Rouge, umo bawishi ba Wayne, nabo baleteya basketball mwibumba lya LSU.
Uyu mulumendo alingishe utukato 5.6 elyo natumbi utwakupususha kwa mupila utuli 2.6 mukuteya kwanshita yapwile.
Pali Cisano ulucelo, kakansha we bumba lya LSU uweshina lya Will Wade atile ibumba lili “nobulanda nganshi” kabili "nalipeshiwa amano" pamfwa yakwa Wayde.
Ba Wade batile "Ifi efyo musakamanapofye lyonse."
Ci Volcano casalanginishisha imito mu Musumba wa Mexico
Imito ukufuma kuli volcano yaku Popocatepetl eifikile ku ncende shaku kapinda kaku kulyo aka musumba ukalmba uwa mexico.
Iciputulwa ca National Center for Disaster Prevention ecasokele abekashi bamu Mexico warned Mexicans pa Cibelushi ukutila batalukeko kuli ci volcano ilyo bamwene ukuti ifilecitika mukati ka cibwendo fyalundwako amaka yakufumya kwa mwela ne mito yafika pali 183 munsa 24.
Ici ciputulwa calececeta ubwingi bwa fibulukutu elyo nefinkukuma.
Ifikope fimo ifyapa fitunshitunshi fyalangile uko amamotoka yali ne mito pa magilasi mu ncende shimo ishamu Mexico pamo ngamu Xochimilco.
Abalolesha pafyo icalo caikala batile kuli ukulundako kwa filecitika muli volcano iyo iyaba apalepele 45 miles (72 kilometers) lwakukabanga ka musumba ukalamba ukufuma apo icinkukuma icikwete amaka 7.1 casunkenye pakati ka usumba wa Mexico mu Sepitemba, 2017 .
Ci volcano icaishibikwa nga "Don Goyo" catendeke ukumoneka mu mwaka wa 1994.
Bakapokola balwishanya nabacisanguka ama Catalan ilyo kwashalafye panono ukuya mukusefya ukwibukisha kwa kuvota kwa buntungwa
Abantu mutanda ebaiketwe mu Barcelona pa Cibelushi panuma abaletungilila ukusefya kwa buntungwa balwishenye na bakapokola, elyo nabengi baibimbile mukulwishanya kwa bacisanguka pakutendeka kwa kusefya kwe voti lya kupatukana kwa fipani mu Catalonia.
Ibumba lya bacisanguka nefifimbo pa menso abacingilishiwe na bakapokola balebatoba amani elyo na penti ya bunga, ukupanga amakumbi ya lukungu mu misebo umo umulingile ukusangwa abatandashi bakutamba icalo.
Ulubuli lwalibuka inshita shimo mu kasuba elyo bakapokola balebomfya inkonto shabo ukukabulwilako ulu lubuli.
Mu nsa ishakonkelepo abaletungilila ubuntungwa balepunda amashiwi yakuti "Takuli ukulaba, takuli ukwelela” lubali lumbi ama Unionist nabo ninshi balepunda baleti "Utwalilile we calo ca Spain."
Abantu 14 ebaileundapwa ku filonda ifinono ifyo bacenenwe muli ishi mpasase, efyalandile umulabasa wakuli ilya ncende.
Incende ilifye iyakutinya muncende umwaba abalwisha ubuntungwa umwaka umo panuma ya kusala kwa referendum yapa 1 Ulusuba-lukalamba ukwamoneke nga ukupula kwe funde ku musumba wa Madrid lelo ukwalesefiwa nabacisanguka abena Catalan.
Bakasala abengi balivotele ukuti bakwate ubuntungwa, nangu cakuti abalekana ukupatukana balicepesha nganshi abakene ukuya votako.
Ukulingana nabakalamba ba ncende ya Catalan abantu ukufika kuli 1000 ebacenawilwe uyu mwaka panuma bakapokola balefwaya ukulesha ukusala ukukonkanyapo pancende shakusalilapo muncende yonse umwali impasase ishingi.
Amabumba ayatungilila ubuntungwa yalipangile inkambi panse pa bushiku bwapali Cisano pakulesha ukuilishanya mukutungilila bakapokola ba calo.
Ukuilishanya kwa bantu kwalikonkenyepo lelo kwalipatikishiwa ukukonka inshila imbi.
Ba Narcis Termes, abali ne myaka 68, bakalungisha ba malaiti abasangilwe ku kuilishanya kwabalefwaya ubuntungwa pamo na bakashi babo batile tabakwete isubilo nakabili ilyakutila incende ya Catalonia ikakwata ubuntungwa.
"Umwaka wafumineko twaikele mu nshita yesu iyamutende nganshi.
Namwene uko abafyashi bandi balilile ifilamba fya nsansa pakukwata ishuko lyakuisalila nomba ino nshita natutitkishiwa," efyo balandile.
Nangu cakuti kwali ukucimfya kwakushala kwempe mukusala kwa mweshi wa Disemba, Abena Catalan abafwaya ubuntungwa balelwisha sana ukuti bengaba mumaka muli uno mwaka ilyo intungulushi shabo ishamaka shimo shicili ku fyalo fyakufisamako elyo shimbi shicili mu fifungo ukulolela ukukandwa pafyo shacitile mukupekanya ukusala kwa referendum elyo nokulanda kwa buntungwa ukwakukonkapo.
Ba Joan Puig, abali ne myaka 42 bakalungisha bama motoka abalekopa ukuilishanya mukutunglila bakapokola pali foni yabo batile ishi mpasase shiletungililwa naba politishani kumbali shonse shibili.
"Ilyashi lile lilekoselakofye," efyo balandile.
Pa Cibelushi, Oriol Junqueras, umo pa ntungulushi 9 ishama Catalan uwalipo mu cifungo ukwabula ukulubulula umwaka wapwile abilishe ukuti ali nokwimininako mukusala kwa Ng’anda ya Mafunde ku Europe uyu mwaka uleisa.
"Ukwimininako mu kusala kwaku Europe emusango uusuma sana uwakukaninamo ukubwelela kufyakunuma mu fikomo fya maisosele no mutitikisha uwamoneka mu buteeko bwa calo ca Spain," efyo balandile.

Ibumba lyaba Livingston ilisumbwilwe elyaponeshe pamusawo Steven Gerrard katungulula we bumba lyaba Rangers mukucimfiwa kwa miku ibili mu kuteya kwa mangalo 18 nga katungulula we bumba lyaku Ibrox.
Akakato kakwa Dolly Menga ekapangile ubupusano ilyo ulubali lwakwa Gary Holt lwaendele capamo nabena Hibernia mu cipande ca bubili.

Ilyo tacilafika pali iyo nshita, ba Rangers bakapokelela ba Rapid Vienna mu Europa League pali Cine.
ibumba lya Livingston, pali ino nshita, lilekonkanyapo nokucimfya kwabo muli ici ciputulwa na mangalo 6, mukutungululwa na kakansha mukalamba uweshina lya Holt uushilacimfiwapo apo apyanine pali Kenny Miler umweshi wapwile.
Ibumba lya Livingston elilepanya amashuko yakucimfya ilyo balepokelela amabumba ayakosa
Ibumba lyakwa Holt lyalingile ukuba pantanshi sana nalintufye tabalaingisha nangu kamo, nomupampamina wabo icingalenga naba Rangers ukukwata amafya ayengi.
Scott Robinson allisapita pakati lelo aliisa wayawaya ilyo asendele umupila, elyo Alan Lithgow aishileingishamo amaka yakwe panuma yakushelela nokukumanya umutwe wakwa Craig Halkett untu aumine ukucilinganya icipanda.
Abene ba cibansa baliicetekela sana pakuleka ba Ranger ukuteya pantanshi yabo, mukucetekela ukuti baleisacimfya abeni panshita ishalingwa.
Nimuli uyu wine musango emo akakato ka bwafya kabasangile.
Ba Rangers baishilepanga fuli kiki elyo ba Livingston babombele pa kwisula inshila, Declan Gallagher na Robinson babombele pamo mukupekanya bwino Menga, uwaikete umupila nokuma ukufuma pakati ka kabokoshi ka cipanda.
Pali iyi nshita, ba Rangers ebasendele umupila lelo basangile abakunuma nabakosa elyo na kasunga wa cipanda nao Liam Kelly ali uwaipekanya bwino,
Ukuteya kwa uyu musango kwalikonkanyapo namu cipande cabubili, nangu cakuti Alfredo Morelos alipatikisha ukupususha kwa mupila ukufuma kuli Kelly.
Scott Pittman alikanishiwa ukuteya kwakwa kasunga wacipanda uwaba Rangers Allan McGregor na Lithgow aliisa pantisha umupila ukufuma ku mupila umbi uwapangilwe naba Livingston.
Ukupanta kwa mupila kwalikonkenyepo ukuya mu ncende yaba Livingston lelo yonse yalebwekeshiwamo, elyo amapenoti yabili - panuma ukulwisha kwakwa Halkett pali kateya uwapyanikishiwemo Glenn Middleton, elyo nokwikata kumo - fyalikanishiwe.

Alasdair Lamont uwaku BBC Scotland pa ncende ya Tony Macaroni Arena

Ku muntu uuli onse, baliteyele bwino, ukukonkanyapo ukucila napafyaleenekelwa muli uku kusumbulwa kwakuya pamulu.
Umusango wabo uwamiteyele tawacinja panuma yakubwelela pamulu, lelo ukutasha kuleya kuli Holt mumusango untu akanshishemo ibumba ukufuma apo aishile muli ili bumba.

Ba Erdogan bapokelelwa mukutwishikwa mu Cologne
Kwali ukumwentula ne nsansa pa Cibelushi (29 Sepitemba) ilyo intungulushi sha calo ca Turkey na Germany shakumene ku cakulya ca lucelo mu Berlin.
Bwali bushiku bwakushalikisha mu butandashi ubwayafya ubwakwa Kateeka Erdogan ubwaku Germany - ubwiminine pakuwamya ubwampano pakati ka bamembala ba NATO.
Balifumamo pamulandu wa milandu imo ukubikapo na insambu sha buntunse, ubuntungwa bwamaisosele elyo nokukwata amaka ukwa calo ca Turkey ayakuba mu EU.
Napanuma ba Erdogan baile ku Cologne mukwisula icilonganino icikalamba ica mosque.
Uyu emusumba uwakwatisha abena Turkey abengi abekala kunse ya calo ca Turkey.
Bakapokola batile pamulandu wa bucingo balelesha cinkupiti wa bantu ukufika kuli 25,000 ukukolongana pantanshi ya ci mosque lelo abengi abaletungilila kateeka balimine akatalamukila ukuti bamone kateeka wabo.
Abantu abengi abashifwaya Erdogan - mbamo abali ma Kurdish - nabo balisosapo, ukususha amafunde yakwa Erdogan's elyo nobusalo bwa buteeko bwa German ukumupokelela mu calo cabo.
Uku kuilishanya kwa bantu kwalipanga akapatulula pakupokelela umweni untu ama Turkish baku German batasha elyo bambi nabo balimusula nga kateeka umunkalwe.
Ubusanso bwamu musebo wa Deptford: Kensha wa nchinga afwa panuma yakupunkana na motoka
Kensha wa nchinga eufwile panuma yakupunkana na motoka mu London.
Ubu busanso bwacitikile mupepi namakumanino ya musebo wa Bestwood Street na Evelyn Street, umusebo uwakalabana sana mu Deptford, lwaku kabanga ka musumba, pa nshita ya 10:15 BST.
Kensha wa motoka aliiminina elyo na bashing’anga baliisa nokwesha ukutangata, lelo uyu muntu afwilile fye palya pene.
Ubu busanso bwacitike panumafye ya myeshi inono apo kensha wa nchinga naumbi afwilile mukupunka-nokubutuka mu Childers Street, apo apalifye umulundu umo ukufuma apacitikile ubusanso bwapa Cibelushi.

Icifungo ca Long Lartin: Abashilika mutanda bacenaulwa mu cimfulunganya
Abashilika baku cifungo ebaceneke mucimfulunganya capa cifungo icikulu icabaume, efilandile Iofeshi lya Cifungo.
Icimfulunganya catendeke pa HMP Long Lartin mu Worcestershire panshita ya 09:30 BST pa Sande elyo kabili cicili cilekonkanyapo.
Abashilika incenshi abaku "Tornado" nabetwa ukuti bese babombele pali ici cimfulunganya, icibimbilemo abafungwa abali 8, elyo cilifye kulubali lumo ulwa cifungo.
Abashilika balitangatwa ku filonda fyakumenso ifinono palya pene pa cifungo.
Efyalandile uulandilako Impuka ya Bashilika ba Cifungo: "Abashilika abakanshiwa bwino ebatuminwe ukuti bese bamone ifilecitika pa HMP Long Lartin.
Abashilika mutanda ebatangetwe ku filonda.
Tatusuminisha ifimfulunganya mu fifungo fyesu, kabili abo abalesangwa muli iyi milandu yakupula ili funde bakatwalwa ku kapokola elyo kuti balundilwako imyaka naimbi iyakwikala mu cifungo.
Icifungo ca HMP Long Lartin cilasunga abafungwa ukucila pali 500, ukubikapo nabantalamisoka ababipisha muli ici calo.
Mu mweshi wa Kapepo-kakalamba cashimikwe ukutila umukalamba wa ici cifungo alileundapwa mu cipatala panuma yakusanswa no mufungwa.
kabili mu mweshi wa Lusuba-lukalamba uyu mwaka abashilika ababombela mukupwisha impasase balitilwe mukukankabula impasase ishabipa umo ababomfi basanshilwe nokubatoba ama bola ya bwangalo bwa pool.
Icimwela ca Rosa Catinya Umusumba wa Phoenix, Las Vegas, Salt Lake na Menshi ya Lyeshi (Incende sha Cilala shena Kuti Shanonkelamo)
Tacicitika sana icakuti imfula ya miceele yaku tropic kuti yafika ku Arizona, lelo ico cine ecingacitika mumulungu uleisa ilyo amaka ayasheleko aya Cimwela ca Rosa yele yalepita mu Desert Southwest, umo ciletwala mulamba wakubunsha.
Iciputulwa icibombela ku kwishiba kwa miceele ica National Weather Service calipeela ubusoko pamulandu wa mulamba pali Cimo napali Cibili ku ncende ya masamba ya Arizona ukuya ku kapinda kakulyo naku kabanga ka Nevada, lwakukabanga ka California na Utah, ukubikapo ne misumba ya Phoenix, Flagstaff, Las Vegas, na Salt Lake City.
Icimwela ca Rosa ecileenekelwa ukupita mu Phoenix pali Cibili, ukufika pa bushiku bwa pali Cimo ne mfula.
Iciputulwa ca National Weather Service mu Phoenix ecalandile ukubomfya icitunshitunshi ca Twitter ukutila “imyela ya kangungwe iili 10 iyaku tropic eyakwata amaka ya cipuupu pa ntamfu ya milundu 200 iyamu Phoenix ukutendeka mu 1950!
Icimwela ca Katrina (1967) cali cimwela icali mukati ka ntamfu ya milundu 40 iya mupaka wa AZ."
Ifilengo fyakushalikisha ifya ciputulwa ca National Hurricane Center filesobela imfula ukufika kuma inchi 2 na 4, elyo namuncende shimo ukufika pama inchi 6 mu Mogollon Rim iyamu Arizona.
Incende shimbi isha Desert Southwest ukubikapo ne ncende ya pakati ka Rockies na Great Basin shileenekelwa ukukwata imfula ama inchi 1 na 2, ne ncende shimo ishingakwata ukufika kuma inchi 4.
Kuli abo abali kunse yabusanso bwa lyeshi, imfula ya Rosa kuti yaba lipaalo pamulandu wakuti iyi ncende yalikwata sana ifilala.
Nangu cakuti ukubunda lisakamiko ilibi nganshi, imfula imo pali iyi ikaba lishuko mu ncende shimo pantu ku ncende iyabela lwa pakati ka masamba na kapinda kukulyo (Southwest) pali ino nshita ili ne cilalala.
Ukulingana naba U.S. Drought Monitor, ukucilako pali 40 pesenti ya ncende ya Arizona eikwete icilala icabipisha, icabubili mumsango uwabipisha," efilandile ba weather.com.
Icakubalilapo, inshila iilepitamo Hurricane Rosa ileya ku mutentemuko wa Baja California peninsula mu Mexico.
Icimwela ca Rosa, icicili na maka ya cipuupu pa bushiku bwapa Sande ulucelo na maka yamwela ukufika pa milundu 85 pa nsa imo, cilepitila apali imilundu 385 ku kapinda kakukulyo akaku Punta Eugenia, Mexico nokuya ku kapinda kaku kuso pa milundu 12 pa nsa imo.
Iyi mfula ilekumana na menshi ayatalala ayamu Pacific icilengele nokuti ilebwelelako panshi.
Kanshi, ileenekelwa ukuloka sana mu Mexico namaka yamfula ya tropic munshita ya cungulo-kasuba nangu mucungulo-bushiku pali Cimo.
Imfula muncende shimo ishamu Mexico kuti yakula sana, icingaleta nesakamiko lya kubunda.
"Ukufula kwa mfula yonse ukufika kuma inchi 3 na 6 eileenekelwa ukufuma ku Baja California ukuya lwaku kabanga ka Sonora, ukufika nakuma inchi 10 inshita shimo," efilandile ba weather.com.
Icimwela ca Rosa panuma cikaya ku kapinda kaku kusu ukupita mu Mexico nge cimwela ca tropic ilyo tailafika ku mupaka waku Arizona mu lucelo lwa pali Cibili ngo mwela wamu tropic, uukapita mu Arizona nokwingila mu southern Utah pali Cibili ubushiku.
"Ubusanso ubukalamba ubuleenekelwa ku Cimwela ca Rosa nangu ifileshalako ku maka ya ciko ni mfula iikulu sana mu Baja California, ku northwestern Sonora, elyo naku U.S. Desert Southwest," efyo ba National Hurricane Center balandile.
Iyi mfula ileenekelwa ukuleta fimulamba ifyabipa sana nefisoso mu ciswebebe, elyo nokubunduka kwa mushili muncende shampili.

Umusepela uwamyaka 17, bambi babili abamyaka 18 elyo naumbi umukalamba uwamyaka 20- ebaiketwe ubushiku mu ncende ya Radstock, efilandile Bakapokola baku Avon naku Somerset.

Ba Trump batile ba Kavanaugh ‘balicula, kukusushiwa, nokufulwa' kwa cipani ca Democratic Party
"Ukuvotela ba Kavanaugh kuli kuvota kwa kukana kwa bunkalwe ne mingalato iyalubana iyaba Democratic Party," Ba Trump balandile aya mashiwi pa kulongana ukwali mu Wheeling, West Virginia.
Ba Trump balandile ukuti ba Kavanaugh "balicula, kukusushiwa, nokufulwa” kwa cipani ca Democratic Party panshita yonse iya mulimo wa kusalwa kwabo.
Ba Kavanaugh bapele ubunte ku kabungwe ka Congress pali Cine, mukupatikisha namubulanda ukukana umutunganya wakwa Christine Blasey Ford ukuti bafwaile ukumucenda ku maka ilyo bali abaice.
Ford nawo alipela ubunte pali uku kulubulula pamulandu nefyo alesosa.
Ba Kateeka balandile pa Cibelushi ukutila "Abena America bamwene amaka, amano, nokushipa" kwakwa Kavanaugh pali bulya bushiku.
"Ivoti lyakushininkisha ba Judge Kavanaugh livoti ilyakushininkisha kwa muntu uwamano uwa nshita yesu, kapingula uwaishibikwa ukubombela abekala calo ifintu ifisuma," ifi efyo baebele ibumba lya batungilila ku West Virginia.
Ba Kateeka balandile pa kusalwa kwaba Kavanaugh ilyo balelanda pafyo aba cipani caba Republican abafulile mukusala kwapakati ka temu.
"Ilyo kwashalafye imilungu 5 ukufika kukusala ukukankala nganshi mu nshita yesu.
Nshileimininako mukusala, lelo mucishinkafye ndeimininako," efyo balandile.
"Ecilengele ukuti ndesangwa muncende ishingi pakutungilila abaleimininako abamaka."
Ba Trump balandile ukuti ama Democrats bali pa mulimo uwabipa "uwakukanya no kucilinganya."
Ukusala kwakubalilapo ukukankala ukwaba Senate pa kusalwa kwaba Kavanaugh kuleenekelwa ukucitika ilyo tacilafika pali Cisano,efyo intungulushi nkalamba iyafwilisha ba GOP yaebele ba CNN.
Imyanda ya bantu ebepaiwe na cinkukuma, amabimbi yaku Indonesia, elyo abalefwa bele balefulilakofye.
Abantu ukufika kuli 384 ebafwile, bambi balisendwa ilyo amabimbi yaleisa ku mulundu, ilyo icinkukuma icikalamba na mabimbi fyaumine icilila ca Sulawesi mu Indonesian, efyo abakalamba balandile pa Chibelushi.
Imyanda ya bantu eyakolongene mukusefya pa mucanga wa mumbali ya bemba mu musumba wa Palu pali Cisano ilyo amabimbi ayalepele amamita 6 (18 feet) yaishile nokuma kumulundu panshita ya cungulo-bushiku nokusenda abantu abengi kumfwa shabo nokonaula fyonse ifyasangilwe munshila.
Aya mabimbi yakonkele pa cinkukuma icakulile ukufika pali 7.5.
"Ilyo ubusoko bwa mabimbi bwaumfwikike mailo, abantu balecita imilimo yabo mumbali ya bemba elyo kabili tababutwike ilyo line kabili balisanswa," Ba Sutopo Purwo Nugroho, abalandilako akabungwe akalolesha ku masanso aka BNPB mu Indonesia ebalandile aya mashiwi kuli bashimilabasa mu Jakarta.
"Amabimbi ya tsunami tayaishile yeka iyo, yalisenda amamotoka, imilando, amayanda, elyo nokuma icili conse icasangilwe pa mushili," efyalandile ba Nugroho, ukulundapo ukutila aya mabimbi yaleenda pali bemba pakubutuka ukufika pali 800 kph (497 mph) ilyo tayalafika kumulundu.
Abantu bamo balinina ku fimiti ukuti babutuke kuli aya mabimbi elyo kabili balipusuka, efyo balandile.
Abantu ukufika kuli 16,700 ebaseshiwe nokutwalwa ku ncende 24 ishakupusukilako mu Palu.
Ifikope fyakukopela mumulu ifyafumishiwe ne ciputulwa icilolesha pa masanso fyalangile ukutila ifikulwa ifingi nama shopu fyalitobaika, amalalo yalinyongana nokubongoloka elyo necilonganino ca mosque ninshi nacishingulukwa na menshi.
Utunkukuma utunono etwakonkenyepo ukupita mumusumba wa mumbali ya bemba pa Chibelushi.
Ukukonkana kwa finkukuma ekwaumfwikike mu ncende umwikala abantu ukufika kuli 2.4 milyioni.
Iciputulwa ca Agency for the Assessment and Application of Technology (BPPT) mu Indonesia calandile mu mashiwi yabo ukutila amaka ayasendelwe ne cinkukuma capali Cisano yalifika pa miku 200 ukucila pe bomba lya atomic ilyaponene pa ncende ya Hiroshima mu nshita ya World War Two.
Kabili batile, imipangilwe ya uyu musumba, uwaikala pampela ya cilila eyalengele ukuti aya mabimbi yakule.
Ba Nugroho balondolwele ubonaushi ukuti “bukulu” nokutila amakana ya mayanda, ifipatala, amatuuka na mahotela fyalitobaika.
ifitumbi fyabantu abafwile fyasangilwe nafifyantama mufimabwe fyafikulwa ifyawile, kabili batile abantu bambi 540 ebacenaike elyo bambi 29 tabalamoneka.
Ba Nugroho batile impendwa ya basanshilwe elyo nobonaushi kuti fyakulisha mumbali ya bemba apali intamfu ya 300 km (190 miles) ku kapinda kaku kuso aka Palu, mu ncende iitwa Donggala, iyapalamina ku ntuntuko ya cinkukuma.
Ukulanshanya “kwalifulunganafye konse ukwabula nokukwatako ilyashi ilili lyonse” ukufuma ku Donggala, efyasosele ba Nugroho.
Mwaba abantu ukucila pali 300,000 abekala muli ilya ncende," efyalandile ba Red Cross mu mashiwi yabo, ukulundapo nokutila ababomfi babo pamo nabaipeleshe bali mukuya kuncende sha busanso.
"Ubu busanso ubwabipa, elyo kabili kuti bwabipilako, efyo balandile.
Aka kabungwe kalisushiwa nganshi pa Cibelushi pakukanaishibisha abantu ukuti tsunami nayuma incende ya Palu, nangu cakuti abakalamba batile amabimbi yaishile panshita ninshi ubusoko nabupeelwa kale.
Muli vidyo imo iyatuminwe pa sosho midya mwali umuntu uwalepunda ukufuma pa cikulwa cantunti ukusoka abantu abali mumusebo pesamba pa mulandu na mabimbi ya tsunami ayaleisa.
Mu mamineti fye ayanono icibumba ca menshi caisa ku mulundu nokusenda ifikuulwa pamo na mamotoka.
Umulabasa wa Reuters walifilwa ukushininkisha bwino iyi vidyo pali iyo nshita.
Icinkukuma na mabimbi fyalilenga ukuti amalaiti yashime nokonaula inshila shakulanshanya ukushinguluka umusumba wa Palu ico icalengele nokuti abakalamba bancende bafilwe ukukondenkanya imisango yakupusushishamo abantu.
Abashilika nabatendeka ukutuma indeke sha fipe no bwafwilisho ukufuma ku Jakarta ne misumba imbi, efyo abakalamba balandile, lelo abantu abalefumishiwa mu busanso bena bacili balekabila ifyakulya nefyakubomfya fimbi ifikankala.
Icibansa ca ndeke ica uyu musumba nacisulwa pamulandufye wakupeela ubwafwilisho elyo cikabafye icaisalika mpaka mu mweshi wa Okutoba.
Ba Kateeka ba Joko Widodo balingile ukutandalila incende umulesungilwa abapuswike mu Palu pa Sande.
Imfwa sha Bantu muli Tsunami yaku Indonesia Shacila pali 800.
Nacibipisha Sana.
Nangu cakuti ababomfi ba World Vision ukufuma ku Donggala nabendafye bwino ukufika ku musumba wa Palu, uko ababomfi bekele mu nsakwe sha tarpaulin ishipangilwe mu lubansa lwe ofeshi lyabo, pakuya bacipita muncende umuli ubonaushi ubwacipesha mano, efilandile ba Doseba.
"Bacinjeba ukuti bacimona amayanda ayengi ayaonaika,” efyo basosele.
Nacibipa sana.
Nangu cakuti amabumba ya bwafwilisho yalemoneka ukutendeka ukupekanya ubwafwilisho bwa masanso, bamo baleilishanya ukuti ababomfi babwafwilisho abakwete ubwishibilo ubukulu ukufuma kunse ya calo baleleshiwa ukuya ku Palu.
Ukulingana na mafunde ya calo ca Indonesia, indalama, ifipe nababomfi ukufuma kunse ya calo kuti batendekafye ukuya kuli iyi ncende ilyofye yalandwa ukuti nincende ya busanso bwa calo (national disaster zone).
Ici cintu tacilati cicitike.
"Ubu bucilifye busanso bwa provinsi," efyalandile ba Aulia Arriani, abalandilako akabungwe ka Red Cross mu Indonesia.
"Ilyofye ubuteeko bwatila, "CISUMA, ubu busanso bwa calo conse," kuti twaisula ubwafwilisho ukufuma ku fyalo fimbi lelo ico tacilati cibe ifyo."
Ilyo bwailile ubwalenga cibili pa musumba wa Palu panuma ya cinkukuma na tsunami yapali Cisano, ifibusa nabalupwa ba abo abalubile bacili nabakwata isubilo ukutila abatemwikwa babo kuti baba nge fisungusho ifyo ifiteeka imitima panuma ya busanso ubwabipa ngobu.
Pa Chibelushi, akamulumendo akanono balikafwasulula mu mupaipi wa busali.
Pa Sande, abalepususha abantu baliisa fyantulula namayo uwatinkishiwe panshi ya fimabwe fyafikulwa panshiku shibili necitumbi cabanyina mupepi nankwe.
Ba Gendon Subandono, bakakansha bebumba lya bwangalo bwakupupuka ubwa paragliding mu Indonesia, balikanshishepo babili pali abo abalubile abali mu Mangalo yaku Asia, ayo ayapwile umweshi wafumineko mu Indonesia.
Bambi pali abo abacilikilwe pa Roa Roa Hotel, ukubikapo na ba Mandagi bali basambi babo
"Ngomukalamba mumulimo wakukansha muli ubu bwangalo bwa paragliding, ninkwata icisendo icikulu nganshi kumutima," efyo basosele.
Ba Gendon balondolwele ifyo munsa ishakonkele pakumfwa ukuwa kwa Roa Roa Hotel nokusalangana kwa ili lyashi muli bonse abacitako ubu bwangalo, batendeke ukutuma imbila shapali WhatsApp kuli bantu bacimfyanya nabo ku Palu, abalesendamo ulubali mukusefya kwa kumbali ya mumana.

"Ndetontonkanya ukuti ici cilepilibula ukuti imbila ishi tashafikile,” efyo balandile.

Bakabolala pali Cisano ebaibile $26,750 ukufuma ku mubomfi waku Brink uwalebiika indalama mu ATM pa Newport ku Levee, ukulingana ne nsebo ukufuma ku Newport Police Department.

Ilyo ali napamfiwa, umuntu umbi "aliisa butuka ukufuma ku numa ya mubomfi waku Brink" nokwiba icola ca ndalama ishali shakusalanganya.
Bakambone batile balimwene abantu abo baletunganya batendeka ukufuma pali iyi ncende, ukulingana ne nsebo, lelo bakapokola balifilwa ukulanda bwino impendwa ya bantu abaibimbile muli uyu mulandu.

Kanye West: Kemba wa nyimbo acinja ishina kuli Ye
Kemba wa nyimbo Kanye West alecinja ishina lyakwe - ukulaitwa Ye.
Mukubilisha kwakwe pa Twitter pa Cibelushi, alembele ati: "Umuntu uwaishibikwe kale nga Kanye West."
West uwamyaka 41, alipelwa ishina lyapambali ilya Ye panshita imo nokubomfya ili shina nga umutwe wa aubamu iyalenga 8 iyafumine mu mweshi wa Juni.
Ukucinja kwe shina kwaisa mukutangilila kwa kumoneka kwakwe pa Saturday Night Live, apo aleenekelwa ukwisula aubamu yakwe iipya iileitwa Yandhi.
Alepyana pali kemba Ariana Grande pali ubu bulangisho uwafuminepo pamulandu wa “malangulushi yamo-yamo” efyalandile bakapanga ba ubu bulangisho.
Pamofye ngokuba kwa kwipifya kwe shina lyakwe ilyo alebomfya muncito yakwe pali ino nshita, West kunshita yakunuma alilandilepo ukuti ili shiwi lyalikwatamo ilangulushi lya mapepo kuli wena.
"Ndesumina ukuti ‘ye’ eshiwi ilyabomfiwa sana mu Cipingo, elyo mu Cipingo lipilibula ukuti ‘iwe’” efyo West alandile ilyo balelanshanya pali aubamu yakwe iipya kukutampa kwa uno mwaka na shimulabasa Big Boy.
"Kanshi nine iwe, nine ifwe, nifwe.
Cafumine kuli Kanye, icipilibula umofye eka, ukuya kuli Ye - icilesokololafye ubusuma bwesu, ububi bwesu, ukufulungana kwesu, fyonsefye.
Iyi aubamu ilelondolola ifingi pafyo twaba."
Ni umo pali bakemba abaishibikwa nganshi mukucinja amashina yabo.

Ba kateeka baku Mexico ba AMLO balaya ukuti tabakabomfye abashilika ukulwisha abekala calo
Ba kateeka abapya aba calo ca Mexico ba Andre Manuel Lopez Obrador nabalaya ukuti tabakatale ababomfya amaka yabashilika mukulwisha abekala calo ilyo icalo cilepalamina mu kwibukisha imyaka 50 iya kusuuma kwa mulopa ukwa basambi.
Ba Lopez Obrador balaile pa Chibelushi pa Tlatelolco Plaza ukuti tabakatale ababomfya abashilika ukucusha abekala calo baku Mexico.
Abashilika balilasawile abaleilishanya mu mutende pa ncende ya plaza pa 2 Okutoba, 1968 nokwipaya abantu ukufika kuli 300 panshita ilyo amabumba yabasambi yaletendeka ukupangwa mu America.
Ba Lopez Obrador ebalaile ukutungilila imisepela yamu Mexico ukupitila mukulipililako abasambi elyo nokwiswilapo ama yunivesiti nayambi.
Batile ukubula kwa ncito elyo nokubulisha kwe shuko lyakusambilila ecilenga imisepela ileingila mu mabumba yabuntala misoka.
Icalo U.S. cilingile ukulundako indalama sha A.I.
Ilyo icalo ca China cilebombesha sana mu milimo ya fitunshitunshi, icalo ca U.S. cilingile ukulundako indalama isho ciposa mu milimo ya kufwailisha, efyalandile shimakwebo kabili uubombela kufya AI Kai-Fu Lee, uwabombapo kale naba Google, ba Microsoft elyo naba Apple.
Aya mashiwi yaisa panshita iyo ifiputulwa ifingi ifyabuteeko bwa calo ca U.S. filepanga ukubilisha kwa AI, nangu cakuti icalo ca U.S. cilemoneka ngecishikwete amanshiko ayafikapo aya AI.
Panshita imo ine, icalo ca China catendeke ubwanshiko bwaciko uyu mwaka: cilepekanya ukuba ba namba 1 mu milimo ya AI ilyo cikalafika mu 2030.
Ukulundako indalama sha kufwailisha kwa AI kuti kwaba intendekelo iisuma, makamaka panshita ilyo Ifyalo ifingi fili kunuma sana mu kupashanya ku calo ca U.S., elyo kabili tulelolesha pa kubomba bwino nakumbi ukwa AI" efyalandile ba Lee.
Ukulundako indalama kuti kwalundako ishuko lyakuti ukubomba bwino ukukakonkapo ukwa AI kukacitika mu calo ca U.S., efyo ba Lee baebele ba CNBC mukulanshanya uno mulungu.
Ba Lee, abo icitabo cabo ica "AI Superpowers China, Silicon Valley and the New World Order" cafumishiwe uno mweshi naba Houghton Mifflin Harcourt, eba CEO ba Sinovation Ventures, iyabikamo indalama ishingi nganshi mu kampani kamo pa twampani utwaishibikwa sana ku milimo ya AI mu China, aka Face++.
Mu myaka yamuma 1980 ilyo bali pa Carnegie Mellon University balebombela pa AI system iyacilike uuntu uwaishibisha sana uweshina lya Othello umwina America, elyo panuma baishileya mukubomba pa Microsoft Research elyo kabili balipo na bakalamba ba Google mu cisampa caku China.
Ba Lee balilandile pa kubomba kwakale ukwa milimo ya tekinoloji ukwa calo ca U.S. pamo nga Defense Advanced Research Projects Agency's Robotics Challenge nokwipusha palyo ukubomba kwakonkapo kulingile ukubako, pakuti kwingaba ukwishiba abantu abali nobwishibilo pali ili lyashi.
Bakafwailisha mu calo ca U.S. balingile ukubombesha pakuti bengawina indalama sha buteeko, efyalandile ba Lee.
"Te calo ca China icilesenda intungulushi sha masambililo; lelo tubungwe," efyalandile ba Lee.
Facebook, Google notwampani tumbi utwa tekinoloji mu myaka iyapita twalingisha ababomfi abengi ukufuma kuma yuniveziti abakubombela pama AI.
Ba Lee batile ukucinja kwa mafunde yakwenda kwa bantu nako kuti kwayafwilisha icalo ca U.S. ukufuntula imibombele ya ciko iya milimo ya AI.
"Ndetontonkanya ukutila amakadi ya gilini yalingile ukulapeelwafye ayene kuli abo abakwata ama PhD mu milimo ya AI," efyo balandile.
Akabungwe ka State Council akaku China kalilanda ubwanshiko bwa calo ubwa Next Generation Artificial Intelligence Development Plan mu mweshi wa Chikungu-lupepo 2017.
Iciputulwa ca National Natural Science Foundation mu calo ca China cilapeela indalama ku bantu abali mu ncende sha masambililo mu musango umo wine uubomba Iciputulwa ca National Science Foundation notubungwe tumbi utwa buteeko ukupeela indalama kuli bakafwailisha ba calo ca U.S, lelo amaka ya aya masambililo yalicepako mu China, efyalandile ba Lee.
Mukutendeka kwa uno mwaka Iciputulwa ca U.S. Defense Department caiswileko Joint Artificial Intelligence Center, iili nomulimo wakubika pamo ababomfi ukufuma ku fiputulwa fya milimo nefya masambililo, elyo ba White House nabo balandile pakupanga kwa kabungwe aketwa Select Committee on Artificial Intelligence.
Elyo uno mweshi ba DAPRA balandile pa ndalama $2 bilyoni ishakubika mu mulimo uuleitwa AI Next.
Lelo kulubali lwa ciputulwa ca NSF, pali ino nshita cilengishamo indalama ukufika kuli $100 milyoni pa mwaka mu kufwailisha kwa AI.
Kulubali lumbi, ifunde lya calo ca U.S. ilyalefwaya ukupanga National Security Commission pama Artificial Intelligence talyamoneka ukubomba mu myeshi iyapita.
Abena Macedonian bavota muli referendum pakucinja kweshina lya calo cabo
Abekala calo baku Macedonia ebasalile muli referendum pa bushiku bwapa Sande pakufwaya ukucinja ishina lya calo cabo ukulaitwa "Republic of North Macedonia," umulimo uwingapwisha ukumana ukwabapo pa myaka iingi ne calo ca Greece icacilikila nokwipusha kwabo ukuba ba membala ba European Union na NATO.
Icalo ca Greece, icakwata provinsi iyeshina lya Macedonia, citile ishina lya kukapinda kakukuso aka calo icina mupalamano limininako icakaniko cimo ica mpanga yabo elyo nacikaanya nokwingila kwabo mu NATO namu EU.
Ifi fyalo fibili fyafikile pakusuminishanya mu mweshi wa Juni pamulandu weshina lyaletelwe ilipya, lelo abapinkana no buteeko ba nationalist batile ukucinja kwe shina kuti kwafulunganya ubuntu bwaba Slavic abafulisha mu Macedonia.
Ba Kateeka ba Gjoege Ivanov batile tabakasaleko muli referendum elyo nokukaana ukongola bakasala nakuleeta ukutwishika ngacakuti bakasala bakafika pa cipimo ca 50 pesenti icifwaikwa pakuti referendum ingakwata amaka.
Ilipusho ilya pe pepala lya kusalilapo referendum lyalembelwe ati: : "Bushe mulefwaya bumembala mu NATO namu EU nokupokelela ukusuminishanya kwa calo ca Greece."
Abaletungilila ukucinja kwe shina, ukubikapo naba Prime Minister ba Zoran Zaev, baletila cilifye bwino ukulipila umutengo uwapalefi pakusuminishiwa ukwingila mutubungwe pamo nga EU na NATO ku calo ca Macedonia, icalo cimo pafilefuma mukuwa kwa Yugoslavia.
"Nacisa ilelo pakwisavotela ubuyo bwa calo, ku misepela ya calo ca Macedonia pakuti bengekala mubuntungwa mwisamba lya European Union pantu cilepilibula ubumi ubusuma kuli ifwe bonse," efyalandile ba Olivera Georgijevska, abali ne myaka 79, mu Skopje.
Nangu cakuti tacilekuma bonse, bamembala ba ng’anda ya mafunde abengi batile bakasumina ifikatumbuka mukusala pakuti ubusalo bukapangwe bwino.
Ukucinja kwe shina kulefwaikwa amavoti ya ba membala ba ng’anda ya mafunde ukucila pa cipendo ca miku itatu.
Akabungwe akabombela mukusala mu calo katile takusangilweko ubwafya mumisalile panshita ya 1 p.m.
Nangu cibefyo icipendo ca bakasala cilifye pali 16 pesenti mukupashanya kukusala kwamu ng’anda ya mafunde ukwaliko mu 2016 ukwali pali 34 pesenti lintu 66 pesenti ya bantu abalembeshe basendelemo ulubali mukusala.
"Njishile mukusala pamulandu wa bana bandi, incende yesu ni Europe," efyalandile ba Gjose Tanevski, abali ne myaka 62, bakasala mu musumba ukalamba uwa Skopje.
Ba Prime Minister ba calo ca Macedonia ba Zoran Zaev, abakashi babo ba Zorica no mwana wabo Dushko baposelemo amavoti yabo aya referendum mu Macedonia ayakucinja ishina lya calo icingabeswila inshila yakwingila mu NATO namu European Union mu Strumica, Macedonia pa 30 Sepitemba, 2018.
Pantanshi ya ng’anda ya mafunde mu Skopje, ba Vladimir Kavardarkov, abali ne myaka 54, balepekanya apakwiminina nokutantika ifipuna pantanshi yamatenti ayapangilwe nabo abalefwaya ukukanasendamo ulubali muli referendum.
"Tulefwaya ukuba mu NATO na EU, lelo tulefwaya ukwingilamo ne mitwe iyaisuka, ukucila ukwingilila mukukanaishiba" efyalandile ba Kavadarkov.
"Tuli calo icipina lelo twalicindama.
Ngacakuti tabalefwaya ukutubuula nga Macedonia, kuti twayalukila kuli bambi nga China na Russia nokwingila mu bwampano bwa Euro-Asia."
Ba Prime Minister ba Zaev batile bumembala bwa NATO bukaleta ubuyantanshi ubulefwaikwa mu Macedonia, umo umwaba icipendo cakukanaingila incito ukucila pali 20 pesenti.
"Ndesubila ukuti abantu abengi balecitungilila pantu icipendo ukufika kuli 80 pesenti ica bantu besu balitemwa EU na NATO," efyalandile ba Zaev panuma yakuposamo ivoti lyabo.
Balandile ukutila ivoti lyakuti "ee" likaba “kushininkisha kwa buyo bwesu."
Ukufwailisha ukwasabankanishiwe pali Cimo ne ciputulwa ca Institute for Policy Research mu calo ca Macedonia kwatile pakati ka 30 na 43 pesenti yabakasala ebakasendamo ulubali muli referendum - icipendo icinono ukucila icilefwaikwa.
Ukufwailisha kumbi ukwacitilwe naba Telma TV, abaku Macedonia kwasangile ukutila 57 pesenti yabantu abayaswike ebalepekanya ukuya mukuvota pa Sande.
Pali abo, abali 70 pesenti batile bakasala ukusuminisha.
Pakuti referendum ingapita kulefwaikwa abakusala ukufika pali 50 pesenti nokubikapo ivoti limo.
Ukufilwa kwakupisha iyi referendum kukemininako ubwafya ubwakulisha ku mafunde ayasuminisha ubuteeko bwaku Kabanga ukufuma apo bwatendekele ukuteeka mu mweshi wa Kapepo-kanono uyu mwaka.

Ukulongana kwaba Trump mu West Virginia
Ba Kateeka balilanda mukulosha ku lyashi ilishingulwike uusalilwe uwaku Supreme Court uweshina lya Brett Kavanaugh ilyo balelanda pa bukankala bwa kufula kwama Republican mukusala kwa pakati ka temu yabo.
"Fyonse ifyo twabomba kuti fyafulunganishiwa mu mweshi wa Novemba.
Ilyo kwashalafye imilungu isano ukufika ku kusala ukukankala nganshi mu myeo yesu.
Ici nicimo pa fikulu, ifikulu -- Nshileimininako mu kusalwa lelo cimo nokuti ndeimninako ecilengele nokuti ndesangwa konse-konse ukulwishishako abaleiminina abamaka,” efyo balandile.
Ba Trump balikonkanyapo, "Namumona ili bumba ilyabipisha, ilibi ilyama Democrats, namumona ifilecitika pali ino nshita.
Elyo kabili balefwaisha ukupokolola amaka ukubomfya inshila iili yonse iyo bengakwanisha, mumone ubunkalwe, imisuula.
Tabasakamana untu balecena, uwo balenyantapo pakuti bengaba mumaka nokutungulula, ifyo balefwaya maka nokupindulula, tatwakabapele."
Ba Trump balandile ukuti ama Democrats bali pa mulimo uwayafya "uwakukanya no kucilinganya."
"Elyo kuti mwamona ifyacitike munshiku shine ishapita,"eefyo balandile, ukwita ama Democrats "abakalipa kabili abankalwe, abamisuula kabili ababufi."
Balandile na mashiwi yalandile ba Senate Judiciary Committee ayakubika Democratic Sen. Dianne Feinstein pe shina, icaletele nokuwela ukwingi ukufuma mwibumba.
"Bushe muleibukisha ubwasuko bwakwe?
Bushe mwalisalangenye icipepala ukwabula insambu?
Uh, uh, finshi.
Awe, uh awe, ndelolela cimo - uko kwali kulanda ukubi ukwa mubili - imilandile iyabipisha iya mubili iyo nshatalamonapo."
Icipani ca Labour tacili nakabili icilonganino icikulu
Tacisuminisha abo abalanda ifishinka ifili mu malangulushi yabo
Ilyo abatungilila Momentum mu cipani candi bavotele ukuti banjiminike mu cipani, tacali cakupapusha.
Nakuba, ndifye umo pa ntungulushi nkalamba isha ciputulwa ca milimo abaebwapo ukuti tabalepokelelwa - pamulandu fye wakulanda ifili mu malangushi yesu.
Umunandi umo uwa mung’anda ya mafunde Joan Ryan nao bamucitile fimofine pamulandu wakuti alikene ukuibimba mu milimo yakususha.
Kulubali lwandi, umulandu wakwiminikwa kwandi wakumine pafyo nakeene ukusuminisha ba Jeremy Corbyn.
Pa bukankala bwe funde lya bunonshi ilingabomba, pa bucingo bwa calo, imilandu iyapalana iyo Jeremy nao akeene ukusuminsha ne ntungulushi shakunuma.
Icishibisho ca kulongana kwa Nottingham East Labour pali Cisano calandile ukuti “tulefwaya ukulongana kuleba ukwabonse kabili ukwabuyantanshi.”
Inshita iikulu iya myaka 8 iyo naba Labour MP, amamiting’i ya GC ayapali Cisano efyo yaba lyonse nifyo fine.
Kucabulanda ilelo, tefilecitika mu kulongana ukwingi elyo no bulayo bwa mashiwi ya mitekele “ayafuuka, ayamutembo” bwalilabwako ngacakuti, mucishinka, bwalitendeke.
Calishibikwafye nomba palwalala ukutila amalangulushi ayapusanako tayasuminishiwa mu cipani ca Labour elyo ne langulushi lyonse lipingulwa mukukonkana nefyo lyapokelewa nangu ukukanwa ne ntungulushi sha cipani.
Ici catendeke panumafye ba Jeremy baishileba intungulushi, ilyo ababomfi banandi abo twakwete nabo amalangulushi yamo yene kunshita yakunuma baleenekela ukuti njaluke mukwangufyanya nokusumina mufyo nshaletontonkanyapo ukusuminamo - cibe nipabucingo bwa calo nangu umushiika umo uwa EU.
Lyonse ilyo nalanda palwalala - elyo tacisakamika nefyo nalandapo - palakonka amashiwi ayayafya pa fitunshitunshi ukulanda ukuti bafwile bamfumyapo, ukususha amashiwi ya mitekele ya pakati, ukunjeba ukuti nshifwile naba mu cipani ca Labour.
Elyo ifi tefyo mpitamofye neka.
Nalishiba ukuti, naliba uwashukako ukucila ababomfi banandi bamo pantu amashiwi ayasoswa pali ine yamoneka nga mashiwi ya mitekele.
Ndasunguka sana pa mibombele no mukosha wa babomfi banandi abasushiwa nganshi pamipangilwe ne mitundu yabo cila bushiku lelo tabanenuka.
Icabulanda sana pali ino nshita mu mashiwi ya mitekele cakumona ifyo umutitikisha ulemoneka ukuba uwasuminishiwa.
Ba Jeremy Corbyn uyu mulungu batile Icipani ca Labour cifwile cakwata umubela wakupokelela fyonse.
Icishinka cakutila tatuli nakabili icilonganino icikulu ngafintu twali kale elyo nalyonse ilyo kwaba amafunde “yakukana cetekelwa” icipani ninshi cileya cilecepelako.
Nalipokelelapo bumpandamano ubwingi sana mu myaka ibili iyapita ukumpatikisha ukuponya umutwe, ukukanalandalanda lyena ninshi "fikabafye bwino."
Lelo ifyo tefyo naingilile mu mashiwi ya mitekele.
Ukufuma apo naingilile mu cipani ca Labour apo apapita imyaka 32 ngo musambi ukupatikisha no mulekelesha wa buteeko bwaba Thatcher ubwalengele ne sukulu lyandi libe mupepi nokuwa, ndafwaisha ukubombesha nokupeela ifintu ifisuma ku bekala calo abalefikabila - nangu ningabafye nga kansela nangu umukalamba wa ciputulwa ca buteeko.
Nshatala mfisapo ubwiminishi bwandi mu mashiwi ya mitekele, ukubikapofye namukusala kwakushalikisha.
Takuli nangu umo uwamu Nottingham East uwingaba uwafulungashiwa pa fikomo fyandi elyo ne fintu fimo ifyo nkanako ifya butungulushi ubulipo ilelo.
Kuli abo abatungilile ili lyashi pali Cisano, ifyo ningalandafye fyakutila ilyo icalo cilefwaisha ukuya ku Brexit iyo iikafulunganya imikalile iingi, amakwebo elyo ne milimo yesu iibombelwa abekala calo, nshileumfwikisha ubu bukabilo bwa bonaushi bwa nshita na maka pa kuipelesha kwandi kuntungulushi ya cipani ca Labour.
Lelo imbilafye imo iyo nkwete teyakuya ku Nottingham Momentum, lelo yakuya kuba muncende yandi, babe bamu cipani ca Labour nangu iyo: Naliipelesha ukumibombela kabili ndelaya ukuti tapali incintinya nangu cimo nangu amashiwi ya mitekele ayakali ayakankanya ukubomba ifyo nasuminamo ukuti efyalungama ukumibombela.
