Ayr 38 - 17 Melrose: ba Ayr abashicimfiwa baya pamulu
Ukucelwa kwa kwesha kubili nga kwalifulunganya insebo shakushalikisha, lelo takuli nokutwishika ukutila ba Ayr balingile ukucimfya muli ubu bwangalo ubwawamishe nganshi pali ubu bushiku mu Tennent Premiership.
Pali ino nshita nomba ebali pamulu, ibumbafye lyeka ilishacimfiwapo pali yonse ayalimo.
Pakulekelesha cali ciputulwa cabo icabucingo bwamupila, pamofye nokusenda bwino ishuko lyabo, ukwalengele ukuti bacimfye elyo nakakansha wabo Peter Murchie ali nensambu shonse ishakumfwa bwino.
"Twalyeshiwa mu mangalo yesu ukufika pali ino nshita, elyo kabili tatwacimfiwapo, nkanshi ningile ukuba ne nsansa,” efyo alandile.
Kumfwa Robyn Christie uwe bumba lya Melrose atile: "Ukutotela kuleya kuli ba Ayr, balibomfya amashuko yabo bwino ukutucila."
Ukwesha kwakwa Grant Anderson ukwapali mineti yalenga 14, ukwabombelwepo na Frazier Climo, ekwabikile ba Ayr kuntanshi, lelo, kadi ya yeloo iyapeelwe kuli Rory Hughes kapitawo waku Scotland, uwasuminishiwe naba Warriors ukuti ateye uyu mupila, ekwalengele ukuti ba Melrose bakwate impendwa elyo Jason Baggot aishilesenda ukwesha kwa mupila uushafikilishiwe ukuti wingile.
Climo ewalundilwile ukuteya kwaba Ayr ilyo aumine penoti, kunuma, panshitafye yakutusha, aliingisha elyo aisaalula nokwngisha akakato kakuteya eka nokufisha pali 17-5 kuli ba Ayr panshita ya kutusha.
Lelo ba Melrose balitendeka bwino icipande ca bubili ilyo Patrick Anderson aumine, Baggot nao aingisha, nokucefyako ukutalukana kwa tukato ukubwesesha pali tusano.
Kwali ukulolela ukutali pamulandu wa kuceneka kwakwa Ruaridh Knott, uwafumishiwemo, elyo lintu batendeke nakabili, ba Ayr baliya kuntanshi ukupitila mu mupila uwaumine Stafford McDowall, nokwingishiwa kumbi ukwakwa Climo.
Uwaiminineko mwipunda lyalwa kapitawo waba Ayr, Blair Macpherson pali iyi nshita aliisapelwa yeloo kadi, ba Melrose baliisaesha sana ukuti bengishe lelo umupila wauminwe na Bruce Colvine walifilikwa ukwingila, pampela yakushokana ukwakosa
Abene ba cibansa baliisa bweluluka na maka, elyo lintu Struan Hutchinson apeelwe yeloo kadi pamulandu wakusansa Climo uushakwete umupila, ukufuma pa mushilwa wa penoti, MacPherson aliisa twala umupila panshi kunuma yaba Ayr abamukonkele.
Climo nakabili aliingisha, ngefyo alecitafye inshita ishingi ukufuma apo batendekele nakabili, panuma Kyle Rowe aishile pokelela umupila waumine David Armstrong mu kabokoshi ka cipanda nokumina kapokelela Gregor Henry pamupila walenga 5 mukuteya kwabene ba cibansa.
Uwangala ubunkolanya bwa Still Game amoneka uwaipekanya ukutendeka umulimo uupya uwamakwebo yakwipika ifyakulya
Uwangala ubunkolanya bwa Still Game Ford Kieran alemoneka uwaipekanya nganshi ukwingila mu makwebo yakupokelela nokusunga abeni panuma casangilwe ukuti alisalwa ukuba umukalamba wa kampani ka aya makwebo.
Umusambashi uuli ne myaka yakufyalwa 56 ewangala pa cifulo cakwa Jack Jarvis mu bunkolanya bwaku BBC, ubo alemba nokwangala nomunankwe wanshita iitali Greg Hemphill.
Aba bantu babili balandile ukuti ubunkolanya ubuleisa ubwalenga 9 ebwakushalikisha ukutambisha, elyo cilemoneka ukuti Kiernan alepekanishisha ubumi bwakwe panuma ya Craiglang.
Ukulingana no butantiko bwa bakalamba ba milimo, emukalamba wa kampani ka Adriftmorn Limited.
Uyu kangala wabunkolanya alikana ukulandapo ifili fyonse pali ili lyashi, nangu cakuti bamo abe pepala lya Scottish Sun balandile ukuti Kiernan alefwaya ukwingila mu makwebao yakwipika ifyakulya fya makwebo ayalebomba bwino sana mu Glasgo."
'Naifwe bene bemba wesu': icalo ca Bolivia icashingulukwa nefyalo fimbi cilesubila ukuti icilye cili nokwisula inshila yakuli bemba wa Pacific
Bakooba ba mato balepitana pa ncende ikalamba iya mato mu La Paz.
Ifikuulwa fyacalo fyonse nafikobeka ama fulagi ya buluu ya bemba.
Incende ishimininamo amato ukufuma kuli Bemba wa Titicaca ukufika ku Amazon nashilembwamo amashiwi yakuti: "Naifwe bene bemba wesu.
Ukumukwata mulimo wesu."
Ukushinguluka icalo conse ica Bolivia, ukwibukisha kwa ncende yamumbali ya bemba iyo ba Chile bapokele mu mpasanse sha mulopa ishamu sencari yalenga 19 icili ileibukishiwa - ngefyo ukufwaisha ukooba amato muli Bemba wa Pacific kucili kulekabilwa nakabili.
Ili isubilo lilekulilakofye mu myaka amakumi iyapita, ilyo calo ca Bolivia cilelolela ubupingushi ukufuma ku cilye ca mulinganya ice sonde pa 1 Okutoba panuma ya myaka isano iyakulanshanya.
"Icalo ca Bolivia calikwata amaka, umupashi wa kwikatana no mutekatima, elyo kabili nokwenekela ifintu ifisuma ifikatumbukamo," efyalandile ba Roberto Calzadilla, abeminishi ba calo ca Bolivia.
Abena Bolivia abengi bakatambako ubupingushi bwa cilye ca ICJ pa fitunsitunshi ifikalamba ifya calo, ukusubila ukuti icilye camuncende ya The Hague cikomfwila abena Bolivia uluse pafyo balanda ukuti - panuma ya makumi ya myaka - icalo ca Chile cilingile ukusumina ukulanshanya pakupeelako icalo ca Bolivia inshila yakuya kuli Bemba.
Ba Evo Morales, ba kateeka ba calo ca Bolivia aba mapepo kabili - abaleshokana no bulwi bwakufwaya ukusalwa nakabili uyu mwaka - nabakwata ukutungililwa ukwamaka mu bupingushi bwa pali Cimo.
"Tuli mupepi sana nokubwelela ku Pacific Ocean," efyo balapile mukupwa kwa mweshi wa Kasaka-ntobo.
Lelo bamo abafwailisha amalyashi baletila kwena icilye limbi tekuti cipingule kubusuma bwa calo ca Bolivia - elyo nokutila finonofye ifikacinja ngacakuti cacita ifyo.
Akabungwe ka UN akasangwa mu Netherlands takakwete amaka ayakupeela incende iyabena Chile, elyo kabili nakatila tekakapingula ifikatumbuka mu kulanshanya ukukabako.
Icishinka cakuti ubupingushi bwa cilye ca ICJ buleisa panumafye ukulanshanya kwakulekelesha kwalangile ukuti umulandu “taushupile,” efyalandile ba Paz Zárate, abaishibisha ifya mafunde ye sonde abamu calo ca Chile.
Elyo nakulubali lwakuwamya ifintu ku bena Bolivia, cilemoneka ukuti imyaka ine iyapita yalifibweseshako kunuma.
"Ilyashi lyakukwata inshila yakuya kuli bemba lyalikatililwa no butungulushi ubulipo mu calo ca Bolivia,” efyalandile Zárate.
Umupatikisha wa bulwi uwaba Morales walisuka wafumyamo ubusuma bonse ubo icalo ca Chile cakwete, efyo balandile.
Icalo ca Bolivia na Chile panshita imo kuti fyalanshnaya, lelo cikaba icakosa sana ukukonkanyapo ukulanshanya panuma ya ifi.
Ifi fyalo fibili tafyatala afitumishanyapo abeminishi ba fyalo ukufuma mu mwaka wa 1962.
Bakateeka bakale ba Eduardo Rodríguez Veltzé, abeminishi ba calo ca Bolivia ku The Hague, balikana ilangulushi lyakuti ubusalo bwa cilye inshita ishingi bwali bwamukwangufyanya.
Ubushiku bwapali Cimo bukaletela icalo ca Bolivia "ishuko ilyailbela ilyakwisula inshita iipya iyabwampano ne calo ca Chile" ne shuko "lyakupwisha imyaka 139 iyakukanaumfwana mu bwampano bwabunonshi,” efyo balandile.
Ba Calzadilla nabo balikana ukutila ba Morales - umo pali bakateeka abaishibikwa nganshi pababa mu Latin America - balebomfya ilyashi lyapali bemba ngo mulandu wakutungililamo amashiwi ya mitekele.
"Icalo ca Bolivia tacakatale acilekelako ku nsambu shakukwata bemba wa Pacific Ocean," efyo balundilepo.
"Ubupingushi kuti bwaba lishuko ilyo tulekabila ilyakucimfishamo ifyakale."
Icalo ca North Korea citile ukufumya amaka ku minshinga ya nyukiliya takwakacitike kanofye ngacingacetekela icalo ca US
Abakalamba abangalila Iciputulwa Icilolesha pa Fyakunse ya Calo mu North Korean ba Ri Yong Ho batile icalo cabo tacakatale acifumya amaka ku minshinga ya nyukiliya pakubala ilyo tacilecetekela umusumba wa Washington.
Ba Ri balandile aya mashiwi pa Cibelushi pa ncende ya United Nations General Assembly.
Balilomba ku calo ca United States ukuti cingafikilisha amalayo ayo capangile pa kulongana kwaku Singapore pakati ka ntungulushi ishilwishanya.
Amashiwi yabo yaisa ilyo Bakalemba ba calo ca US ba Mike Pompeo balemoneka ukuba mupepi nokutendeka ukulanshanya ukwakakata ukwapa minshinga ya nyukiliya apo apapita imyeshi itatu ukufuma apo kwabelelele ukulanshanya kwaku Singapore naba Kim Jong Un abaku North Korea.
Ba Ri batile "ciloto icishakacitike" icakuti ifibindo ifyakonkanyapofye ifya calo ca U.S. elyo nokukana landa bwangu ukupwisha inkondo ya calo ca Korea kuti kwalenga icalo caku Kapinda ka Kukuso ukucimba.
Umusumba wa Washington nausakamana pa kusuminisha ukulanda kwa musumba wa Pyongyang ukwakubalilapo ukutendeka ukufumyamo amaka ya minshinga.
Ba Kim pamo naba Kateeka ba calo ca U.S. Ba Donald Trump balefwaya kukabe ukulongana kwacibili.
Lelo kuli ukutwishika kwakuti umusumba wa Pyongyang kuti waba abaipela ukulekelako ku cintu ico bamona nga cimofye icakubacingilila .
Ba Pompeo balepekanya ukutandalila umusumba wa Pyongyang ku kukumana kwa cibili ukwaba Kim naba Trump.
Amakwebo ya mifwalile mu Paris yalangisha ukubomba ukupya ukwafyakufwala fyakumitwe ifili mukuletwa mu High Street mupepi naimwe
Ngacakuti mulefwaya ukulundako ubwing bwa fisote fyenu nangu ifyakumicingilila ku kasuba mwiya ukutali.
Bakapanga ba Valentino naba Thom Browne ebasokolwele ifisote ifyamisango na misango mukukolonganika kwa SS19 mu mbali ya musebo ifyabengeshimishe ubutantiko pa Paris Fashion Week.
Ifisote ifisuma nganshi efilemonekela pa Instagram ino nshita ya lusuba elyo bakapanga nabo ebatumine ifyakupanga ifyayemba ku ncende shonse namumisebo yonse.
Icisote icacililemo ubusuma icapangilwe na Valentino cali icikulu icelangi lyabutulukila icakwete impela iyapala amasako iyalefimba bwino umutwe wa ufwele.
Fimbi ifyali ifikulu fyali ni cimo icabamo notubekobeko twalutanga-menshi, icisote ca ndoshi elyo necapala icinanashi - lelo ifi tafyapangilwa ukuleta icikabilila ku mitwe.
Ba Thom Browne kabili balisokolola ififimbo fyaku menso - ilyofye kwashala panono ukufika ku Halloween.
Ififimbo ifingi ifyaku menso fyalikwete imilomo iyabilililwapo kabili fyalemoneka nga Hannibal Lecter ukucila haute couture.
Icapangilwe cimo calemoneka ngefyakufwala fyakowelamo pa mumana (scuba diving gear) ukubikako nomupaipi nama gilasi, elyo cimbi naco calemoneka nga akakopo ka aisi kilimu iyasungululwa.
Elyo ngacakuti wakonkanyapo amashiwi ya makwebo ya fyakufwala ayakulu - ninshi washuka.
Abaceceta ifyamifwaille batile ifi fisote ifikulu pali ino nshita fileenda nokufika mu misebo iipalamine kuli imwe.
Ifisote ifikulu filemoneka bwino ukufwalila pa nsapato ishitali ishakwa 'La Bomba', icisote ca fyani icakwata impela shibili cilamoneka ku mitwe yabengi ukufuma kuli Rihanna ukufika kuli Emily Ratajkowski.
Icipe cimbi icasendele sana abantu mukulunda pali ici cisote icaleshinguluka pa fitunshitunshi nokulenga icakupanga nacimbi cishibikilwemo - kacola ka fyani akalemoneka mubukulu nge cisote ico kalepashanya kuli uyu uucifwele.
Akasote ka macungwa-macungwa aka raiffia, umwalesangwa utwakupikula elyo no mukobelo wa mpapa iyabuta ekaishibikwe sana mufyakukolonganya fyakwa Jacquemus' La Riviera SS19 pa Paris Fashion Week.

John Edward: Ukwishiba ifitundu cikankala nganshi ku bekala calo isonde lyonse
Amasukulu ayaibombela ku calo ca Scotland yalikonkanyapo ukuba pamulu mukubomba bwino mu masambililo, neci nacikonkanyapo namu 2018 ilyo kuli ukupaasa nakumbi ukusuma nganshi, uko ukukoseleshiwefye nokuibikapo kwa cila muntu elyo nokubombela pamo mu mangalo, ifyakupangapanga, ukwimba elyo nemilimo imbi iyamuncende.
Ilyo abasambi balefula ukufika ku cipendo ca 30,000 mu calo ca Scotland, aya masukulu, ayaleimininwako ne ciputulwa ca Scottish Council of Independent Schools (SCIS), yalalwisha namaka ukupeela amasambililo nokubomba ukwafikapo ku basambi naku bafyashi.
Amasukulu ayaibombela yaiminina pa kupekanya abasambi ukuya ku masambililo yapamulu, ukubomba imilimo iyo bafwaya elyo nokukwata incende yabo ngabekala calo be sonde.
Nge ciputulwa ca masambililo icingapanga nokufikilisha ubutantiko bwa masambililo ubwafikapo, tulemona ifyo ifitundu ifipya filefulilako nokufwaikwa nge fisambililo mu masukulu yesu.
Ba Nelson Mandela batile: "Ngawalanda ku muntu mu citundu ico omfwa, ninshi ifyo walanda fyaya ku mutwe wakwe.
Ngawalanda kuli ena mu citundu cakwe ninshi fyaya ku mutima wakwe."
Ici cibukisho icisuma sana icakuti tekuti tushintililefye pa Cingeleshi ilyo tulefwaya ukukuula ubwampano nokucetekelwa na bantu ukufuma ku fyalo fimbi.
Ukufuma ku fyatumbwike mu mashindano ya uno mwaka, kuti twamona ukuti ifitundu efileba pamulu mu butantiko bwa kupaasa sana mu masukulu ayaibombela.
Abasambi ukufika kuli 68 pesenti abasambilila ifitundu fyakunse ya calo ebapaashile sana ukufika pali Giledi A ya Pamulu.
Ili lyashi, ilyasendelwe ukufuma ku masukulu 74 ayamu SCIS, lyalangile ukuti 72 pesenti ya basambi balipashile ukufika pali Giledi A ya Pamulu mu citundu ca Mandarin, 72 pesenti bali ni abo abalesambilila ici German, 69 pesenti abalesambilila ici French elyo 63 pesenti balesambila ici Spanish nabo balikwete Giledi A.
Ici cilelangisha ukuti amasukulu ayaibombela mu calo ca Scotland yaletungilila ifitundu fyakunse ya calo nge fintu ifikankala ifyo abana ne misepela bakalakabila kunshiku sha kuntanshi.
Ifitundu nomba, nge cisambililo cakusalapo, filesendwa mu musango umo wine nge fisambililo fya sayanshi nangu STEM (sayanshi, tekinoloji, ifyakulungisha ne nsamushi) mu butantiko bwa fisambililo mu masukulu ayaibombelafye elyo na masukulu yambi.
Ukufwailisha ukwacitilwe naba UK Commission for Employment and Skills mu mwaka wa 2014 kwasangile ukuti pa milandu abengisha incito bapele iyo bashupikilwa ukwisushisha ififulo fyancito, 17 pesenti yali nipamulandu wa kubulisha kwa bwishibilo fya fitundu.
Kanshi ukufula kwa bwishibilo bwa fitundu kulefwaikwa sana pakupekanishisha imisepela ku ncito shabo ishakuntanshi.
Panshita ilyo incito ishingi shilefwaya abakwete ubwishibilo bwa fitundu, ubu bwishilo bukankala mwisonde ililebombela pamo.
Tacilesakamika incito iyo umuntu asala, ngacakuti alisambililako icintundu cabubili, akakwata ishuko kuntanshi ilyakukwata umulimo uwakwikalilila ngoyu.
Ukukwanisha ukulanshanya nabantu wemwine abakufyalo fimbi kukalenga umuntu uwaishiba ifitundu ifingi ukuba neshuko ilyacila bambi.
Ukulingana nokufwailisha kwaba YouGov ukwa bantu abakalamba abali 4,000 abaku UK mu mwaka wa 2013, abantu ukufika kuli 75 pesenti balifililwe ukulanda icitundu cakunse ya calo mukulanshanya bwino nabantu bambi elyo ici French ecitundufye icalandilwe ne cipendo cabantu icikulileko pali 15 pesenti.
Ici eco cibelele icikankala nomba ukubika indalama mukusambilisha kwa fitundu ku bana ba lelo.
Ukwishiba ifitundu ifingi, makamaka ifyakufyalo ifilekula, cikafwilisha abana ukukwata ishuko lyakusanga incito iyalondololoka.
Mukati ka calo ca Scotland, cila isukulu likapusana mu fitundu ifyo likalafundisha.
Amasukulu yamo yakaposa sana amano ku fitundu ifipya, elyo yambi nayo yakalafundisha ifitundu ifimoneka ukuba ifikankala ku calo ca UK ilyo kuli ukulolesha kuntanshi ku mwaka wa 2020, pamo nga ici Mandarin nangu ici Japanese.
Ifili fyonse ifyo umwana wenu akalafwaya, kukaba ifitundu ifingi ifyakusalapo mu masukulu ayaibombela, nabakafundisha abakanshiwa muli ulu lubali.
Amasukulu ayaibombela ayamu Scotland nayaipelesha ukupanga incende yamasambililo iikapekanya abana nokubapangasha no bwishibilo ubulekabilwa pakuti bengaya pantanshi, muli conse icingaba kuntanshi yabo.
Tekuti cikanishiwe pali ino nshita, muncende ya makwebo ye sonde lyonse, ukutila ifitundu fyalikonkanyapo ukuba ifikankala ku buyo bwa calo, kanshi ici cifwile camonekela mu masambililo.
Mu cishinkafye, ifitundu fyaino nshita filingile ukutontonkanishiwapo "ngefya kulanshanishishanyamo ne sonde lyonse."
Amasukulu ayaibombela yakakonkanyapo ukupeela ubu busalo, ukufula kwa fitundu nokuwamya imisambilile ya misepela yamu calo ca Scotland.
Tulingile ukubomba bwino-bwino.
Ba John Edward e Bakalamba ba ciputulwa ca Scottish Council of Independent Schools
LeBron ukuteya umuku wakubalilapo muli ba Lakers pa Sande mu San Diego
Ukulolela nomba kwalapwa ku batamba umupila abalefwaya ukutamba LeBron James ukutendeka ukuteya muli ba Los Angeles Lakers.
Kakansha we bumba lya Lakers uweshina lya Luke Walton ewalandile ukuti James akateya mu bwangalo bwa kwiswila pa Sande ilyo bakalashokana naba Denver Nuggets mu San Diego.
Lelo amamineti yantu akateyamo tayalati yalandwe.
"Kuti yaba ukucila pali mineti imo kabili ukucepako pa mamineti 48," efyalandile ba Wallton pa “webusaiti” yaba Lakers".
Kasabankanya we lyashi uwaba Lakers Mike Trudell alembele pa Twitter ukutila James cilemoneka ukuti akateyafye amamineti ayalingwa.
Ukukonkana nokuteyanishisha kwa mupila uno mulungu, James balimwipwishe pa mapange yakwe pa butantiko bwa mangalo mutanda ayaba Lakers ayakutangilila inshita ya mangalo.
"Nshilekabila amangalo yakutangilila inshita ya kuteya pali ino nshita ya ncito yandi pakuti ningaipekanya," efyo ayaswike.
Inshita ya Kulongana kwaba Trump ku West Virginia, Umulabasa wa YouTube
Bakateeka ba Donald Trump baletendeka ukulongana kwabo ukwakongola bakasala ilelo ubushiku mu Wheeling, West Virginia.
Uku nikumo pa kulongana 5 uko ba Trump bapekenye mu mulungu uwakonkapo, ukubikapo napa matuuka ayabela mu ncende umwaba abantu ukubikapo namu Tennessee namu Mississippi.
Ilyo ukushininkisha kwe voti kulelolelwa ukwakwisushisha icifulo camu Supreme Court, Ba Trump balefwaya ukukusha ukutungililwa ku kusala kwa pakati ka temu ukuleisa apo ba Republican bali pa busanso bwakulufya ubutungulushi bwamu Ng'anda ya Mafunde ilyo amavoti yakabako mu mweshi wa Novemba.
Bushe ninshita nsh iyo ukulongana kwaba Trump ukwaku West Virginia kulebako ilelo ubushiku elyo kabili kuti mwatampa shani pa intaneti?
Inshita ya Kulongana kwaba Trump ku West Virginia ibikilwe pa 7 p.m. ET ilelo ubushiku, pa Cibelushi, 29 Sepitemba, 2018.
Kuti mwatamba ukulongana kwaba Trump ukwaku West Virginia pa YouTube ukupitila muli live stream.
Ba Trump baleenekelwa ukulanda pakulublula kwa uno mulungu ukuli ku cilye ca Supreme Court pamulandu waba Brett Kavanaugh, ukwakosele sana pamulandu wa mutunganya wakufwaya ukulunganya umwanakashi kumaka ilyo ivoti ililepembelwa ilya kushininkisha kwaba kwiminikwe ukufika pa mulungu ilyo ba FBI balefwailisha.
Lelo umulimo uukalamba uwa uku kulongana konse kwafwilisha ba Republican ukuipekanishisha bwino ku kusala kwamu Novemba ukulepalamina.
Kanshi, amakampeni yaba Kateeka ba Trump ayamuli uku kulonga kusano muli uyu mulungu yeminine pa "kupela amaka kuli abo abaipelefye elyo nabaletungilila ba Republican ukwesha ukucingilila nokukusha ifipuna ifyo bakwata mu Senate na Mung’anda ya Beminishi," ukulingana no mulabasa wa Reuters.
"Ukutungulula kwa Ng’anda ya Mafunde (Congress) nakubakosela ba kateeka icakuti balingile ukwenda mu ncende ishingi ilyo tuleingila mu nshita iyapamfiwa iya kongola bakasala," efyo uulelandilako ibumba lyamakampeni ilyaba Trump uwakene ukumulumbula aeble ba Reuters.
Ukupekanishiwe ukubela ku Wesbanco Arena mu Wheeling, ukulongana kwa lelo kuti kwaleta abatungilila ukufuma ku "Ohio na Pennsylvania elyo nabakutamba abengi pa mulabasa wa Pittsburgh," ukulingana naba West Virginia Metro News.
Ubushiku bwapa Cibelushi ebukaba bwa cibili mu mweshi ubwaba Trump ukutandalila incende ya West Virginia, nakuba kuli iyi ncende ekwali ukucimfya kwa mavoti ukucila pali 40 pesenti mukusala kwamu 2016.
Ba Trump baleesha ukwafwilisha abeminine ku West Virginia mu cipani cama Republican Senate ba Patrick Morrisey, abo abashalileko muli uku kusala.
"Tacili icilangililo icisuma kuli ba Morrisey ukuti ba kateeka balingile ukwisa nokubafwilishako ukulundako amavoti," efyalandile ba Simon Haeder, abasambilisha ifya mashiwi ya mitekele pa West Virginia University, ukulingana no mulabasa wa Reuters.
Icikombe ca Ryder 2018: Ibumba lya Team USA lyalanga amaka yakulwisha pakusungilila isubilo ilyo kuli ukupalamina ku kuteya kwapa Sande ukwaumo-umo
Panuma yakuteya kutatu ukwafipande fyalubali lumo, ukuteya kwapa Cibelushi ukwa 4/4 limbi kuti kwaba eko Icikombe ca Ryder calekabila.
Ukushinguluka kwa pendulum ya momentum lyashi lyamangalo ilipya lelo limo ilyo abaleyangala basuminemo, kabili ukwingacilanapo pakucimfyanya ukwapala uku.
Kanshi nipesa apo bengatila epo momentum ili pali ino nshita?
"Baciba pantanshi no tukato 6 nomba pali ino nshita twashala 4, kanshi tuletunganya ukuti ico kuti caba kulunda kwa maka," efyalandile Jordan Spieth ilyo ainwike pampela ya ubu bushiku.
Icishinka cakuti, ba Europe bali ne shuko, utukato tune pantanshi ilyo kwashala amangalo ikumi na yabili.
Abena American, ukulingana nefilandile Spieth, baleimona ukuti nabakwatako icimwela icingi icakuitwalila pantanshi elyo nabakwata ifyakubakoselesha ifingi, ukubikapo na Spieth na Justin Thomas abateyele akasuba konse nokwingisha cilaumo utukato tutatu patuli tune.
Spieth euli uwakalipisha mukwingisha utukato ukufuma ku ‘tee’ ukufika ku ‘green’ ukuba nge cakumwenako.
Kulya kuwelesha kwa kusefya kwaleya kulekulilakofye ilyo ukuteya kwakwe kwaleya pantanshi, ukwingisha akakato akayafya ukulinganya pa tukato 4 mumbali shonse ilyo wena na Thomas balishalileko no tukato tubili-tubili.
Akakato kakwe akalengele bacimfye ubu bwangalo bwalenga 15 kapokelelwe nokuwelesha kumo kwine, umusango wakusefya uwingamyeba ukuti alisumine ukuti ibumba lya bena America tekuti lifumemo muli ubu bwangalo.
"Mulingilefye ukwimba intunkwe nokusakamana pa bwangalo bwenu," efyalandile Spieth.
Echimofye ico cila umo uwa ili ibumba lya bakateya ashele naco.
Ifilindi 18 pakuti bengapanga icishilwa.
Bakateya abalipofye no tukato utwingi ukucila Spieth na Thomas panshiku shibili ishapita ni Francesco Molinari na Tommy Fleetwood, ilyashi ilishili lyakutwishika ilya Ryder Cup.
Aba bantu babili abaku Europe baba mucipande ca 4 ukufuma kuli 4 elyo kabili tekuti balufyanye.
"Ba Moliwood" ebantufye babili abashakwanishe ukwingisha akakato ka bogey pa Cibelushi icungulo, lelo kabili tabalefwaya ukuma ama bogey pa Cibelushi ulucelo, pali Cisano icungulo elyo nefya kunuma ifili 9 pali Cisano ulucelo.
Kulya kubutuka, elyo nefyo amaka yabo yalemoneka ukufuma kuli cinkupiti wa bantu cileshininkisha ukuti aba ebakateya aba kucimfya pa Sande, elyo takwakabe kateya naumbi uwaishibikwa sana uwakwisalila ukucimfya ukwingacitika mu Europe ilyo akasuba kawa kuli ba Le Golf National ukucila kuli ba Fleetwood nangu ba Molinari.
Icingacitikila pamuku umowine mutulindi utwapusana.
Nangu cibefyo, ukulanda pa lulumbi lwabena Europe kucili takulalinga.
Ukuteya kwakwa Bubba Watson na Webb Simpson kulengele ukuteya kwakwa Sergio Garcia ukumoneka ukwapelebela, uyo uwaciba ni kacimfya mu nshita ya lucelo, ilyo acibikwa pamo na Alex Noren.
Akakato ka bogey elyo notuma double tubili pantanshi ya 9 kwacingisha umwina Spain no mwina Sweden mu cilindi umo bafililwe ukufuma.
Pa Sande, nangu cibefyo, tapali nangu umo uwakumyafwako ukumifumya mu cilindi.
Ukuteya kwa 4 na 4 kulomfwika bwino ukutambila mupepi pamulandu wabwampano ububa pabaleteya babili-babili, bumpandamano ubo bapeela, bumpandamano ubo bashipeela elyo nefyo imiteyele ingacinja mukashita akanono.
Ba Europe baliteyapo bwino nge bumba ukufika pali ino nshita elyo kabili ebali pantanhsi ilyo baleingila mu bushiku bwa kushalikisha lelo mukuteya kwa 4 na 4 ukwa iyi nshita ya mangalo kulelanga ukuti ibumba lya Team USA nalyo nalikwata amaka yakulwisha ayo bamo, makamaka ba Stateside, baletwitwishika.
Ba Europe bali pantanshi no tukato 10-6 pa bushiku bwa kushalikisha ubwa Cikombe ca Ryder Cup
Ba Europe balekwata ishuko ilisuma ilyo baleingila mu bushiku bwa kushalikisha ubwa Cikombe ca Ryder Cup panuma ya kucimfya kwa bwangalo bwa 4 na 4 ubwapa Cibelushi notukato 10-6 pantanshi yaba United States.
Abalumendo abapambana babili Tommy Fleetwood na Francesco Molinari ebatungulwile ukushokana nokucimfya kubili kuli ba Tiger Woods abalewishikana nokulundako utukato utli 4 pa pacibansa ca Le Golf National.
Ibumba lyabena Europe ilyakwa Thomas Bjorn, ililefwaisha ukubwesha icikombe ico balushile pa Hazeltine imyaka ibili iyapita, ebali pantanshi ya bena America abalepusa-pusa mu kuteya kwa 4 na 4 ukwa lucelo, nokukwata utukakato 3-1.
Ibumba lya U.S. baleesha ukukosa mukuteya kwa 4 na 4, ukuwinako amangalo yabili, lelo nabafilwa ukukwanisha ukufisha pa tukato.
Ibumba lyakwa Jim Furyk lilekabila utukato 8 ukufuma mu kuteya ukuli 12 ukwa umo-umo ukulebako pa Sande pakuti lingabwesha icikombe.
Fleetwood eumo umupya mu bwangalo uwakubalilapo ku Europe ukucimfya utukato 4 utwakonkana ilyo wena na Molinari, abetwa ishina lya "Molliwood" panuma ya kuteya ukwamaka ukwapa mpela ya mulungu ebakwanishefye ukukwata utukato 4 mu mangalo 4 ayakwiswila ukufuma apo amangalo ya Ryder Cup yatendekele.
Panuma ya kucimfya Woods na Patrick Reed mukuteya kwa 4 na 4 nokuteya namaka ukucimfya Woods uwatompoka elyo na umbi umupya mu bwangalo uwaku American Bryson Dechambeau mukupusanakofye na kakato kamo pali 5 na 4.
Woods, uwaile aleisendelenkanyafye mu mangalo yabili ayapa Cibelushi, alilangako ukuteya bwino panshita shimo lelo nomba nalusapo 19 pa mangalo yakwe 29 mukuteya kwa 4 na 4 elyo pa miku 7 mukukonkana.
Justin Rose, alitusha mukuteya kwa 4 na 4 ukwalucelo, nokubwela ukwisayafwana na Henrik Stenson mukuteya kwa 4 na 4 nokucimfya Dustin Johnson na Brooks Koepka 2 na 1- ababa pa nambala 1 na 3 mwisonde lyonse.
Abena Europe tefyonse fyabawimine pali ubu bushiku ubusuma, ubwa kamwela lwaku masamba ya musumba wa Paris.
Uwacimfyapo imiku itatu Jordan Spieth na Justin Thomas ebatendeke ukwimika ishina ilisuma ku bena America ilyo baingishe utukato tubili pa Cibelushi.
Bakwete utukato 2 na 1 ukucimfya Jon Rahm na Ian Poulter abaku Spain mukuteya kwa 4 na 4 nokubwela kabili ukwisa cimfya Poulter na Rory McIlroy 4 na 3 mukuteya kwa 4 na 4 panuma yakuluusa utulindi tubili utwakwiswila.
Nipa miku ibili mu mulumbe wa cikombe ca Ryder Cup ilyo ibumba lyabweluluka ukufuma mukucimfiwa kwa takato 4 nokwingila mukuteya kwa umo-umo, nangu cakuti ibumba lyakwa Furyk lilekabilafye nangu ukulingana kwatukato (draw) pakuti bengasunga icikombe.
Panuma yakuba abacibili mukuteya ukusuma pa nshiku shili, lelo, cilemoneka kwati ukuteya kwapa Sande kwena kukabakosela.
Icalo ca North Korea citile 'takuli inshila' iingabomfiwa palwaikofye iyakufumisha amaka ya minshinga yabo ukwabula icicetekelo
Abalolesha kufya Kunse ya Calo mu North Korea baebele icisaka ce sonde lyonse ica United Nations pa Cibelushi ukutila ifibindo filekoseshako ukukanacetekelwa kwa calo ca United States elyo takuli no musango untu icalo cingalekeleko ku fyanso fyaciko ifya nyukiliya mukukonkana nefilecitika.
Ba Ri Yong Ho baebele Inganda Nkalamba (General Assembly) iya cisaka ce sonde lyonse ukutila icalo ca North Korea calisenda "inshila ishamusuma" mu mwaka wapwile, pamo nga ukuleka ukwesha iminshinga ya nyukiliya, ukonaula incende yakweseshapo iminshinga elyo nokukanalundapo iminshinga ya nyukiliya pamo tefisolobelo fyakupangila.
"Nangu cibefyo, tatulemona ubwasuko ubuli bonse ukufuma ku calo ca U.S.," efyo balandile.
"Ngacakuti takuli ukucetekelwa ukuli konse ku calo ca U.S. takwakabe icicetekelo icili conse mu bucingo bwa calo cesu elyo ngacaba muli uyu musango tapakabe inshila nangu imo iingabomba ukuifumisha ifyanso fyesu fwebene."
Ilyo ba Ri balebwekeshapo ukuilishanya ukwaseeka ukwa calo ca North Korea pamulandu wa kukana kwa musumba wa Washington panshila "ishatantikwa" ishakufumishamo iminshinga ya nyukiliya isho icalo ca North Korea cingalambwilwapo ngacakuti casenda intampulo mukukonkana, amashiwi yabo yaliumfwika ayakankala mukumona ukuti tabakene ukufumya kwa minshinga ya nyukiliya palwabo abene ngefyo umusumba wa Pyongyang wabombapo munshiku shakunuma.
Ba Ri balandile pa mashiwi ayalandilwe naba Kim Jong Un elyo naba Donald Trump pakukumana kwali ukwakubalilapo ukucitika pakati kakwa kateeka wa calo ca U.S. elyo naka kateeka wa North Korea mu Singapore pa 12 Juni, ilyo ba Kim balaile ukubombela pa “kufumya amaka ya minshinga ya nyukiliya mu ncende ya Korean peninsula” elyo ba Trump nabo balaile ukupeela ubucingo ubwafikapo ku calo ca North Korea.
Icalo ca North Korea caba pakufwailisha inshila yakupwishishamo Inkondo yaku Korea iyacitike mu 1950-53, lelo icalo ca United States catila umusumba wa Pyongyang ulingile watala walekelako ku minshinga yauko iya nyukilia.
Umusumba wa Washington nao walikana ukupapata kwa kunashako ifibindo pa calo ca North Korea.
"Icalo ca U.S. calikosapofye pa "kubalilapo ukufumya amaka ya minshinga ya nyukiliya" elyo nokukoshako ukupatikisha ukupitila mukukoseshako ifibindo pakuti bafikilishe ubufwayo bwabo mumusango wakupatikisha, pamofye nokukana ku "mashiwi yakupwisha kwa nkondo,"" Efyo balandile.
"Ukutontonkanya ukuti ifibindo kuti fyalenga ukuti tucimbe ciloto fye icishakafikilishiwe icabantu abashatwishiba bwino.
Lelo ubwafya bwakutila ukukonkanyapo kwa fibindo kulelundakofye ukukana cetekela kwesu."
Ba Ri balilandapo pa mapange yakukumana kwacibili ukwaba Kim naba Trump uko intungulushi ya calo ca U.S. yalandilepo pa United Nations mukutendeka kwa uno mulungu.
Ba cililo ba buteeko balandile pa kukumana kutatu pakati kaba Kim ne ntungulushi ya South Korea ba Moon Jae mu myeshi isano iyapita nokulundapo ukutila: "Ngacakuti abalelanda pali ili lyashi lya kufumya amaka ya minshinga ya nyukiliya niba South Korea ukucila pali ba U.S., ukufumya amaka ya minshinga mu ncende ya Korean peninsula ngatakwakosa muli uyu musango."
Nangu cibefyo, imilandile yaba Ri yalipusanako kufyo balandile uyu mwaka, ilyo baleeba ba U.N. General Assembly ukutila ukusonta iminshinga ya calo ca North Korea pa calo ca U.S. cintu icishingafilikwa panuma "Kateeka Umubi" Trump aitile ba Kim "umuntu wa minshinga" uuli pa mulimo wakuikulika.
Uno mwaka pa cisaka ca United Nations, ba Trump, abatinishe na mashiwi ya "konaula umupwilapo" icalo ca North Korea, balibikapo amalumbo pali ba Kim pakushipa kwabo ukwakusenda intampulo shakufumya amaka ya minshinga, lelo batile kuli imilimo iingi iilingile ukucitwa elyo ifibindo fifwile fyaikalafye fintu fili mpaka icalo ca North Korea cikafumyemo iminshinga ya nyukiliya.
Pali Citatu, ba Trump tabakwete inshita iyapekanishiwa mukubomba uyu mulimo, nokutila "ngacasenda imyaka ibili, imyaka itatu nangu imyeshi isano - tacilesakamika."
Icalo ca China na Russia balelanda ukutila ba U.N. Security Council bafwile balambula umusumba wa Pyongyang pa ntampulo ishasendelwepo.
Nangu cibefyo, ba U.S. Secretary of State ba Mike Pompeo baebele ba U.N. Security Council pali Cine ukutila: "Ukukosha kwa fibindo fyaba Security Council kulingile kwakonkanyapo namaka mpaka tukashininkishe ukuti iminshinga ya nyukiliya yafumishiwa mumupwilapo, kabili mukushininkisha."
Ba Security Council balilundako amaka ya fibindo fya calo ca North Korea ukwabula ukukanishiwa ukutendeka mu mwaka wa 2006 pakuti bengacefya indalama shakuya ku milimo ya minshinga ya nyukiliya ku.
Ba Pompeo bakumenye ba Ri panshita ya U.N. General Assembly napanuma batile bakatandalila umusumba wa Pyongyang nakabili uyu mweshi uuleisa mukupekanishisha ukulongana kwa cibili.
Ba Pompeo balitandalilapo icalo ca North Korea imiku itatu muli uno mwaka, lelo ubulendo bwa kushalikisha tabwaendele bwino.
Bafumine mu Pyongyang mu Julai nokutila ifintu filifye bwino, lelo panumafye ya nsa ishinono icalo ca North Korea caliisa kana amashiwi yabo nokutila balepanga "ifyakupamfya kwati mukalamba waba ntalamisoka."
Icalo ca North Korea calaile ukukumana naba Moon uno mweshi pakonaula incende ya minshinga elyo ne cikuulwa ca nyukiliya ngacakuti icalo ca United States casendapo "intampulo ishayana."
Batile ba Kim balibebele ukutila "intampulo ishayana" isho balefwaya ninshila sha bucingo isho ba Trump balaile mu Singapore elyo nokubomba ukukumine kukuwamya kwa bwampano no musumba wa Washington.
Abasambi bapa Harvard batendeka icisambililo cakukwata ukutuusha ukwalinga
Icisambililo icipya pe sukulu likalamba ilya Harvard University uno mwaka nacilenga abasambi abapya balesendama sana pakuti bengacefyako ulutambi ulwaishibikwa nga ‘macho’ ulwakubelenga kwabantu ababelenga ‘bushiku bonse’ mukubomfiwa no muti wa kafeni.'
Kafundisha umo asangile abasambi bape sukulu likalamba ilye sonde lyonse inshita ishingi ukwabula ubwishibilo mu lyashi lya fikomo fyakusunga bwino imyeo yabo.
Ba Charles Czeisler, incenshi mu muti wakusendama pa Harvard Medical School kabili shing’anga pa Brigham and Women's Hospital, ebapangile ici cisambililo ico batile kwena ecakubalilapo mu musango wa ciko mu calo ca US.
Bakoseleshiwe ukutendeka ici cisambililo panuma yakulanda pafyo ukubulisha utulo kufulunganya imisambililile.
'Pampela ya kulanda kwabo umukashana umo alishile nokutila: 'Mulandu nshi naebelwa ifi fintu mukucelwa ilyo ndi mu mwaka wesukulu lya pamulu?'
Alandile ukuti tapaba nangu umo uwatala amwebapo ifili fyonse pa bukankala bwa tulo - icampapwishe sana,’ efyo baebele ipepala lye lya ilya Telegraph.
Ici cisambililo, icatendeke pa muku wakubalilapo uno mwaka, cilelondolwela abasambi ubukankala bwafyo imisendamine isuma yafwilisha ukubomba bwino mu masambililo na mumangalo ya lubilo, pamofye nokuwamya imibele ya bumi.
Ba Paul Barreira, ba pulofesa ba mitontonkanishishe pa Harvard Medical School kabili abakalamba ba ciputulwa ca buumi pali ili sukulu, batile isukulu lyasalile ukuleta ili sambililo panuma yakusanga abasambi bali ababulisha utulo mukati ka mulungu.
Ici cisambililo icilepwa insa imo nacibimbamo imilimo iyakulanshanya iingi.
Mu cipande cimo muli icikope ca muputule wa kusendamamo, umo abasambi baletinika pa makaapu ya koofi, ifisambililo ne fitabo pakuti bengebwa ifyo kafeni no lubuuto fibomba elyo nefyo ukubomba kwa lubilo kufulunganishiwa pamulandu wa kubulisha utulo, elyo nobukankala bwa kusendama pa nshita iyapimwa.
Mu cipande cimbi, abasambi balesambilishiwa ifyo ukubulisha utulo panshita iitali kwingalundako ubwafya bwa malwele yaku mutima, situloko, amasakamiko elyo na kansa.
Mapu ye sukulu, notukope utwakulanshanyapo, nato tulakoselesha abasambi ukutontonkanya pafyo babomba cila bushiku.
'natwishiba ukuti tacakacinje imibele ya basambi apopene.
Lelo tulesumina ukuti nabakwata insambu shakufishiba - pamofye ngefyo mwakwata insambu shakwishiba ubwafya bwakusala ukupeepa fwaka bwaba ku buumi bwenu,' efyo ba Prof Czeisler balundilepo.
umubela wa cilumba uwa 'kucesha mukubelenga' eko ucili, efyo balandile, nokulundapo ukutila ifitunshitunshi fya ino nshita elyo nokukusha kwa kupamfiwa ku basambi cipilibula ukuti ukubulisha kwa tulo bwafya ubulekulilakofye.
Ukushininkisha ukukwata utulo utwalinga, utwafikapo, cifwile caba ‘icanso icankama’ ku basambi icakucimfya ukufunshika, ukunaka na masakamiko, efyo balandile - nangufye ukucefyako ukwina, pantu ukubulisha utulo kulalenga bongobongo ilecepelwa ifyakulya, nokulenga ukuti abasambi lyonse baleumfwa insala.
Raymond So, uuli ne myaka 19 uwaku Californian uulesambilila ifisambililo fya chemical na physical biology, ewayafwilisheko ba Professor Czeisler ukupanga ici cisambililo, panuma yaku sambililako icisambililo cabo cimo uyu mwaka wapwile mu mwaka wakwe uwacimo pa Harvard.
Batile ici cisambililo calishibula amenso yabo nokubakoselesha ukufwaisha ukubikako icisambililo cabasambi bonse pa sukulu.
Ulutampulo lwakonkapo, balesubila ukuti, ukwipusha abasambi banse abalepwisha amasambililo ukuti bengasambililako icisambililo camusango uyu ilyo tabalaingila mu twampani umwafula ukucimfyanya.
Ba Prof Czeisler bakoseleshe ukuti abasambi balingile ukutontonkanya pa kubika alamu iyakubebukisha ukuya mukusendama, pamofye nenshita yakubuukilapo, nokwishiba amasanso ayaba mu ‘lubuto lwa buluu’ ulufuma ku fyakutamba elyo namalaiti ya LED, icingafulunganya imibele ya nshita yabuntu, nokulenga ukukwata amafya yakusendama.
Livingston 1 - 0 Rangers: Akakato kakwa Menga kabwesha abantu bakwa Gerrard panshi
Ba Rangers ebacimfiwe nakabili ku cibansa cabene ilyo akakato kakwa Dolly Menga kaishilefulunganya ibumba ilishaikatene ilyakwa Steven Gerrard nokucimfiwa 1-0 pa Livingston.
Ibumba lyaku Ibrox lilafwaisha ukucimfya kwakubalilapo munshila yabo ukutendekafye ilyo bacimfishe 4-1 pa St. Johnsone mu mweshi wa Kabengele-Kakalamba, lelo ibumba lyakwa Gary Holt elyaletele ubwafya kukucimfya kwa cibili ukwe bumba lyakwa Gerrard mu mangalo 18 ngo mukalamba we bumba ukuleka ibumba lyakwe ukuba notukato 8 kunuma ya ntungulushi sha Ladbrokes Premiership ba Hearts.
Menga aingishe akakato ilyo kwashelefye amamineti 7 ukufika pakati ka bwangalo elyo ibumba lyaba Rangers ilishakwatishe amaka talyalemoneka ukuti kuti lyabasanga.
Ilyo ba Rangers nomba babwelela pa cifulo calenga 6, ba Livingston banina ukuya pa 3 panuma yaba Hibernian mukupusana kwa tukato.

Almanac: Kapanga wa Geiger Counter
Nomba ibuula ukufuma mwipepala lyesu ilya "Sunday Morning" ilileitwa Almanac: pa 30 Sepitemba, 1882, apapita imyaka 136 ilelo, no KUPENDA ... ubushiku ubo katukuta wa sayanshi Johannes Wilhelm "Hans" Geiger afyelwepo mu calo ca Germany.
Geiger ewapangile inshila yakwishibiliko nokupima radioactivity, icintu icalengele ukufika mukupangwa kwa cibombelo icitwa Geiger Counter.
Ishintililo lya butukuto bwa sayanshi ukutendeka ilyo capangilwe, Geiger Counter aishileba kabili nge shintililo lya lutambi, pamo nga mu bunkolanya bwamu mwaka wa 1950 ubwa "Bells of Coronado," umwasangilwe intukushi sha sayanshi shimo apali na Roy Rogers elyo na Dale Evans:
Umuntu: "Nicinshi ico cine kanshi?"
Rogers: "Nici Geiger Counter, icibomfiwa mukupima radioactivity iisangwa mu mabwe yamo, pamo nga uranium.
Ngawabika utu utwakumfwilako mu matwi, kuti waumfwa amaka yama atomu ayali mu mabwe ayapangwa na radioactivity iilimo mukati."
Evans: "Ninshi uletila, elyo cipangilwe!"
"Hans" Geiger afwile mu mwaka wa 1945, ilyo kwashelefye inshiku ishinono ukuti akwaninshie imyaka yakufyalwa 63.
Lelo icibombelo icainikwako ishina lyakwe cena epo cicili.
Umuti uupya uwakucingilila ku bulwele bwa kansa kuti wafundisha ubucingo bwa mubili 'ukumona' amaselo ya kansa
Umuti uupya uwakucingilila ku bulwele bwa kansa kuti wafundisha ubucingo bwa mubili 'ukumona' amaselo ya kansa nokuyepaya
Umuti wa bucingo wafundisha ubucingo bwa mubili ukwishiba amaselo ya kansa nge nshila yabundapishi
Iyi nshila ilebimbwamo ukusenda amaselo ya bucingo bwa mubili ukufuma ku mulwele, nokuyacinja mu labu
Lyena kuti 'yamona' puloteni iyaseeka mu malwele ya kansa ayengi kabili nokuyabwekesha mumubili
Umuti wakufwailisha ulelangisha isubilo mu balwele abakwata imisango ya kansa iyalekanalekana.
Namayo umo uwapeelwe uyu muti wa bucingo, uufundisha ubucingo bwa mubili ukwishiba amaselo ya kansa, apapilefye ifyo kansa yakwe iyaku fisansala fya mani yapwilepa myeshi ukucila pali 18.
Iyi nshila ilebimbwamo ukusenda amaselo ya bucingo bwa mubili ukufuma ku mulwele, nokuyacinja mu labolatole pakuti yenga "mona" puloteni iyaseeka mu misango ya kansa iingi iitwa HER2,elyo kabili nokuyabwekeshamo mu mubili.
Ba Professor Jay Berzofsky, abaku US National Cancer Institute mu Bethesda, Maryland, batile: "Insebo shesu shilelangisha ukuti tuli nesubilo lyakukwata umuti wa bucingo uusuma nganshi."
Kansa ya HER2 "eitungulula imisango ya kansa iingi," ukubikapo na kansa yaku mabele, ku fisansala fya mani, kuli ba pwapwa neya mumatumbo, efyalondolwele ba Prof Berzofsky.
Umusango umo wine uwakusenda amaselo ya bucingo bwa mubili ukufuma ku balwele no "kuyafundisha" ifyakusansa amaselo ya kansa walibombapo mukundapa umusango wa bulwele bwamu bumfyompo ubwitwa leukaemia.

Kanye West aliwelwa mu studyo mukwimba kwakwe ukwapa Cibelushi panshita ya Saturday Night Live panuma yakwimba sana ilyo aletasha Kateeka wa calo ca U.S. Donald Trump nokutila akeminako mukusala kwamu 2020.

Cilifye, ngacakuti ukupatulula kwa mitundu calinsakamika ngakale nafuma mu calo ca America," efyo alandile.

Bacilatila, 'wiya kuntanshi ninshi naufwala ako kasote.'
Nabancusha sana!
Elyo kabili bacialtila ndesangwa mu ncende iyabunda," efyo alandile, ukulingana naba Washington Examiner.

Esheniko icitemwiko."

West aletelwefye mukucelwa ngo wakupyanikisha pali kemba Ariana Grande, uwo cibusa wakwe umwaume, uuli ni kemba Mac Miller afwile inshiku ishinono ishapitilepo.
West alisungusha abengi ilyo aimbile ulwimbo lwakutila I Love it, ninshi nafwala nga Perrier Bottle.

Lelo uutekesha pulogilamu yabulangisho Karen Hunter alembele pa Twitter nokutila West "alangishefye fintu aba elyo neci cilifye bwino sana."
"Lelo ndesala UKUKANA lambula umuntu umo (ukupitila mukushitako inyimbo shakwe nangu ifyakufwala nangu ukutungilila "ukutukuta" kwakwe) untu njishibe ukuti alesenda nokulanda ifintu ifili no busanso ku ncende yendi.
Ali umuntungwa.
Cimo cinefye naifwe," efyo alundilepo.
Ilyo ubu bulangisho tabulabako, uyu kemba alandile pa Twitter ukutila nacinja ishina, nokutila nomba ali "muntu uwaleitwa kale nga Kanye West."

Kangala wa bunkolanya bwa Game of Thrones Kit Harington akalipa sana pa bantu ababa no mubela wakususha banamayo
Kit Harington aishibikwa bwino ku mulimo wakwe uwakupilibula ulupanga nga Jon Snow mu bunkolanya bwa mpasase sha kale ubwaba HBO ubwitwa Game of Thrones.
Lelo uyu kangala wabunkolanya, uuli ne maka 31, nakalipa sana pamubele wa misuula uwakwa macho hero, nokutila uku kutambisha kwapa fitunshitunshi kulepilibula ukuti abalumendo bafwile baba abashupa pakuti bengacindikwa.
Mukulanda kwakwe kuli ba Sunday Times Culture, Kit aletontonkanya ukuti ifintu fimo nafilubana' elyo alefwaisha nokwishiba ifyakupwisha ici icimusango cakussusha abanakashi munshita ino iya #MeToo.
Kit, uwo nombalinefye aupile umuntu untu bangala nankwe mu bunkolanya bwa Game of Thrones Rose Leslie, nao uuli ne myaka 31, atile aleumfwa ukuti 'alingile ukubombesha' pakulolesha pali ubu bwafya.
'Ndeyumfwa palwandi, ukuti ndingile ukubombesha, pali ino nshita - nipesa apo twalufyaninshisha pamulandu wa maka yesu nga baume?,' efyo alandile.
'Nifinshi ifyo tufundisha abaume ilyo balekula, pamulandu wa bwafya ubo tulemona pali ino nshita?'
Kit atile umulabasa wa fikope ewaleta ubwafya bwakufula kwa misango ya mucushisha wa baume pamulandu wa kufula kwa baume abatambishiwapo mubunkalwe.
Akonkenyepo ukutila: 'Nifinshi ifyo twafyalwa nafyo kabili nifinshi ifyo tusambilila?
Ifyo tusambilishiwa pa TV, namu misebo, efilenga abalumendo ukuyumfwa ukuti balingile ukuba ifi pakuti bengetwa abaume?
Ndetontonkanya ukuti ili elipusho limo ilikalamba sana mu nshita yesu - kuti twacinja sha uyu mubela?
Pantu icishinkafye kuli fimo ifyalubana ku bana abalumendo.'
Muli uku kulanshanya kabili asumine ukuti takakonkanyepo ukupanga ubunkolanya bwakubwekeshapo nangu ubwakupangila limo ubwa Game of Thrones ilyo ubutantiko ubulipo bukapwa mu lusuba ululekonkapo, kabili atile ‘nafileka ifyakwangala no bulwi na ma hosi'.

Akashishi ka HIV/Aids: Icalo ca China catila ukwambula kwa kashishi ukupya kwafika pali 14%
Icalo ca China nacilanda pakutoloka kwa cipendo ca bekala calo abaleikala na kashishi ka HIV na AIDS ukufika kuli 14%.
Abantu ukucila pa cipendo ca 820,000 ebo cikumine mu calo, efilandile abakalamba balolesha kufya bumi.
Icipendo ukufika kuli 40,000 ica kwambula ukupya ecalandilwe muli koota ya cibili iya mwaka wa 2018 yeka.
Abantu abengi abambwile bayambwilile ukupitila mu kulungana, ukupusanako nefyo cali kunuma.
Munshiku shakunuma, ukusabankana kwa kashishi ka HIV mu calo ca China ilingi kwalecitika ukupitila mu kupeleshanya kwa mulopa.
Lelo impendwa ya bantu abaleyambula HIV muli uyu musango nomba naibweshiwa ukufika mupepi na ziro, ifi efyalandile ababombela kufya bumi pa kulongana ukwali mu Yunnan Provinsi.
Ukupashanya ku myaka yakunuma, nangu cibefyo, impendwa ya bantu abali nakashishi ka HIV na Aids mu China nainininako pamulu ne cipendo ca 100,000.
Ukwambula kwa kashishi ka HIV ukupitila mu kulungana mulandu uwakakata sana mu China umwaba abantu abengi abo abengapanga icupo no musango wa muntu uuli onse (LGBT).
Ukulungana no mwaume munobe nangu no mwanakashi munobe calisushiwe mu China mu 1997, lelo ukusushiwa kwa ba LGBT kushimikwe ukuti nakubipisha.
Pamulandu wa mubela wa calo uwakucindika intambi ne fikomo, amasambililo yasanga ukuti 70-90% iyabaume abolungana na baume babiye kukulekelesha bakopa abanakashi.
Ukusalangana ukwingi ukwakashishi kucitika pamulandu wakubulisha ubucingo ubwafikapo muli ubu bwampano.
Ukutendeka mu mwaka wa 2003, ubuteeko bwa calo ca China bwalilaile ukupeela abekala calo bonse umuti wa kashishi ka HIV ngo musango wakucimfishamo ubu bwafya.
Ba Maxine Waters bakana ukuti ilyashi ilifumine ilyaba GOP senator' lilesalanganya 'ubufi bwabusanso' na 'malyashi ya mutunganya'
Abeminishi ba calo ca U.S. ba Rep. Maxine Waters pa Cibelushi ebasushishe umutunganya uwakuti membala wa babomfi babo alibika ilyashi lya bantu batatu ama Republican senators ba calo ca U.S. pa mabuula yakwa uyu shimafunde ayapa Wikipedia.
Uyu Democrat waku Los Angeles atile uyu mutunganya walepangwa na "abaku kuboko kwaku kulyo" bakasabankanya bafya mitekele elyo nama webusaiti.
"Ifyabufi, ubufi ubwine-bwine, ubufi ubwafiita fititi," efyalandile ba Waters mu mashiwi yabo ayapa Twitter.
Ilyashi ilyasalanganishiwe lyashimikwe ukubamo utweyala twa mayanda nama foni namba yaba U.S. Sens. ba Lindsey Graham abaku South Carolina, ba Mike Lee naba Orrin Hatch, bonse babili abaku Utah.
Ili lyashi lyamonekele pa intaneti pali Cine, ilyabikilwepo no muntu uushaishibikwe bwino pa Capitol Hill panshita kwali ukulubulula kwaba Senate mu mulandu wa mutunganya wakufwaya ukulunganya kumaka uwa abo abasalwa ku Supreme Court ba Brett Kavanaugh.
Ili lyashi lyasalangene panuma ninshi ba senator batatu nabapwa ukulubulwisha ba Kavanaugh.
Ama webusaiti yaba Conservative pamo nga Gateway Pundit na RedState balandile ukuti IP address iyalelondolola uwatumine ifi yasuntinkanishiwe ne ofeshi lyaba Waters kabili yasalangenye ilyashi pa mubomfi waba Waters, efyo ipepapala lya Hill lyalandile.
"Uyu mutunganya uwabula ukushininkisha bufi ubwabipisha kabili ubwafita fititi, efyalandile ba Waters.
"Umubomfi wandi - untu mufulunganishishe ifishibilo, ilyashi lyapalwakwe, elyo nobucingo pamulandu waubu bucenjeshi no mutunganya wabufi - mucishinkafye tewasalangenye ili lyashi.
"Uyu mutunganya uwabula ukushininkisha bufi ubwabipisha kabili ubwafita fititi.
Amashiwi yaba Waters mukwangufayanya yalisushiwa nabantu abengi pa intaneti, ukubikapofye na kalemba we lyashi lyaku White House Ari Fleischer.
"Uku kukana kwakufulwa," efyo Fleischer alembele.
"Ici cilepilibula ukutila takwete umutima wakuba membala wa Nganda ya Mafunde.
Ilyo umuntu atunganishiwa icintu ico tacitile, talingile ukufulwa.
Talingile ukukalipa kwakuipokolola.
Talingile kwipusha ico uulemutunganaya emininepo.
Afwilefye ukuba uwafuuka kabili uwatekanya."
Ba Fleischer baleesha ukupashanya ukufulwa kwaba Waters nokususha kwaba Democrats ukukwa Judge Kavanaugh, uwatunganishiwe nabamususha ukuti ali uwafulwa sana panshita ya kulubulula kwa pali Cine.
Ba Omar Navarro, abaleiminina pe tiketi lyama Republican abalefwaya ukufumyapo ba Waters mukusala kwapakati ka temu, nabo balilandapo amashiwi pa Twitter.
"Ici cikulu ngacakuti cacishinka," efyo baposele pa Twitter.
Mu mashiwi yabo, ba Waters batile iofeshi lyabo nalicebusha "abo cikumine elyo nabo ababombela kukufikilisha kwa mafunde pamulandu wa uyu mutunganya wa buntala-misoka.
"Tukashininkisha ukuti bantala-misoka basangwa," efyo balandile, "elyo kabili nokutila bakapelwa imilandu pa milimo yabo iyabonaushi kabili iya busanso ku muntu uuli onse pamo nababomfi babo."
Ukupituluka muli Johnny English Kwabwela Nakabili - ubwangalo bwa Rowan Atkinson ubwakwesha mukusekesha
Cili nomba ngo lutambi ukusanaga ifilepala kuli Brexit mu bunkolanya bonse ubupya ubukwetemo ilyashi lyaku Britain neci ecilecitika kuli ubu bunkolanya bwakusekesha ubupya ubuleitwa Johnny English action-comedy spoof franchise - ubwatendeke mu mwaka wa 2003 na Johnny English elyo nokwisabwela nakabili mu mwaka wa 2011 peshina lya Johnny English Reborn.
Bushe kuti bwaleta ukususha kwakusekesha pa lyashi lyafyo twaba no bwafya nge calo ukulosha ku lyashi lye shuko ilya kutuma ifipe fyesu kunse ya calo?
Mu musango uuli onse Johnny English uwa menso ayatumbuka, icinso icabula ukushininkana alibukulusha icitupa cakwe pamuku wa cibili uwakutendeka ukupanga ifyakusekesha - ishina ililelangisha ukuti aliipelesha ukucila fyonse ukuti ni umo uulebomba ifyakusekesha ifyapangilwa incende ishishilanda Icisungu ishipanga ifyabunkolanya.
Muntu umo uubomfya akabuwelewele kankama kamo akakusekesha ukusanshamo ifyakusekesha ifyabamo bu Kaceceta bunono, mukupashanya Mr Bean namumusango umbi ukupalako ulya muntu uulelundako ishiwi ku lwimbo lwa Chariots of Fire pakusefya kwa kwiswila kwa London 2012 Olympics.
Kabili pakubala ashintilile pamuntu uwaleenda sana kabili umwaume wa calo conse Atkinson uwalesangwa mu bunkolanya ubwalabwa pali ino nshita ubwaleleta ifishibisho fya Barclaycard TV, uwalesha amafya monse umo alepita.
Muliko icintu cimo nangu fibili ifiweme mu mipekanishishe ya bunkolanya ubupya ubwa JE.
Naumfwile bwino ukumona Johnny English aleya ku ndeke ya helikopita ninshi nafwala suti yamunshita shakale iya nkondo ninshi namapindo yandeke yalemukumyako panono ku cimpompo cakwe.
Icabupe cakwa Atkinson icakwangala ifyakusekesha camoneka, lelo inshita shimo ifyakusekesha filamoneka ukucepelwa amaka napansita shimo ukucila mucipimo, makamaka ilyo ubunkolanya “ubwakuposako amano” pamo nga 007 na Mission Impossible umulesangwa nomba ifyakusekesha ngefyakuwamishako
Ifyakusekesha ilingiline fimoneka ngefipangilwa abaice ukucila abakalamba, elyo mu fingi ifipitamo Johnny English tamuba utwakushamo tumbi utusuma pamo ngeficitika mu bunkolanya bwakwa Atkinson ilyo angala pa cifulo cakwa Bean.
Ilyashi ililelandwapo nomba mu mwaka lyakuti Great Britain ili mu bwafya ubwakakata.
Ntalamisoka wapa intaneti naingila mu netiweki yafyankama iya intaneti ifya nengu sha calo ca Britain, nokusokolola ifishinka fya beminishi ba calo ca Britain bonse abasalangana mu milimo, neci calisungusha umuntu uwali pancito pali iyi nshita - umulimo uunono sana kuli Kevin Eldon.
Ici cili icintu icakosa nganshi kuli ntungulushi nkalamba (prime minister) iyakwatisha icilumba kabili iili mu bwafya, iilecula kukucepelwa kwa maka ya butungulushi bwaiko nokwishibikwa kwa mu mashiwi ya mitekele: Ba Emma Thompson balibomba bwino mukwangala pa cifulo cakwa quasi-Teresa-May lelo tamuli ifingi mu butantiko bwa mashiwi ya bunkolanya ifyakubombelapo.
Ba mpandamamo babo babebele ukuti epo imilimo shonse isha nengu nashikatwako, balingile ukubwesha bonse abaleka imilimo.
Neci cilepilibula ukubikako na Johnny English wine uwacimfulunganya, uulebomba nomba ngo mukalamba we sukulu limo, lelo alepeela ifisamililo ifikumine ifyo umuntu engabomba ukwabula ukwishibikwa: icakusekesha cimo apa, ilyo English alesambilisha amasambililo ya nengu pa School of Rock.
English afyushiwa nokutwalwa ku Whitehall ku kukumana kwa mukampampa elyo kabili akumana nowali kale umunankwe uwo bacula nankwe Bough, icifulo kabili icasendwa na Ben Miller.
Bough pali ino nshita nomba alyupa, nokubikwa pamo na umukalamba wa cibwato capanshi, namayo uwaishibikwa sana icifulo ico Vicki Pepperdine alemoneka uwapwa sana.
Kanshi ifintu ifishingapatulwa mukulola kukulenga ifintu fibipe mu Fyankama fyakwa Namfumu (Her Majesty's Secret Service) nafibwela mu maka nokukumanya Ophelia Bulletova umukashana uwamingalato mu cifulo cakwa Olga Kurylenko.
Kulubali lumbi, intungulushi nkalamba (prime minister) alewila mu citeyo icabusanso icamuntu uubombela kufitunshitunshi uwakwatisha indalama uuletila kuti apwisha amacushi ya calo ca Britain ayakumine ifitunshitunshi: uwakutiinya Jason Volta, icifulo icasendelwe na Jake Lacy.
Ubulendo bakwa English na Bough ubwakuifungushanya bwatendeka: ukuipanga ngabakapeela wafyakulya, basonteka umuli kwituuka lyakulilamo ilyaci French; baleta impasase ilyo bafyuka ukubomfya ubwato bwa Volta's luxury yacht; elyo English aleta impasase ilyo aesha ukubomfya utwakumfwilako utwa Virtual Reality pakuti eshibe bwino ifyo ing’anda ya Volta yapangwa.
Ifyakwiminikila fyonse fyafumishiwa pakuti ukutamba kwakushalikisha kucitwe, lelo nangu bwingawamisha nokusekesha muli uyu musango, ifikumine abaice emo ficili mu lyashi lyonse.
Ifintu ifyalingako panono.
Elyo pamofye ngama filimu yakwa Johnny English ayengi nalitontonkanya ukuti: bushe utwampani twa mafilimu utwaku Britain tekuti tupele Rowan Atkinson ukwangalila pa cifulo icingamulenga abomfya bwino italanta ilyo akwata?
Icipani ca Labour cakana ukuti cilepanga ukuti abena Britain bakulabomba inshiku 4 mu mulungu elyo bafola indalama sha nshiku 5.
Icipani caba Jeremy Corbyn ica Labour ciletontonkanya pa mapange ayakalenga abena Britain bakalebomba inshiku 4 mu mulungu - lelo ukulafola indalama sha nshiku 5.
Icipani cashimikwe ukuti cilefwaya abakalamba ba twampani balefumya indalama ishapangwa ukupitila mu milimo ya fitunshitunshi (AI) nokushipeela ku babomfi ukupitila mukubapeelako ubushiku nabumbi ubwakutusha.
Ici cikalenga ababomfi ukulakwata inshiku shitatu ishakutusha pampela ya mulungu - lelo ukulafola indalama shimo shine.
Abatupelako ilyashi batile aya mapange kuti ‘yalinga’ mu bwanshiko bwandalama na mapange yakwalula icalo mukuwamisha ababomfi imikalile.
Ukwalukila ku mulungu wa nshiku 4 kwalitungililwa na kabungwe ka milimo aka Trades Union Congress ngo musango wakuti ababomfi bomfweko bwino munshita ya kulubana kwa ndalama.
Umukalamba umo uwamu cipani ca Labour aebele ipepala lya Sunday Times ukutila: 'Ukupituluka kwa muli ici cikomo kuleenekelwa ukubilishiwa ilyo umwaka taulapwa.
'Tacakacitike munshita iinono lelo umulungu wa nshiku shakubomba 4 emapange ayalelolenkana no bwanshiko bwa cipani ubwakuwamya imikalile yababomfi pamofye na mapange yakuwamya amakwebo ya calo.'
Icipani ca Labour tecikabalilapo ukufikilisha aya mapange, lintu ne Cipani ca Green naco calilaile umulungu wamilimo uwa nshiku 4 panshita yakongola ba kasala mukusala kwa cinkumbawile mu mwaka wa 2017.
Nangu cibefyo, aya mapange tayatungililwa umupwilapo ne Cipani ca Labour.
Uulandilako Icipani ca Labour Party atile: 'Umulungu wakubomba inshiku 4 tecikomo ca cipani elyo kabili taciletontonkanishiwapo ne cipani.'
Ba Shadow Chancellor abali niba John McDonnell babomfeshe ukulongana kwa cipani ca Labour ukwa uyu mulungu ukubukulushishamo icimonwa cabo icakuwaminisha amaka ya ndalama na makwebo.
Ba McDonnell batile bali abaipelesha sana ukupokolola amaka ukufuma ku ‘bakalamba ba milimo ababula ubuyo’ elyo na 'abafwaya ukusombola ifingi' mu twampani utubomba imilimo yabekala calo.
Amapange yaba chancellor ba shadow kabili yalepilibula ukuti abakwatamo amasheya mu twampani twa menshi limbi tekuti babwesulushe indalama shabo shonse pantu ubuteeko bwa cipani ca Labour kuti ‘bwasusaulamo’ indalama shimo pamilandu ya filubo fimo ifyo bacitile.

Ba Lindsey Graham, ba John Kennedy baeba "60 Minutes" ngacakuti ukufwailisha kwaba FBI pamulandu waba Kavanaugh kuti kwacinja amalangulushi yabo
Ukufwailisha kwaba FBI pa mutunganya waba Judge Brett Kavanaugh nakushingashingishako ukuvota kwakushalikisha pakusalwa kwabo ukwaku cilye ca Supreme Court pamulungu umo, elyo nacileta ne lipusho lyakumona ngacakuti ifyasangwa naba kafwailisha ba milandu kuti fyafulunganya amalangulushi yama senator ama Republican ukuti bafumyemo ukutungilila kwabo.

"Nomuntufye onse untu engalumbula tekuti ashininkishe uyu mulandu.
Papita nomba imyaka 36.
Nshilemonapo ifipya ifili fyonse ifilecinja."
Bushe Global Citizen Festival nicinshi elyo kabili bushe Calibombapo Ifili Fyonse Mukucefyako Ubupina?
Pa Cibelushi mu New York mukaba ukwimba kwa Global Citizen Festival, ukwimba kwa cila mwaka uko ukusangwa bakemba abapusanapusana abemba, mukukonkana no mulimo uukulu; ukupwisha ubupina mwisonde.
Uno nomba mwaka walenga 7, kuli uku kwimba kwa Global Citizen Festival kukasangwa amakana ya makumi aya bantu abakaya ku Great Lawn iyaku Central Park tekuya mukumfwafye ukwimba kweka ukwa bakemba pamo nga Janet Jackson, Cardi B na Shawn Mendes, lelo namukuya mukwishibisha abantu pa bukankala bwa uku kwimba ubwakupwisha ubupina ilyo tacilafika mu mwaka wa 2030.
Ukwimba kwa Global Citizen Festival, ukwatendeke mu mwaka wa 2012, kulundulula kwa Global Poverty Project, ibumba lye sonde lyonse ililesubila ukupwisha ubupina ukupitila mukufusha abantu abaleibimbamo mukulwisha ubupina.
Pakuti mwingapokelela itiketi ilyabula ukulipila (kanofye ngamulefwaya ukushita itiketi lya VIP), abalefwaya ukuyatambako balingile ukupwisha imilimo imo iitantikwe, nangu "imilimo" pamo nga ukuipeleshafye ku mulimo, ukutuma imelo ku ntungulushi ya calo imo, ukutuma foni nangu umulimo uuli onse uwingalenga uyu mulimo wakupwisha ubupina wishibikwe.
Nomba bushe uyu mulimo wa Global Citizen walibombapo ifili fyonse ilyo kwashalafye imyaka 12 iyakufikilisha ifyo watendekele?
Bushe ukupeela abantu amatiketi yalutu aya konsati enshila iyayana iyakupatikisha abantu ukuti bepushishemo ukuti umlimo ubombeke nangu ninshilafye naimbi iya “iyakutinika-tinika pa intaneti” - abantu ukumona kwati pali ifyo balebomba ukupitila mukusaina ukulanda kumo ukwapa intaneti nangu ukutuma ilyashi ukupitila muli ka tweet?
Ukufuma mu 2011, ba Global Citizen batile balilembako “imilimo” ukucila pali 19 milyoni ukufuma ku bacitungilila, ukufwaya ukuti imilimo iingi icitwe.
Balandile ukuti iyi milimo yalyafwilishako ukupatikisha intungulushi sha calo ukubilisha ukuti balelaya indalama ne fikomo fyakubomba ifingafika naku cipendo ca $37 bilyoni ico icingafwilisha abantu ukufika ku cipendo ca 2.25 bilyoni ilyo tacilafika mu mwaka wa 2030.
Mukutampa kwa mwaka wa 2018, ili ibumba lyalandile pa malayo nefishibisho ukufika kuli 390 pamulandu ne milimo yabo, pali ifyo ukufika kuli $10 bilyoni yalikolonganishiwa nokusalanganishiwa.
Ili ibumba lilelanda ukuti indalama ishakolonganishiwapo shalyafwilishako abantu ukufika ku cipendo ca 649 milyoni isonde lyonse.
Amalayo yamo pali aya paliba The Power of Nutrition, umulimo wa bwampano bwa twampani twaku U.K. uwaiminina pa "kwafwilisha abana banono ukukula bwino ukufika apo bengafika," ukulaya ukupeela icalo ca Rwanda indalama $35 milyoni iyakwafwilisha ukupwisha ukucepelwa kwa fyakulya mu calo panuma yakupokelela utumakalata twapa Twitter utuli 4,700 ukufuma ku Bekala Calo be Sonde.
"Nokutungililwa ukufuma ku buteeko bwa calo ca UK, abapeela ubwafwilisho, amabuteeko yamu fyalo, elyo na Bekala Calo bamwi Sonde pamofye nga imwe, kuti twabomba umulimo wakulenga ukubulisha kwafyakulwa kwashalafye ngo mulumbe wakwibikishapofye," abeminishi ba The Power of Nutrition ba Tracey Ullman efyo baebele cinkupiti wa bantu abasangilwe kuli konsati mu London mu mweshi wa Shinde 2018.
Ili bumba kabili lyatile panuma ya milimo ukucila pali 5,000 iyabombelwe ukulomba ubuteeko bwa calo ca U.K. ukuwamya imilele ya banyina nabana babo, ubuteeko bwalibilishe ukupeela indalama kumulimo wakuti Power of Nutrition, uyo uukafika kuli banamayo na bana abali 5 milyoni nobwafwilisho bwa milile isuma.
Mukwasuka ku Mepusho Ayepushi Lyonse (FAQ) pa webusaiti yabo ilyakuti "nifinshi ifilelenga mutontonkanye ukuti kuti twapwisha ubupina ubwabipisha?"
Ba Global Citizen balyaswike nokutila: "Ukuba mulimo uwakosa kabili uwanshita iitali - inshita shimo tulafilwa kabili nokufilwa.
Lelo, pamofye ngo tubungwe twakulwila insambu nakapatulula ka nkanda utwaliko, tukasuka tukacimfye, pantu ilyo twabombela pamo ninshi twakwatisha amaka.

Ubuteeko bwa calo ca US kuti bwabomfya Abashilika bapa Menshi ukuba nge "cakucinga" pakulesha ukwingila kwafipe fyaku Russia - Kalemba wa Buteeko
Umusumba wa Washington "ngacilefwaikwa" kuti wabomfya abashilika ba pamenshi ukulesha ifipe fyaku Russia ukufika mu mishika, ukubikapo naku Middle East, ukulingana ne pepala lya Washington Examiner.
Ba Zinke balandile ukuti ubwampano bwa calo ca Russia na Syria - icimoneke, uko balebombela pa bwite bwa buteeko ubwacishinka - kabepeshofye kakufwailishishamo imishika ya fipe fya maka.
"Ndesubila ukuti ico babelele mu Middle East cakutila balefwaya ukulanshanya pa fipe fya maka ngefyo bacita ku kabanga ka Europe, naku kapinda kaku kulyo aka Europe," efyo balandile.
Elyo, ukulingana no mukalamba wa buteeko, kuliko inshila ishakubombelamo.
"Icalo ca United States calikwata amaka, ukubomfya Abashilika besu abapa Menshi, ukushininkisha ukuti inshila shapali bemba nashisuka, elyo ngacilefwaikwa nokushisala, ukushininkisha ukuti ifipe fyabo tafingile mu mishiika," efyo balandile.
Ba Zinke balelanda ku bantu abasangilwe pa kulongana ukwatekeshiwe naba Consumer Energy Alliance, akabungwe akaita ukuti "ishiwi lyaba kabomfya ba fipe fya maka” mu calo ca US.
Bakonkenyepo ukupashanya imibombele ya musumba wa Washington mukubomba ne calo ca Russia na Iran, nokutila filifye cimo cine.
"Imibombele yafikumine indalama ku Iran na Russia, ili mukufula nangu ukucefyako, ukubomfya bwino nokupyanikishapo ifyamafuta," efyo basosele, mukulosha ku calo ca Russia nga "incenjeshi mu cintu cimo" mukushintililafye pa mafuta ayakufuma ku fintu ifyakale.
Aya mashiwi yaisa panshita iyo ubuteeko bwaba Trump bwaba pakukushako ukutuma kwa gasi ya menshi ku Europe, ukupyana pali Russia, ukusangwako ifintu ifyacipa kuli bakabomfya baku Europe.
Pamulandu wa ici, ubuteeko bwaba Trump, ukubikapo naba Kateeka ba US ba Donald Trump abene, baleesha ukupatikisha icalo ca Germany ukufumamo mumulimo "uushalolamo" uwa Nord Stream 2 pipeline project, uwo ukulingana naba Trump, walengele Moscow yaku Berlin "ukuba abasha."
Umusumba wa Moscow walilanda pa miku iingi ukutila umulimo wa ndalama $11 bilyoni uwa Nord Stream 2 pipeline, uuleenekelwa ukulundako kumipaipi iyabako kale iisunga icipendo ca 110 billion cubic meters, umulimo wakulundulula kwa makwebo.

Ba Elizabeth Warren "Bakapitulukamo Bwino Sana" pa Kwiminina mu Kusala kwakwa Kateeka mu 2020, efilandile ba Senator baku Massachusetts
Ba Senator baku Massachusetts ba Elizabeth Warren pa Cibelushi batile balingile “ukutontonkanyapo sana” pa kwiminina pa kusalwa nga kateeka panuma yakusala kwa pakati ka temu.
Panshita ya kulongana kwamu cikulwa camu musumba wa Holyoke, Massachusetts, ba Warren bashininkishe ukuti baletontonkanyapo pa kwimininako muli uku kusala.
"Ninshita ya banamayo besu iyakuya ku musumba wa Washington nokuyawamya ubuteeko ubwaonaika neci cilepilibula namayo ukuba pa butungulushi bwa pamulu," efyo balandile, ukulingana ne pepala lya The Hill.
"Panuma ya bushiku bwapa 6 Novemba, nkatendeka ukutontonkanyapo pa kwiminina pa kusalwa nga kateeka."
Ba Warren balipimine ba Kateeka ba Donald Trump panshita yakulongana kwamu cikulwa camu musumba, nokutila "baletwala icalo kuntunga iyalubana.
