Ba Sarah Palin balanda pali PTSD yakwa Track Palin pa kulongana kwaba Donald Trump
Track Palin, uuli ne myaka 26, apwile umwaka umo mu Iraq panuma yakulembesha Sepitemba.
Aliketwe nokupelwa umulandu wa mutitikisha uwacitike pa bushiku bwa pali Cimo ubushiku.
"Ifyo umwana wandi alepitamo, ifyo alepitamo pakubwela kwakwe, kuti napashanya ku ndupwa shimbi ishipita mukukankambwa kwa PTSD elyo nokucenwa kumo uko abashilika besu babwela nako," basosele aya mashiwi kwibumba ilyasangilwe pa kulongana kwaba Donald Trump mu Tulsa, Oklahoma.
Ba Palin balandile ukuti ukwikatwa kwa mwana kwali nge "nkalamo mu muputule" nokutila umwana wabo nabashilika bambi, "babwela abacinjako, babwela abakosa imitima, babwela nokutwishika ngacakuti kucili ukucindikwa ngefyo kwaba ukwakuti abashilika banabo, abashilika ba mumulu, nabashilikafye bambi, bapela ku calo cabo."
Aiketwe pali Cimo mu Wasilla, Alaska, nokupeelwa umulandu wamutitikisha ku mwanakashi, ukupumfyanya insebo sha mutitikisha elyo nokukwata icanso ca bulwi ninshi nakolwa, ukulingana na mashiwi yaba Dan Bennett, abalandilako Impuka yaba Kapokola mu Wasilla.
Imisumba 18, D.C. yatungilila ukususha kwa cikomo icipya icabucingo bwa bantu
Imisumba 18 pamo ne Boma lya Columbia baletungilila ukususha kwa cikomo icipya mu calo ca U.S. icliekanya ukupokelela nokucingilila abantu abalebutuka umutitikisha wabantala-misoka nangu uwamu mayanda.
Abeminishi ukufuma mu misumba 18 pamo ne boma limo balembele amashiwi ayaleitwa friend-of-the-court pali Cisano mu musumba wa Washington pakutungilila umuntu uulefwaya ukucingililwa uulesusha ici cikomo, efyalandile ba NBC News.
Ishina lyonse ilyakwa kailishanya mu mulandu waba Grace v. Sessions untu akabungwe ka American Civil Liberties Union kalembele mu mweshi wa Kasaka-ntobo ukuilishanya pa cikomo ca buteeko talisokolwelwe.
Uyu mukashana alandile ukuti cibusa wakwe "nabana bakwe ba memba bebumba lyakwe," balemucusha lelo abakalamba ba calo ca U.S. balimukenye ukwipusha kwakwe ukwakucingililwa mu mweshi wa Julai pa 20.
Asungilwe mu musumba wa Texas.
Bandubulwila ba uyu musumba abaletungilila Grace balondolwele incende ya El Salvador, Honduras na Guatemala, nge ncende ukufuma sana abantu abafwaya ubucingo ku buteeko bwa calo ca U.S., pantu encende umwaba sana amafya ya mutitikisha wa bantalamisoka pamo namundupwa.
Icikomo icipya ica calo ca U.S. ica bucingo cabwesulwishe ubusalo bwa mu mwaka wa 2014 ubwapangilwe naba Board of Immigrant Appeals ubwasuminishe abantu abashalembwa abaleingila mu calo ukuti kuti baipusha ubucingo.
Ba Attorney General be Boma lya Columbia ba Karl Racine sbalandile mu mashiwi yabo pali Cisano ukutila icikomo icipya "cilesusha ifunde lya misumba icfyalo ne sonde lyonse ilya makumi ya myaka iyapita."
"Ifunde lya buteeko lifwaya ukuti ukwipusha konse ukwabucingo bwingapingwilwa ukukonkana ne fishinka fimo pamo nefyacitike pakwipusha ubo bucingo, elyo noku kukanya kulepinkana neci cikomo," efyalandile amashiwi ya friend-of-the court.
Ba ndubulwila kabili balandile muli aya mashiwi ukutila ici cikomo icilekanya abaleingila mu calo cilelenga ukuti amakwebo ya calo ca U.S. yafulunganishiwe, nokutila aba bantu kuti baisaba bashimakwebo pamo "nokuleta imilimo iingafwaikwa."
Ba Attorney General Jeff Sessions bakambishe bakapingula ababombela ku baleingila mu calo ukukapela ubucingo kuli abo abalebutuka ku mutitikisha wa buntala-misoka no lukakala lwamu mayanda mu mweshi wa Kapepo-kakalamba.
"Ubucingo bulasangwa kuli abo abafuma mu fyalo fyabo pamulandu wakutitikishiwa nangu ukutinishiwa pamulandu wa mutundu, amapepo, icalo, nangu bu membala mu kabungwe kamo nangu ilangulushi lyapa mitekele ya calo," efyo ba Sessions balandile mu mashiwi yabo ayapa 11 Akapepo-kakalamba ilyo balebilisha ici cikomo.
Ubu bucingo tabwapangilwe ukuti bwingapwisha amafya yonse -- nangufye amafya yonse ayakakata -- ayo abantu bakumanya cila bushiku isonde lyonse.
Ukulwisha ukusanga nokupususha abapusunswike kulekonkanyapo mu Palu ilyo impendwa ya bafwile yalundako
Kuli abo abapuswike, ifintu tafibawamine.
"Cileumfwika icayafya," efyasosele namayo uwamyaka 35 uweshina lya Risa Kusuma, pakutalalika akamwana kakwe akanya pa ncende yakusungilapo abapuswike mu musumba wa busanso uwa Palu.
"Cila nshita motoka yabalwele ileletelapo ifitumbi nafimbi.
Amenshi ayabusaka nayabula."
Abekala calo balemoneka ukulabwelela ku mayanda yabo ayaonaika, ukutolamo ifintu fimo ifibundilwe mu menshi, ukwesha ukusendako ifyo bengasangamo.
Imyanda ya bantu baliceneka elyo ne fipatala, ifyaonaike ne cinkukuma ca maka 7.5, fyaliisula.
Abantu bamo abaceneke, apali na Dwi Haris, uwakontweke inuma no kubeya, baletusha panse ya Cipatala ca Bashilika mu Palu, apo abalwele baleundapilwa panse pamulandu wakukonkanyapo kwa kutenta kwa mushili panuma ya cinkukuma.
Ifilamba fyaiswile mu mesno yakwe ilyo alelondolola ifyacitike ilyo icinkukuma catenseshe umuputule wapantunti yalenga 5 mu hotela umo baleikala no mukashi pamo nomwana.
"Takwali inshita yakuipususha fwebene.
Ndetontonkaya, nalitininkishiwe mu fibumba ifyabongoloka," Efyo Haris aebele ba Associated Press, ukulundapo ukutila ulupwa lwakwe lwali mu tauni ku bwing.
"Naumfwile umukashi wandi alepunda, elyo pali tondolo.
Nshishibe icacitike kuli wene no mwana wandi.
Ndesubila ukuti balifye umutende."
Umwiminishi wa calo ca U.S. atunganya icalo ca China ukuba 'nomucushisha' ukubomfya 'ukusabankanya ukwayafya'
Panuma fye ya mulungu umo ukufuma apo ipepala lye lyashi ilya calo ca China lyasabankenye amakwebo mwi papela lya calo ca U.S. ukulanda pa fisuma ifingaba mu bwampano bwa makwebo pakati ka calo ca U.S. na China, abeminishi ba U.S. ku China batungenye umusumba wa Beijing ukulabomfya amapepala ya calo ca America ukusabankanya ilyashi ilyayafya.
Bakateeka ba calo ca U.S ba Donald Trump pali Citatu iyafumineko balandile pe pepala lye lyashi ilya China Daily nefilundwamo ifya Des Moines Register - ipepala ilishitishiwa sana mu musumba wa Iowa - panuma yakutunganya icalo ca China ukufwaya ukuibimba mu kusala kwamu U.S. congress ukwapa 6 Novemba, umulandu untu icalo ca China cikene.
Umutunganya waba Trump uwakutila umusumba wa Beijing uleesha ukwingila mu kusala kwa calo ca U.S. washininkishe ifyo abakalamba bamo abaku U.S. baebele umulabasa wa Reuters ngo musango uupya untu umusumba wa Washington ulefwaya ukubomfya pakuti ubike ubwafya pa calo ca China.
Nangu cakuti calibafye bwino ifyalo fyakunse ukubika ifyakubilisha fya kusumbula amakwebo mu mapepala ye lyashi, umusumba wa Beijing na Washington ili mu bulwi bwa makwebo ubwayafya ubulengele nokuti imisonko ya fintu ififuma ku calo cimo ukuya kucibiye ulundweko.
Imisonko ya fipe fya China mukutendeka kwa mwaka yabikilweko pakuti ingakuma abashitisha ifipe kunse ya calo mu misumba pamo nga Iowa iyaletungilila icipani caba Trump icama Republican, efilandile abalolesha ku makwebo mu calo ca China.
Ba Terry Branstad, abeminishi ba calo ca U.S. ku China kabili abakokwelepo sana pali bu Governer mu musumba wa Iowa, ukufuma ifyabulimi ifingi ifiya ku China, batile umusumba wa Beijing walilufyenye sana ku babomfi baku American, abalimi elyo nabashimakwebo.
Ba Branstad balembele mulyashi lya malangulushi mwipepala lyapa Sande ilya Des Moines Register, ukutila "Icalo ca China nomba cilelundapo umutitikisha ukupitila mukulasabankanya amashiwi ya makwebo ayayafya mu mapepala yesu ayabula ukulipila."
"Ukupitila mu kusabankanya kwa aya makwebo yabo ayayafya, ubuteeko bwa calo ca China buleileta pa bwelu ku maisosele ayabuntungwa aya calo ca America namapepala ya lutu ilyo babika ukusabankanya kwa makwebo ukwakulipilila mwipepala lya Des Moines Register," efyo ba Branstad balembele.
"Mukupashanya kuli ifi, pa tebulo lye lyashi mu musebo umo muno mu Beijing, mulesanga amashiwi yakususha ayanono kabili tamwamonepo amashiwi yabupusano ayo abena China bengakwata pamulandu wa buyo bwa makwebo ya calo ca China ayalemoneka ukubwelela panshi, neci nipamulandu wakuti imilabasa mu China yaikatililwa ne cipani ca Chinese Communist Party," efyo balembele.
Balundilepo nokutila "ipepala limo ilyaishibikwa sana mu China lyalikana ukusabankanya" ilyashi lyabo, nangu cakuti tabalumbwile ilyo ipepala lye lyashi.
Ama Republican Balepatulula Banamayo Abalesala Mukutangilila Ukusala kwa Pakati ka Temu Pamulandu wa Lyashi lyaba Kavanaugh, Efisokele Abapituluka mu lyashi
Panshita iyo ama Republican abengi baletungilila uusalilwe ku Supreme Court Brett Kavanaugh uutunganishiwe mu malyashi ayakufwaya ukucenda umwanakashi kumaka, abapituluka mu malyashi batile kukaba ukusanswa nganshi, makamaka kuli banamayo, panshita ya kusala ukuleisa ukwapakati ka temu.
Amalangulushi ayashingulwike uyu mulandu yali sana pamulu, elyo nama Republican abengi bashimikwe ukutila bena nabaipekanya kale ukusuminisha kuli uku kusala.
Ifyo fintu tekuti fibweseshiwe kunuma," ba Grant Reeher, abasambilisha pafya mitekele pa sukulu lya Maxwell pa Syracuse University baebele ipepala lye lyashi ilya The Hill mu lyashi ilyalembelwe pa Cibelushi.
Ba Reeher batile baletwishika ukuti ukupatikisha kwapakushalikisha ukwaba Senator Jeff Flake (R-Arizona) ukuti kube ukufwailisha kwaba FBI kuti kwabweshako icipyu cabakasala abafulilwe.
"Banamayo tabakalabe ifyacitike mailo yafumineko - tabakacilabe mailo ileisa kabili tabakacilabe mu mweshi wa Novemba," ba Karine Jean-Pierre, bampandamano mukalamba kabili abalandilako ibumba lya buyantanshi ilitwa MoveOn balandile aya mashiwi pali Cisano, ukulingana nepepala lye lyashi ilya Washington, D.C.
Pali Cisano ulucelo, bakailishanya balepunda aya mashiwi "Novemba ileisa!" ilyo baleilishanya mu cikulwa ca Senate panshita iyo ama Republican abaletungulula Akabungwe ka Bupingushi basalile ukuya pantanshi no kusalwa kwaba Kavanaugh nangu cakuti pali ubunte bwaba Dr. Christine Blasey Ford, efyalandile ba Mic.
"Umupatikisha no kusamwa kwa ma Democrat kuli nokufuma mu fyalembwa," ba Stu Rothenberg, abapituluka mu malyashi abashaba mu cipani icili conse, efyo baebele ipepala lya lyashi ilyapa intaneti.
"Abantu baletila nacicilamio; ici cishinka.
Lelo kuti cacilanapo, makamaka pali banamayo nemisepela abali ni bakasala aba muncende shama komboni, abali ne myaka 18 ukufika pali 29, abakuti nangu cakuti tabatemenwe kateeka, ilingiline tabavotako."
Nangufye ilyo Ford talapela ubunte bwapalwala ukulanda pa mutunganya wakwe uwakufwaya ukucendwa nabasalilwe ku Supreme Court, abapituluka mu malyashi batile kuti kwaba ukusanswa ngacakuti ama Republicans bapatikisha ukusuminisha.
"Ici nacisanguka ubwafya ubukulu kuli ba GOP," efyalandile ba Michael Steele, abali bakumupando kale mu Republican National Committee, mukutendeka kwa uyu mulungu, ukulingana naba NBC News.
"Tacilifye pa mulandu wa kusala kwa komiti nangu ukuti bushe ba Kavanaugh babikwe pa benci, nacikuma kabili no musango untu ama Republicans basendelemo ili lyashi elyo nefyo babombele noyo namayo," Ba Guy Cecil, abakalamba be bumba lya Priorities USA, ibumba ilyafwilishako ukusala ama Democrat, ebalandile ifi ku mulabasa we lyashi.
Nangu cibefyo, abena America balemoneka abapatulukana pamulandu wa bunte bwa kwa Ford na Kavanaugh elyo abengi baletungilila Kavanaugh.
Ukufwailisha ukupya ukufuma ku YouGov kulangile ukuti 41 pesenti yabaleyasuka nabasumina mumupwilapo nangu eyefilyako ku bunte bwakwa Ford, elyo 35 pesenti nabo batile balesumina mumupwilapo nangu eyefilyako ku bunte bwakwa Kavanaugh.
Mukulundapo, 38 pesenti batile baletontonkanya ukutila Kavanaugh alilanda ifyabufi mu bunte bwakwe, elyo abali 30 pesenti nabo balandile cimo cine ku bunte bwakwa Ford.
Panuma yakupatikisha kwaba Flake, ba FIBI pali ino nshita balefwailisha uu mutunganya uwalandile Ford pamo no muntu umbi nao uwaletele umutunganya, Deborah Ramirez, Efyalandile ipepala lya Guardian.
Ba Ford bapele ubunte ku kabungwe ka Senate Judiciary Committee ilyo balapile uyu mulungu wapwile ukutila ba Kavanaugh balibasanshile ninshi nabakolwa ilyo balifye ne maka 17.
Ba Ramirez nabo batile abasalilwe ukuya ku Supreme Court balibalangishe ifyamfwalo ifyafisama ilyo bali pa kusefya lintu balesambilila pe sukulu lya Yale mu myaka yamuma 1980.
Uwapangile akasolobelo ka Intaneti aketwa World Wide Web Alepekanya Ukupanga Akasolobelo ka Intanenti kambi Akengapyanina pali Google na Facebook
Tim Berners-Lee, uwapangile World Wide Web, alatendeka akasolobelo kambi akalemoneka ukuti kuti kacimfya Facebook, Amazon na Google.
Akasolobelo akapya aka uyu muntu uwaishibisha ifya tekinoloji, akaleitwa Inrupt, kampani akapya akalebombela pa kasolobelo kakwa Berners-Lee akeshina lya Solid.
Akasolobelo ka Solid kalasuminisha abalebomfya ukusala uko ilyashi lyabo lilingile ukusungilwa elyo nabantu abalingile ukumonako ilyo lyashi elyo nelyashi ilyo balingile ukumona.
Mukulanshanya ukwaliko naba Fast Company, Berners-Lee alandile mukusekesha ukutila icilefwaikwa sana ukucitika pakupanga kwa Inrupt kufwaya "ukwikatilila isonde lyonse."
"Tulingile ukucita ici nombaline," efyo alandile pamulandu wa aka kasolobelo.
"Ninshita imo iikalandwapo kunshita shakuntanshi."
Aka kasolobelo kabomfya tekinoloji ya kasolobelo ka Solid pakusuminisha abalebomfya ukupanga "umwakusungila ilyashi lyabo lyonse pa intaneti" nangu ukupanga POD.
Mulesangwa ubutantiko bwa fintu, ifyakubomba, ubutantiko bwa nshiku, umwakusungila inyimbo elyo notusolobelo tumbi utwacilamuntu pamo notwamilimo.
Aka kasolobelo kali mu musango wakuti Google Drive, Microsoft Outlook, Slack na Spotify fikalasangwa pe buula limo panshita imo ine.
Icipuseneko ku misungile ya lyashi muli aka kasolobelo cakutila cili kuli kabomfya umwine ukusala ilyashi ilyo engalangisha nabantu abengalimona.
Aka kampani kaleita aka kasolobelo ukuti "ukupelwa amaka cila umo ukupitila mu lyashi lyandi."
Imipangilwe ya Inrupt, ukulingana nabakalamba ba kampani ba CEO John Bruce, kufwaya ukuti akampani kabike pamo, imilimo no bwishibilo ubwakwafwilisha ukuti akasolobelo ka Solid kalesangwa ku muntu uuli onse.
Muli aka kampani pali ino nshita mulesangwa ba Berners-Lee, ba Bruce, abalebombela ku bucingo abashitilwe na IBM, ababomfi bambi abengishiwe ukubombela pali uyu mulimo elyo nabambi abaipeleshe ukulaingishamo amanambala.
Ukutendeka uno mulungu, bakapanga batusolobelo twa tekinoloji isonde lyonse kuti bapanga utusolobelo utwabo abene ukubomfya ifibombelo ifili pa webusaiti ya Inrupt.
Berners-Lee atile ena ne bumba lyakwe tabalelanda kuli "Facebook na Google pakuti bengapanga ukwalula ukupya ukwakuti amakwebo yabo yonse yapilibulwe munshita iinono.
"Tatulebepusha ukuti batupeele insambu."
Mu mashiwi ayalembelwe pa Medium pa bushiku bwapa Cibelushi, Berners-Lee alembele ukuti “umulimo” wa kasolobelo ka Inrupt kupeela amaka ya makwebo ne mibombele iyakwafwilisha ukucingilila umucinshi no busuma bwa kasolobelo akapya akapa intaneti aka Solid."
Mu mwaka wa 1994, Berners-Lee apilibwile imibombele ya intantei ilyo apangile akasolobelo ke sonde lyonse aka World Wide Web Consortium pa Massachusetts Institute of Technology.
Mu myeshi iinono iyapitapo, Berners-Lee alilandapo sana pa lyashi lya mulinganya wapa intaneti.
Nalintufye Inrupt ileisulwa, Berners-Lee alekonkanyapo ukuba Kasanga kabili Umukalamba wa Kampani ke Sonde Lyonse aka World Wide Web Consortium, akampani ka Web Foundation elyo na Open Data Institute.
"Ndi nesubilo ilikalamba nganshi pamulandu wa iyi nshita iipya iya kubomba kwa intaneti," Berners-Lee efyo alundilepo ukulanda.
Bernard Vann: Shimapepo wamu WW1 Victoria Cross asefiwa
Shimapepo fye umo uwa cilonganino ca Church of England uwacimfishepo icilambu Victoria Cross munshita ya Nkondo ye Sonde Lyonse iya Bumo uwalwileko ubulwi ewasefiwe mu musumba muntu aleikala apo nomba apapita ne myaka 100.
Ba Lt Col Reverend Bernard Vann bacimfishe ici cilambu pa bushiku bwapa 29 Sepitemba 1918 mu kusansa ukwacitike pa Bellenglise elyo napa Lehaucourt.
Nangu cibefyo, aipaiwe no muntu uwalelasa imfuti panuma ya nshiku shine kabili taishibe nokuti alicimfishe cilya cilambu ca mucinshi uwakulisha mu mpuka shabashilika abaku Britain.
Ilibwe lyakumwibukisha lyasokolwelwe nabeshikulu bakwe babili pakusefya ukwabelele ku Rushden, Northamptonshire, pa Cibelushi.
Umwishikulu wakwe umo, Michael Vann, atile cali "cishibilo icisuma" ilibwe lyalingile ukusokololwa pa numa ya myaka 100 ukufuma apo bawishikulu bacimfishe ici cilambu.
Ukulingana ne pepala lya lyashi ilya London Gazette, pa bushiku bwapa 29 Sepitemba, 1918 ba Lt Col Vann batungulwile impuka yabo mu Canal de Saint-Quentin "ninshi kwali fubefube iyatikamisha ninshi imfuti shilelila ishamitundu iyayafya."
Panuma balile pa mulongo wakulashilalapo "nokushipa ukukulu" ilyo batungulwile abalelisha imfuti ukuya kuntanshi nokulasa imfuti bekafye nokwipayapo abashilika batatu.
Ba Lt Col Vann baipaiwe no mushilika waku Germany pa 4 Okutoba 1918 - ilyo kwashelefye mupepi no mweshi umo ukufika pa kupwa kwa nkondo.
Ba Michael Vann, abali ne myaka 72, batile ifyo bawishikulu bacitile fyali"fintu ifyo ine limbi tekuti ncite lelo fyali fintu ifisuma nganshi.”
Bena pamo nabamunyina ba Dr James Vann nabo balibikilepo amaluba panuma ya kusefya, ukwatungulwilwe naba Brentwood Imperial Youth Band.
Ba Michael Vann batile "baleyumfwa abacindikwa sana pakuba ulubali lwa uku kusefya" nokulundapo ukutila "ululumbi lwamuntu uwabombele ifikulu lumonekela mukutungilila ukupeelwa nabantu abengi."
Abatamba ubwangalo bwa MMA balolela ubushiku bonse ukuti batambe Bellator 206, lelo batambishiwa Peppa Pid
Elenganye ici, mwapembela ubushiku bonse ukwabula ukusendama pakuti mutambe ubwangalo bwa Bellator 206 lelo mwakanishiwa ukutamba ico mwacilapembela.
Ukubilisha ukufuma ku San Jose kwalimo amangalo ya lubuli ayali 13, ukubikapo nayambi 6 ayali pali kadi elyo yaletambishiwa ubushiku bonse mu UK pa mulabasa 5.
Pa nshita ya 6am, ilyofye Gegard Mousasi na Rory MacDonald balepekanishisha ukuti bashokane, bakatamba abamu UK calibapesha amano ilyo umulabasa waishilecinja nokubikapo ubwangalo bwa Peppa Pig.
Abantu bamo tabaumfwile bwino panuma yakwikala ukwabula ukusendama mpaka ku maca necabipishe cakuti bwali bushiku.
Umo uutamba pa Twitter alondolwele ukucinja kwa butantiko nokubatambisha ubwangalo bwa baice cali "kubangasha ukwabipa."
"Caliba lifunde lya buteeko ilyakuti filya ifyo balefwaya ukutambisha tafyalinga ukutambisha pa nshita ya 6 a.m. " efyalandile ba Dave Schwartz, inkonkani yantungulushi ya Bellator ababombela ku kusabankanya nokulanshanya, ilyo baipushiwe pamulandu wa fyacitike.
""Peppa inkumba," ee."
Intungulushi ya kampani ka Bellator ba Scott Coker batile bali nokucinja ubutantiko bwa mitambishishe pakuti bengabimbamo nabatamba abaku U.K. mu nshiku sha kuntanshi.
"Ndetontonkanya ukuti ilyo naelenganya pa kubwekeshapo kwa kutambisha, ndesubila kwena kuti twacita ifyo," efyalandile ba Coker.
"Lelo cili ninshita ya 6 koloko iyapa Sande kulya elyo tekuti tucite ifili fyonse mpaka pa Sande yesu ifwe, iikaba ni pali Cimo kuli bena.
Lelo tulebombelapo.
Ndemyeba icishinka, panumafye yakucinja kwakutamba kwali imbila ishingi ishaletumwa elyo kwena tashaweme iyo.
Twalelwisha ukuti tufiwamye, twaletontonkanya ukuti kulifye ubwafya ubwacitike.
Lelo kanshi tefyo cali, wali mulandu uukumine ubuteeko.
INdemilaya ukuti ici cintu tacakabwekeshepo.
Nomba twakulatambisha amangalo ya lubuli 5 munshita ya 6 - ngefyo tucita lyonse - twalefwaya ukuti tumfwishe bwino abaletamba lelo twalicila mucipimo.
Cali cintu icabulanda."
Desert Island Discs: Tom Daley aleyumfwa 'uwabula incito' pamulandu wa mipangilwe yakwe
Uwangala ubwangalo bwa kowa kwa Olympic Tom Daley atile alekula nokuyumfwa uwabula incito kumuntu uuli onse pamulandu wa mipangilwe yakwe ku mipangile ya cupo - lelo ico ecamupeele ukukoseleshiwa ukuti akacitepo cimo mucalo.
Umulumendo uwamyaka 24 taishibe mpaka lintu aile ku sukulu lya sekondale ukuti "abantu bambi tabali ngaena."
Ilyo alelanda pa mulabasa wa kubalilapo uwa Radio 4 Desert Island Discs mukutungululwa na Lauren Laverne, atile alelanda pa nsambu shabantu abopana bekabeka pakuti engabapela "isubilo."
Kabili atile ukuba umufayshi kwalilengele ukuti acefyeko ukusakamana pamulandu wa kucimfya ama Olympics.
Umuntu uutungulula uku kulanshanya panshita iitali, Kirsty Young, aliba pa cuti pamyeshi imo pamulandu wa kulwala.
Ukumoneka ngo muntu uwabula incito muli pulogilamu yakubalilapo iyakwa Laverne, Daley atile aleyumfwa kwati "ali uwacepako" pa bantu bonse ilyo alekula pantu "tacali icapokelelwa ku bantu ukutemwa abalumendo na bakashana."
Atile: "Ukufika ilelo, ayo malangulushi ayakuyumfwa uwacefiwa, nokuimona uwaibelako, yaliba fintu fimo ifyampela amaka ne nkosho ishakucitapo fimo pa calo."
Alefwaya ukuti ashininkishe ukuti nao "alipo cimo," efyo alandile, pakuti tomfwishishe abantu bamo insoni ilyo baisaishibapo fimo pa mipangilwe yakwe.
Umulumendo uwacimfya ifilambu fibili ifya Bronze muma Olympic alisa sumbulwa sana pali abo abatungila LGBT elyo alibomfya nokumoneka kwakwe pa Mangalo ya Commonwealth aya uno mwaka mu Australia ukulomba ukuti ifyalo nafimbi fifumyeko ifibindo ifyabikwa kubantu abopana bekabeka.
Atile alandile aya mashiwi pantu aleyumfwa uwashuka pakwikala umuntungwa ukwabula ifyakumutitikisha elyo kabili alefwaya nabambi bakakwateko "isubilo."
Umulumendo uwacimfyapo pamiku itatu mwisonde lyonse atile nabatemwanako no mulumendo umo - uupanga amafilimu mu calo ca US uweshina lya Dustin Lance Black, untu akumenye mu mwaka wa 2013 - "nao alinjikete ku mutima icakupapa."
Daley aupile umo uwacimfishe icikombe ca Oscar, uumucilileko ne myaka 20, uyu mwaka lelo atile ukutalukana kwa myaka pakati kabo tacamusakamike.
"Ngacakuti wapita mu fintu ifyakosa ngefi mu nshita ya bwaice bobe" - aile ku kucimfyanya kwama Olympics ilyo ali ne myaka 14 elyo bawishi bafwile panuma ya myaka itatu - atile cali icakosa ukusanga umuntu uwali mu munshiku umo wine uwapitileko mufintu fimo fine ngaena, ifisuma ne fibi.
Aba bantu babili baishileba abafyashi mu mweshi wa Juni, ku mwana umwaume uweshina lya Robert Ray Black-Daley, elyo Daley atile "imimwene yakwe yonse" yalicinja.
"Ngacakuti mwalinjipwishe muli uyu mwaka wafumineko, ubwasuko bwandi lyonse bwaleba bwakuti ndefwaya ukucimfya icikombe ca golide'," efyo alandile.
"Namwishiba, kwaliba ifintu ifikulu fimbi ifyacila pa kucimfya ifikombe fya golide muma Olympics.
Icikombe ca golide candi icama Olympic nomba ni Robbie."
Umwana wakwe akwata ishina limo line ngeshina lyaba wishi abafwile mu mwaka wa 2011 ninshi bali ne myaka 40 panuma yakusangwa na kansa yakuli bongo-bongo.
Daley atile bawishi tabashininkishe ukuti bali mukufwa elyo nelipusho bashilikishe ukwipusha lyapa matiketi yakuila ku London mu 2012 - pantu balefwaisha ukwikala ku fipuna fyakuntanshi.
"Nalifililwe ukubeba ukuti ‘tamwakasangweko tata pakuti mukekale pa fipuna fyakuntanshi'," efyo alandile.
"Nalikete ukuboko kwabo mpaka ilyo balekele ukupema elyo nilintufye balekele ukupema nokufwa elyo naishileishiba ukuti kanshi nabo kuti bacimfiwa," efyo alandile.
Umwaka wakonkelepo Daley alisendelemo ulubali mukucimfyanya kwa 2012 Olympics nokucimfya icikombe ca bronze.
"Nalishibefye ukuti ici eco nalelotapo umweo wandi onse - ukowa kuntanshi ye bumba lya bantu mu ncende ya kumwesu mu Mangalo ya Olympic, tapali icacila palici kubusuma," efyo asosele.
Ecalengele nokuti asale ulwimbo lwaku balilapo ulwakuti - Proud ulwaimbwa na Heather Small - ulo aleimbakofye lyonse ilyo alepekanishisha ukusangwa ku mangalo ya Olympic elyo lwalemupela nokusakamana.
Pulogilamu ya Desert Island Discs ilabako lyonse pa mulabasa wa BBC Radio 4 cila Sande pa 11:15 BST.
Mickelson abikwa pambali pamulandu wakukanateya bwino mu cikombe ca Ryder Cup pa Cibelushi
Umusambashi uwaku America Phil Mickelson akapanga ishina pa Sande ilyo akalateya ubwangalo bwakwe ubwalenga 47 mu cikombe ca Ryder Cup, lelo alingile ukubombesha sana namaka pakucingilila ukukanaba inshita yakwe iyabulanda sana.
Mickelson, uwateyapo mu bwangalo bwa miku ibili mu mwaka pa muku walenga 12, alibikwa pambali na kapitawo wakwe Jim Furyk mu bwangalo bwapa Cibelushi ubwa 4 na 4.
Munshita yakuti abe pakati ka kuteya konse, pamo ngefyo aba lyonse ilyo ateya mu United States, uyu muntu uwacimfyapo pa miku isanao alisapatulula ubushiku bwakwe pakati ka kuba uwasefiwa elyo nokubombela pe bumba lyakwe ukuti awaminishe amafya ayalemucusha.
Uushatala abapo kensha uwafikapo nangufye nipakuwamisha kwa mangalo yakwe, umusambashi wa myaka 48 tekuti akwanishe ukushokana mu bwangalo bwa Le Golf National course, umo ubutali bwa cibansa inshita ishingi buba bwafya kukuuma kwa tumbombo utulefuma munshila.
Elyo ngacakuti ubutali bwa cibansa bweka tekuti bube ubwafya, Mickelson, mu bwangalo bwakwe ubwalenga 9 pa Sande alingile ukushokana no musambashi waku British Open uweshina lya Francesco Molinari, untu babombele pamo nomuntu uwaishibisha ukuteya Tommy Fleetwood pakucimfya amangalo ayali 4 ayo bakwete uno mulungu.
Ngacakuti abena America, abali notukato 4 mukutendeka kwabo ukwakuteya kwa mangalo 12 aya umo-umo, batendeka fye bwino, ubwangalo bwakwa Mickelson bukaba ubwayafyako.
Furyk alicetekela sana uyu muntu, tekumukutila kuti alandapo ifintu nafimbi.
"Aliishiba bwino sana umulimo untu alingile ukucita ilelo, angumako panono panuma nokunkumbatako elyo atila akaba uwaipekanya mu bushiku bwa mailo," efyalandile Furyk.
"Alikwata icicetekelo mu mwine eka.
Niumo pa babombesha ifingi nokusangwa pa Hall of Famer elyo kabili alibomba ifingi ifyakulunda kuli aya mabumba kunshiku shakunuma, elyo nauno mulungu.
Nshaleelenganya ukuti kuti ateyafye imiku ibili.
Nalemutontonkanishisha ukucila pali ifyo, lelo ifyo tefyacitike elyo apo penefye epo twatontonkenye ukuti epo twingapelela.
Alefwaisha ukusangwamo, pamofye ngefilesangwamo bonse."
Mickelson akacila pa kuteya kwakwa Faldo pabantu abateyamo sana mu cikombe ca Ryder Cup ubukateyekwa pa Sande.
Kuti caba nimpela ya kuteya kwakwe ukwamu cikombe ca Ryder Cup uko ukushatala akulingana nobukulu bwa miteyele yakwe palwakwe.
Mickelson alicimfyapo imiku 18, ukulusapo imiku 20 elyo nokuwa amangwa, nangu cakuti Furyk atile ukusangwamo kwakwe kwaliletele ifintu ifisuma ifishingacitwa mwibumba.
"Aliba nefyakusekesha, limo alalanda ifyayafya, uwansansa, alitemwa ukweba abantu ifyakubasekesha, elyo muntu umusuma sana ukukwata mu muputule we bumba," efyo alondolwele.
"Ndesubila ukuti imisepela ishileteya shalimumfwa bwino, pamo fye namuli uno mulungu, uwali uwakusekesha.
Alikwata ifintu ifingi ukucila napa kuteyafye kweka."
Kapitao waku Europe Thomas Bjorn naishiba ukuti ubutungulushi bwakwe ubwaishibikwa sana kuti bwaluba nombaline
Thomas Bjorn, kapitao waku Europe, naishiba ukulingana nefyo amonapo nokupitamo ukutila ukuba pantanshi kwakwe ukwaishibikwa sana ukwakwingila mu nshiku shakushalikisha isha kuteya kwa umo-umo mu cikombe ca Ryder Cup kuti kwamwalukila mukwangufyanya.
Uyu musambashi umwina Denmark amonekele pamuku wakubalilapo mu bwangalo bwamu 1997 pa Valderrama, apo kapitao wa lubali aliko Seve Ballesteros akwete ukucimfya abena America utukato 5 lelo pakushalikisha baishilepwishafye mupepi nokulingana notukato 14½-13½.
"Lyonse uleibuskisha ukutil twali sana pantanshi pa ncende ya Valderrama; twali pantanshi pa Brookline, apo twalushile, elyo napa Valderrama, apo twacimfishe," efyalandile Bjorn, uuli mucikope, panuma yakutamba ba Class of 2018 bacimfya 5-3 pali Cisano na mailo yafumineko nokuba pantanshi no tukato 10-6 pa Le Golf National.
Kanshi ifyacitikapo kunuma fikananga pamo nabonse abali muli lilya ibumba ukuti ili lyashi talilapwa.
Ubushiku bwa mailo ukengilamo na maka yonse.
Ukaye nokucita fyonse ifyo wingacita.
Uyu mulandu tekuti upwe mpaka wakwata utukato utulefwaikwa.
Natukwata ibutukilo, neli ibutukilo kushininkisha ukuti twacimfya icikombe, elyo napali ici epo tutontele amenso.
Efyo nanda lyonse ukutila, amano yandi yonse yaba pali bakateya abali 12 abali ku lubali lwesu, lelo natwishiba bwino sana abo abeminine ku lubali lumbi - bakateya abamaka sana mwisonde."
Mukusekelela pafyo bakateya bakwe babombele mu cibansa icashupa, Bjorn alundilepo ukutila: "Tekuti njeshe ukubomba ukwabula ukuipekanya muli ili lyashi.
Ubushiku bwa mailo bushiku ubwakukumanya iciswango.
Ubushiku bwa mailo bukaba bwakuteya kwacilamuntu ukuleisa, elyo ici cintu cakucita icaibelako.
Cilomfwika bwino ngacakuti muli nomunobe elyo ifintu fileenda bwino, lelo ngacakuti ulifye weka, lyena ninshi uleeshiwa ukufika apo wingapelela nga kateya wa gofu.
Iyi embila iyo ulingile ukusalanganya kuli bakateya, iyakuti mulingile ukufika pa busuma bonse ubwakubomba kwenu ubushiku bwa mailo.
Nomba, washa umunobe kunuma nao uulingile ukubombesha kubusuma bwakwe, cimo cine naiwe."
Mukupashanya kuli Bjorn, inambala yakulubali lumbi Jim Furyk akalafwaya abakuteya bwino sana cilaumo ukucila ifyo bengateya ngacakuti bali mwibumba, ukufumyakofye Jordan Spieth na Justin Thomas, abakwete utukato tutatu pali tune.
Furyk umwine nao alisangwamo muli ishi nshita shakwaluka kwafintu pakulekelesha, ilyo asangilwe mwibumba lyacimfishe pa Brookline ilyo talalusa lintu ba Europe bapangile "Icisungusho pa Medinah."
"Ndeibukisha ishiwi lyonse ilyalandilwe pali ici," efyo alandile mukwasuka ku lipusho lyafyo Ben Crenshaw, kapitao wamu 1999, atungulwile ibumba lyakwe ukuya ku bushiku bwakushalikisha.
"Natukwata amangalo ayakankala 12 mubushiku bwa mailo, lelo kuti mwatemwa ukuya kuli kulya kutendeka kwakubalilapo ngefyo mwamwene pa Brookline, ngefyo mwamwene pa Medinah.
Ilyo amaka ya musango uyu yabafye kulubali lumo, cilabika ukutitikishiwa ku amangalo ayali pakati.
Natutantika bwino abakuteya ukulingana ne nkonka nokubika abalumendo mu musango untu tulemona bwino, namwishiba, tuleesha ukupanga icisungusho mu bushiku bwa mailo."
Thomas napelwa umulimo wakwesha ukutungulula ubulwi bwakubwekesha elyo akalashokana na Rory McIlroy mu bwangalo bwa pamulu, na Paul Casey, Justin Rose, Jon Rahm, Tommy Fleetwood na Ian Poulter abena Europe bambi abali mu lubali lumbi ulwabwangalo.
"Naingile neli ibumba lya balumendo muli uyu musango pantu naletontonkanya ukuti likabomba fyonse ukufika kumpela," efyo Bjorn alandile pamulandu wa kusala kwe bumba lyakwe ilyakuteya kwa umo-umo.
Ubwato bwa nkondo ubwa calo ca German bwatantalishiwa nakabili
Ubwato ubupya ubwa bashilika ba pamenshi aba calo ca German bwalingile ukutendeka ukubomba mu mwaka wa 2014 nokupyanikisha pa mato yamu nkondo ya Cold War ayakotele, lelo tabwatendeke ukubomba mpaka noyu mwaka, pamulandu wa kulubana kwa fibombelo fimo elyo nokunina kwa mitengo ya fintu.
Ukwisula kwa bwato bwa "Rheinland-Pfalz," ubwato bwakutungulula amato yambi aya Baden-Wuerttemberg-class, nomba nakutantalishiwa ukufika mukutendeka kwa mwaka wa 2019, ifi ekulingana na ipepala lye lyashi ilya Die Zeit ilyalembele ifyalandile uulandilako abashilika.
Ubu bwato bwalingile ukwingila mu mpuka ya Bashilika bapa Menshi mu mwaka wa 2014, lelo amafya ayakumine ukutwala kwabwato yalengele ukuti ili lyashi lifikilishiwa.
Amato yane ayeshina lya Baden-Wuerttemberg-class ayo Impuka Yabashilika bapa Menshi yashitile mu mwaka wa 2007 eyaleisa mukupyana pa mato ya Bremen-class ayakotele.
Yashimikwe ukuti yakakwata icakuposa iminshinga icamaka, imisango yaminshinga yandeke na mato yabiye pamo nefisolobelo fimbi ifya tekinoloji, pamo nga icakumwenako apatali, infrared elyo nefyakupiminako ukwenda kwa mato.
Ifintu fimbi ifikankala ifikasangwa muli aya mato pali inshita iitali iyakufiwamishapo - aya mato kuti yasalanganishiwa ukufika ku myaka ibili ukufuma kumulundu.
Nangu cibefyo, ukukonkanyapo kwakutantalisha kulepilibula ukutila amato ayasuma ayaleenekelwa ukucilngilila icalo ca Germany pali bemba, yakaba ninshi nayacepelwa amaka panshita ilyo yakalaingila mu milimo, efyalandile ba Die Zeit.
Ubwato bwa F125 ubulemoneka ngo bushakabombe bwangu ebwali mumalayashi yonse uyu mwaka, ilyo impuka ya Bashilika bapa Menshi yakenye ukwisula ubu bwato nokububwesesha kuncende ya mato ku Blohm & Voss mu Hamburg.
Iyi eyali inshita yakubalilapo iyo impuka ya Bashilika yabwekeshemo ubwato kubabupangile panuma yakupokelela.
Ifyalengele ukuti babwekeshemo ubu bwato tafyaishibikwe sana, lelo imilabasa yamu German yalilandileko ifintu fimo pamo nga "amafya kuli sofutiweya ne fibombelo fimo" ifyo ifingalenga ukuti ubwato bwibomba bwino ngacakuti bwatumwa ku mulimo wa bucingo.
Amafya ya sofutiweya yali ayakankala nganshi pamulandu wa kuti aya mato ya Baden-Wuerttemberg-class yakalabomfiwa nabantu abali 120 - abali ni citika wa bantu ababombela mu mato yakale aya Bremen class.
Cimbi naco, casangilwe ukuti ubwato bwalifinisha sana ico icingacefyako imibombele nokucefya amaka ya Bashilika ayakulundako fimbi ifyakuwamyako.
Ubwato bwa "Rheinland-Pfalz" bwafina 7,000-ton ibwasuminwa ukuti bwalifinapo imiku ibili pa mato ayapalako ayalebomfiwa mu Nkondo Yacibili iye Sonde Lyonse mu German.
Ukulunda pafibombelo fimo ifyali namafya, umutengo wa mulimo onse - ukubikapo nokukansha kwabakwensha - nao buli bwafya ubukulu.
Cishimikwe ukuti umutengo naufika pali €3.1 billion ($3.6bn) - ukufuma pamutengo wakubalilapo uwa €2.2 billion.
Amafya ayalesangwa mu mato ayapya yali ayakankala nganshi mukukonkana nobusoko bwandakai ubwakuti impuka yabashilika bapa menshi mu calo ca Germany yele yalecepako.
Mukutendeka kwa uno mwaka, ba Hans-Peter Bartels, abakalamba ba ciputulwa cabucingo ica calo ca German, batile Impuka ya Bashilika bapa menshi “naicepelwa amato ayo bengatuma ku bucingo."
Balandile ukutila ubu bwafya bulekulilakofye mukuya kwa nshita, pamulandu wakuti amato yakale yalafumishiwapo lelo tapaba yakupyanikishapo yambi.
Baliilishenye pamulandu wakuti tapali nangu bumo pa mato ya Baden-Wuerttemberg-class ubuli nokutendeka ukubomba mu Mpuka ya Bashilika bapa Menshi.
Akabungwe ka National Trust kakutikako ku nkama sha bwikalo bwa milima.
Ukufwailisha ukulecitika pa ncende imo iyamu Scottish Highlands kulefwaya ukwishiba ifyo imilima ibomfya impanga nefyaishingukuka pakusanga ifyakula.
Cileenekelwa ukutila ifikasangwamo ifipya fikafwilishako ukubika ulubuuto ulupya pa mibele ya ishi nama ishipupuka nokwafwilisha ukutungulula pa misungile ya ncende iyakuntanshi.
Uku kufwailisha kwa sayanshi pa National Trust for Scotland kukakonka imilima ya misango iyaseeka elyo na soprano pipistrelle pamo ne milima iyalepa amatwi elyo ne milima ya Daubenton pa Inverewe Gardens mu Wester Ross.
Ifyakukopelako amashiwi fikabibikwa mu ncende ishashinguluka iyi ncende pakulakonka bwino ifyo imilima shicita inshita yonse.
Ababomfi bapa NHS pamo nabo abaipeleshe bakalafwailisha ukubomfya utusolobelo twakuminwe.
Ukuceceta kwa fiunda ukwashika kukalacitwa pa fiunda fyonse pakumfwa imililile ya milima elyo ne misano ya milima iilecita ifintu ifyapusanapusana.
Mapu ya iyi ncende ne nsebo lyena fikabomfiwa pakupanga icikope icikulu icancende elyo ne mibele ya milima.
Ba Rob Dewar, bampandamano ba misungile ya filengwa na Lesa pa NTS, baleenekela ukuti insebo ishikasangwa shikasokolola bushe nincende nshi ishaba sana ishikankala ku milima elyo nefyo ishi ncende shibomfiwa kuli cila musango wa milima.
Ili lyashi likafwilishako ukwishiba ubukankala bwa kusungilila incende ishapala inika elyo nefya kusunga bwino imiteengo ya fimiti umwikala imilima elyo nefilengwa na-lesa fimbi.
Impendwa ya milima mu Scotland namu UK naicepelako muli senchari iyapita.
Iletinishiwa ukuloba pamulandu wa fikulwa nemilimo ya buyantanshi iilefulunganya incende sha fyuni nokonaula kwa bwikalo bwafyuni.
Fimashini fyakupanga amalaiti ukubomfya umwela pamo namalaiti nafyo fileleta ubusanso, pamofye namapepala ya muti wakwipaila balunshi ne miti imo iyo bawamishako ifkulwa, pamofye nokuliwa nabapushi.
Imilima tempofu iyo.
Nangu cibefyo, pamulandu wa misango yaiko iyakulungilamo, amatwi yashiko eyabomfiwa sana ukucila amenso ilyo shileikata ifyakulya.
Shilabomfya umusango wakumfwilamo iciunda umo uwaibela uwakwishibilako apali ifishishi elyo nefyakucinga munshila yashiko.
Akabungwe ka NTS, akabomba umulimo wa kusunga kwa fikulwa ifili 270 ifyakale, ama galadeni ayakankala ayali 38 elyo nama hekita 76,000 ayampanga ukushinguluka ici calo balisakamana sana pa milima.
Aka kabungwe kalikwata abakanshiwa abali ikumi, ababomba imilimo yakufwailisha, ukuceceta incende shakutushishamo elyo munshita shimo nokushipususha.
Aka kabungwe kalipangako nencende iyakubalilapo kabili iyabafye yeka mu calo ca Scotland iyakusungilako imilima pa Threave estate mu Dumfries na Galloway, ukusangwa imisango 8 pa misango 10 iya milima iisangwa mu Scotland.
Umukalamba wa iyi ncende David Thompson atile iyi ncende encendefye iyalinga uko imilima shingekala.
"Pano pa Threave twalikwata incende iikulu iyamilima," efyo balandile.
"Twalikwata ifikuulwa ifyakale, ifimiti ifingi ifyakale elyo nencende iisuma iyabwikalo bwa fyuni.
Lelo kwaliba nafimbi ifyapa milima ifishilaishibikwa, kanshi imilimo iyo tulebomba pali ino ncende ikatwafwilishako ukumfwikisha bwino ifyo imilima shifwaya pakuti shikale bwino."
Balondolwele ubukankala bwa kuceceta kwa milima ilyo tabalabomba umulimo wakuwamya ifuklwa pantu ukonaula kwa ncende imo iitushamo ifyuni kuti kwaipaya ifyuni ifikota no twana ukufika kuli 400, ico icingonaula impendwa yonse iisangwa pali iyo ncende.
Imilima yalicingililwa kabili mulandu ukwipaya, ukucusha nangu ukufulnganya nangufye ukonaula incende iyo shikalamo
Ba Elisabeth Ferrell, abakalamba ba kabungwe ka Bat Conservation Trust mu calo ca Scotland, balikoselesha abekala calo ukuti nabo bengaibimbamo mukwafwilisha.
Balandile ukuti: "Kuli ifintu ifingi ifyo tulingile ukusambilia pa milima yesu pantu pa misango iingi iyo twakwata tatulati twishibe ifyo shileikala."
Ronaldo akana ku lyashi lya mutunganya wa kulungana no muntu ku maka ilyo bandubulwila balepekanya ukutwala German magazine ku cilye
Cristiano Ronaldo atile umulandu untu balemutunganya ilya kulungana no muntu ku maka "lya bufi," nokutila "abantu bamo balefwaya ukuisumbula" ukupitila mukubomfya ishina lyakwe.
Bandubulwila bakwe balepekanya ukutwala ku cilye ipepala lye lyashi ilyaku German ilitwa Der Spiegel, ilyasabankenye ili lyashi lya mutunganya.
Kateya wa mupila muli ba Portugal naba Juventus ewatunganishiwa no mulandu wa kulungana kumaka na namayo umwina America, uweshina lya Kathryn Mayorga, mu muputule we hotela lyaku Las Vegas mu mwaka wa 2009.
Cisoselwe ukuti panuma ya ifi alimupeele indala ukufika kuli $375,000 pakuti ekalanda ifyacitike, efyalandile ipepala lya Der Spiegel pali Cisano.
Mukulanda kwakwe ukwapa Vidyo yapa Instagram kubantu abali 142 million panuma ye lyashi lyamutunganya, Ronaldo, uuli ne myaka 33, akene kuli uyu mutunganya nokutila "lyashi lyabufi."
"Awe, awe, awe, awe, awe.
Ifyo bacilanda ilelo, lyashi lyabufi," umusambashi uwacimfyapo imiku 5 mu cikombe ca Ballon d'Or efyo asosele ninshi alelolesha muli kamera.
"Balefwaya ukuisumbula ukubomfya ishina lyandi.
Filacitika.
Balefwaya ukuti beshibikwe ilyo balumbula ishina lyandi, lelo encito yabo.
Ndi muntu uwansansa kabili fyonse fileendafye bwino," efyo alundilepo, ninshi alemwentula.
Bandubulwila bakwa Ronaldo balefwaya ukutwala ipepala lye lyashi ilya Der Spiegel ku cilye pamulandu wa uyu mutunga, untu batile, "ukusabankanya ilyashi ilyabula ukushininkisha ilyankama sha muntu," ukulingana no mulabasa wa Reuters.
Ndubulwila uweshina lya Christian Schertz atile kateya wa mupila kuti afwaya icifuta mulandu pamuladu wa "ukonaula kwa nkama sha muntu mukukonkana no kutoba kwe funde, icaba mulandu uwakakata sana mukufulunganya insambu sha muntu mu myaka iyapitapo."
Ili lyashi lya mutunganya lishimikwe ukuti lyacitike mu mweshi wa Juni mu 2009 mu muputule wa Palms Hotel and Casino mu Las Vegas.
Panuma yakukumana mu cikulwa ca bwalwa, Ronaldo na Mayorga bashimikwe ukutila balibwelele ku muputule wakwa kateya wa mupila, kuntu cishimikwe ukuti alyulungene nankwe ku maka ukupitila ku numa, ukulinga na mapepala ayatwelwe ku Clark County District Court mu Nevada.
Mayorga atile Ronaldo awile pa makufi panuma ya fyacitike nokutila naliba "99 persent" umuntu "umutuntulu" ukubulishakofye "1 pesent"
Aya mapepala yalandile ukuti Ronaldo alisumine ukuti cishinka balilele pamo lelo nico balisuminishenye.
Mayorga nao atile alile ku kapokola nokuyakopesha ifikope fya fikwebululwa ku cipatala, lelo panuma alisumine ukupwishisha umulandu kunse ya cilye pantu "aletina ukulandula" elyo nokutina "ukusebana ku cintubwingi."
Uyu namayo uuli ne myaka 34 atile alefwaya nomba ukubwesulusha uyu mulandu pantu alikonkanyapofye ukucushiwa no mutima pamulandu nefyacitike.
Ronaldo ali panshita yakwingila mwi bumba lyaba Real Madrid ukufuma kuli ba Manchester United panshita ilyo ili lyashi lyacitike, elyo pali iyi nshita aselele kuli ba Juve abaku Italy pa ndalama ukufika kuli €100 million
Brexit: Icalo ca UK 'cikaiseka umuyayaya' pakulusa bakapanga ba myotoka
Icalo ca UK 'cikaiseka umuyayaya' ngacakuti calusa icifulo caciko icakuba bakapanga ba myotoka panuma ya Brexit, efilandile ba Business Secretary ba Greg Clark.
Balundilepo ukutile "cilekuma " ilyashi ilyalandile ba Toyota UK kuli ba BBC ukutila ngacakuti ba Britain bafuma mu EU ukwabula ukulanshanya bwino ninshi bakeminika ukupanga kwa mamotoka pa ncende ya Burnaston, mupepi na Derby.
"Tulekabila ukusuminishanya," efyasosele ba Clark.
Bakapanga ba mamotoka abaku Japan batile ifingacitika pakukokola kwa kwisula kwa mipaka pamulandu wakukanakwata ukulanshanya kwa Brexit kuti kwalenga abengi incito ukupwa.
Incende yakupangilapo iyaku Burnaston - apapangilwa amamotoka ya Toyota Auris na Avensis - yapangile ukufika ku mamotoka 150,000 uyu mwaka elyo 90% pali ayo yalishitishiwe ku fyalo fimbi ifyamu European Union.
"Ilangulushi lyandi lyakuti ngacakuti Britain yafuma mu EU pampela ya mweshi wa Kutumpu tukamona ukuti ukupanga kwaiminikwa mu ncende yesu," efyalandile ba Marvin Cooke, abakalamba ba kampani ka Toyota pa Burnaston.
Utwampani tumbi utupanga amamotoka mu UK natulanga ukusakamana palyashi lyakufuma mu EU ukwabula ukusuminishanya pafyo amakwebo yakwabuka imipaka yakalabombeka, ukubikapo naba Honda, BMW elyo na Jaguar Land Rover.
Kucakumwenako, ba BMW, batile bakesala incende ya Mini ku Oxford pa mweshi umo panuma ya Brexit.
Amasakamiko ayakulile sana ukukuma kuli bakapanga ba mamotoka batile musango wakushitishishamo ngacakuti tapali ukulanshanya kwa Brexit.
Imipangile yaba Toyota ibomba "ukukonkana ne nshita", ilyo ifipe fyakupangila fifika lyonse panuma yamamineti 37 ukufuma kubabashitishako ifipe mukati ka UK namu EU ifya mamotoka ayapangwa ninshi nayakwata kale abakushita.
Ngacakuti icalo ca UK cafuma mu EU ukwabula ukusuminishanya pa 29 ya mweshi wa Kutumpu, kuti paba ukufulunganishiwa pa mupaka ico batile kuti calenga kwaba ukucelwa nokubulisha kwa fipe.
Kuti caba icakosa nganshi kuli ba Toyota ukwikala pa ncende ya Derbyshire ubushiku bumo ukwabula ifyakupangila, efyo akampani kalandile, neci kuti calenga imipangile ukwiminina.
Ba Clark batile amapange yaba Theresa May ayabwampano bwakuntanshi ne cisaka ca EU "yalipangwa bwino sana pakutalusha ifi fintu ifingacitika pa mupaka."
"Tulekabila ukusuminishanya. Tulekabila ukukwata ukulanshanya nokusuminishanya ukusuma ukukatusuminisha ngefyo nsosele tekukwatafye ubuyantanshi bwapali ino nshita lelo nokutifye tukwate ili ishuko," efyo balandile ku mulabsa wa BBC Radio 4 pali pulogilamu iitwa Today.
"Ifishinka ukufuma kuli ba Toyota nabakapanga bafipe bambi fyakuti tulingile ukukonkanyapo icintu icaba lyonse icakutwafwa mu makwebo yesu."
Akampani ka Toyota takalandile inshita iingapitapo pakuti bese batendeke ukubomba nakabili, lelo mukuya kwa nshita, balipeela ubusoko bwakuti imitengo yafipe ngayakula kuti cacefya amaka ya mipangile ayakucimfyanya nabambi elyo kabili kuti calenga ne ncito sha bantu ukupwa.
Ba Peter Tsouvallaris, ababombelapo pa Burnaston pa myaka 24 elyo kabili eba kalamba ba kabungwe ka babomfi pali iyi ncende, batile bamembala babo nabasakamana sana: Ukulingana nefyo namonapo, incito sha musango uyu tashimoneka nakabili ngashapwa.
Abalandilako ubuteeko batile: "Twalipekanya ubwanshiko ubusuma kabili ubwafikapo pa bwampano bwesu ubwakuntanshi ne cisaka ca EU."
Ukukumana kwaba Trump naba Rosenstein kuti kwatantalishiwa nakabili, efilandile ba White House
Ukukumana kwaba Donald Trump ukwayafya naba deputy attorney general ba Rod Rosenstein kuti "kwatantalishiwa nakabili pa mulungu umo" ilyo ubulwi bwa wasalwa ukuya ku supreme court ba Brett Kavanaugh bulekonkanyapo, efyalandile ba White House pa Sande.
Ba Rosenstein ebalolekesha pa milimo yakwa shicilye uwaibela Robert Mueller, uulefwailisha ukufulunganishiwa kwa kusala kwaku Russia, ubwampano pakati kabakafwilisha baba Trump na Russia elyo nokucilinganya kwa bupingushi ukwaba kateeka.
Ngacakuti ba Trump bakatamfya inkonkani yakwa attorney general nangu iyo, umo umwingafuma ubusanso ku buntungwa bwaba Mueller, elyashi ililandwapo mu musumba wa Washington pa myeshi iyapita.
Mukutendeka kwa uno mweshi, ipepala lya New York Times lyalandile ukuti ba Rosenstein balepanga ukusenda akasolobelo akakulakopa amashiwi yonse ayo bakalalanda naba Trump nokumona ngacingacitwa icakufumyapo ba kateeka ukubomfya ukwalula kwefunde ukwalenga 25th.
Ba Rosenstein balikana kuli aya mashiwi.
Lelo pa bushiku bwapali Cimo iyafumineko baile ku White House, ilyo kwaumfwikilwe amashiwi yakuti balefwaya ukuleka imilimo.
Munshita yakuti cibefyo, ukukumana naba Trump, abo pali iyo nshita bali pa cisaka ca United Nations mu New York, kwalitantalishiwa ukutwalwa pali Cine.
Ba Trump batile kuti "batemwa" ukukanatamfya ba Rosenstein incito lelo ukukumana kwalitantalishiwa pakubutuka ku kupinkana nokulubulula kwa kabungwe ka Senate judiciary committee umo ba Kavanaugh na namayo umo uwabalumbwile mu mulandu wa kufwaya ukulungana nankwe ku maka, Dr Christine Blasey Ford, bonse balubulwile.
Pali Cisano, ba Trump bakambishe ukufwailisha kwaba FBI ukwamulungu umo mu milandu yaba Kavanaugh, ico icatantalisheko ivoti lyaba Senate.
Kalemba we lyashi uwaba Trump, Sarah Sanders, ewamonekele pa Fox News pa Sande.
Ilyo aipushiwe pamulandu wa kukumana kwaba Rosenstein, atile: "Ubushiku bwa uku kukumana tabulabikwa, kuti bwaba uno mulungu, kuti caba ni ulya mulungu pamulandu wafintu ifilecitika ku supreme court.
Lelo tukalanda elyo kabili lyonse nalitemwa ukwishibisha imilabasa pafilecitika."
Bashimilabasa bamo kuti bakana kuli uku kulanda: Ba Sanders tabatala abatekeshapo ilyashi na bashimilabasa ku White House ukufuma pa 10 Sepitemba.
Uwatekeshe iyi pulogilamu Chris Wallace alipwishe icalengele.
Ba Sanders batile ukucepelwa kwa kulanshanya nabashimilabasa tekukanakatemwa kwa "kumonekela," kwaba shimilabasa bapa TV,” nangu cakuti batile: "Nshakane icishinka cakuti balitemwa ukumonekela."
Kabili balandile ukutila ukulanshanya kwaba Trump na bashimilabasa kwalafulilako.
"Bakateeka besu balitemwa ukulongana kwa Mepusho na Masuko ukucila bakateeka bonse abakunuma," efyo balandile, mukulundapo ukwabula ukulandapo ilyo fyacitike: "Twaliloshapo pali ifyo fipendo."
Ukulanshanya kulekonkanyapo ukulacitika, efyo ba Sanders balandile, nomba "ngacakuti bashimilabasa nabakwata amepusho ayakwipusha bakateeka ba calo ca United States abene, ico kuti cawamishapo ukucila ukulanda naine.
Tulesha ukucita ifyo inshita ishingi kabili mwalimona ilyo twacitapo ifyo mu mulungu uwapita elyo kabili ifyo efikacitika pa nshita kulanshanya na bashimilabasa ilyo mwingalanda kuli bakateeka ba calo ca United States."
Ba Trump ishinta ishingi balasuka amepusho ilyo balefuma pa White Housenangu ilyo baleyasuka amepusho nangu pa kukumana kwa milabasa na beni abetwako.
Ukulanshanya na bashimilibasa palwabo beka takwaseeka.
Mu musumba wa New York uno mulungu bakateeka balilangishe icilenga, ukumonekela kwakuitemenwa elyo napanshita shimo ukwakupumikisha ku mabumba ya bashimilabasa.
Ba kalemba ba ciputulwa ca Bumi nabalembela ababombi baku cisaka ca EU ababa pa NHS ku Scotland pamulandu wa masakamiko ya Brexit
Ba Kalemba ba Ciputulwa ca Bumi ebalembele ku babomfi ba cisaka ca EU abalebombela pa ncende ya NHS ku Scotland ukubatasha sana pakukonkanyapo ukubomba pali iyi ncende panuma ya Brexit.
Ba Jeane Freeman MSP ebatumine inkalata ilyo kwashalafye imyeshi mutanda ukufika apo icalo ca UK calafumina mu cisaka ca EU.
Ubuteeko bwa calo ca Scotland bwalipanga kale ubutantiko bwakulipila indalama shonse ishilebomfiwa ku kwipusha kwa mikalile ya bakela-calo bamu EU abalebombela muncende shabo.
Mu nkalata yabo ba Ms. Freeman balembele ukutila: "Munshita ya lusuba, ukulanshanya pakati ka calo ca UK ne cisaka ca EU ukwaiminikwe kwalikonkanyapo, ukutungulula ku busalo ilyo cikalafika ku nshita ya mibundo uno mwaka.
Lelo Ubuteeko bwa calo ca UK bwalitendeka ukupekanya ifyakucita ngacakuti kwakana ukuba ukulanshanya ukwayana.
Ninjishiba ukuti iyi kuti yaba inshita iyayafya nganshi kuli imwe.
ici ecilengele ukuti mfwaye ukulanda nomba pafyo nacindika imilimo yonse iyo cila mubomfi abomba, ukwabula ukulolesha pa calo ico afumako.
Mwe babomfi banandi ukufuma cisaka ca EU monse, nokucilamo, mulaleta ubwishibilo ubwafikapo ubukosha nokuwamya imibombele ya ciputulwa ca bumi, nokunonsha abalwele pamo nende isho tubombela.
Scotland ecalo cenu mucishinka elyo kabili tulefwaisha ukuti imwe mwikale kuno."
Christion Abercrombie Abombelwapo Mukampampa Panuma ya Kuceneka Icilonda ku Mutwe
Kateya wamu Tennessee State Tigers Christion Abercrombie ewabombelwepo mukampampa panuma yakuceneka icilonda ku mutwe ilyo bateyele ubwangalo bwa pa Cibelushi umo bacimfiwe 31-27 kuli ba Vanderbilt Commodores, efyalandile Mike Organ uwaku Tennessee.
Kakansha mukalamba uwe bumba lya Tennessee State Rod Reed aebele bakasenda wa lyashi ukuti ici cilonda cacitike ilyo kwashelefye panono ukuya mukutuusha pakati ka kuteya.
"Aselele kumbali yamushilwa nokwisaponafye umwine," efyo ba Reed balandile.
Bakakansha nababombela kufyabumi balipeelako Abercrombie umwela palyapene elyo bamusendele ukuyamuceceta bwino.
Umukalamba umo ukufuma ku Tennessee State aebele ba Chris Harris abaku WSMV mu Nashville, Tennessee, ukutila Abercrombie alifuma mukubombelwapo ku Vanderbilt Medical Center.
Ba Harris balundilepo ukutila tapalaba "ifishinka ifili fyonse ifya musango no bukulu bwa cilonda" elyo ba Tennessee State baleesha ukufwailisha inshita ilyo ici cilonda cacenneke.
Abercrombie, nikateya wamupila uuli mu mwaka wa cibili pa sukulu, ali mukuteya kwakubalilapo naba Tennessee State panuma yakusela ukufuma kuli ba Illinois.
Alikwete ukuteya ukuli 5 pa Cibelushi ilyo talafumamo, ico icalengele nokuti ibumba lyakwe likwate ukuteya konse pamo ukuli 18.
Abaleshita ifipe abakunse ya calo bakalalipilishiwa imisonko iikulu ilyo bashita ifipe mu UK
Abaleshita ifipe abakunse ya calo bakalalipilishiwa imisonko iikulu ilyo bashita ifipe mu UK nendalama ishakulundapo ishikalayafwilisha abashakwata pakwikala ukukonkana na mapange yaba Tory.
Uku kubomba kukapwisha amaka yaba Corbyn ayakufwaya ukongola bakasala imisepela.
Uyu musonko wamapepala yafipe ukalipilishiwa kuli abo abashilipila umusonko mu UK
Icibikilo ca Ndalama cileenekela ukulapanga indalama ukufika kuli £120 cila mwaka ishakwafwilisha abashakwata pakwikala
Abaleshita ifipe abakunse ya calo bakalalipilishiwa imisonko iikulu ilyo bashita ifipe mu UK - nendalama ishakulundapo ishikalayafwilisha abashakwata pakwikala, ba Theresa May balebilisha ili lyashi ubushiku bwa lelo.
Uku kubomba kukamonwa ngo kwakwesha ukupwisha amaka yaba Jeremy Corbyn ayakufwaya ukongola bakasala imisepela abalelaya ukuti bakalapeela amayanda ayanaka imitengo nokulalungama abakwatisha indalama.
Uyu musonko wamapepala yafipe ukalipilishiwa ku bantu no twampani utushilipila umusonko mu UK, nendalama ishakulundapo shikafwako Ubuteeko ukubombela pa kucefya kwa mafya yakubulisha apakusendama.
Uyu musonko - uuli musonko wakulunda ku musonko wakale, ukubikapo naumbi uwapamulu uwalundilweko imyaka ibili iyapita ku mayanda ya cibili elyo nayakusonkesha - kuti wafika pali 3 pesenti.
Icibikilo ca Ndalama cileenekela ukulapanga indalama ukufika kuli £120 million cilamwaka.
Ukufika kucipendo ca 13 pesenti ya fikuulwa ifyamu London efishitwa nabantu abashili bamu calo ca UK, ukukosha imitengo nokucilenga icayafya kubekala calo abengafwaya ukushita pakuti bengaba pali abo abakwata amayanda.
Incende ishingi ishikankala ishamu calo shalisanguka "amatauni ya milungulwa" pamulandu wabashita aya mayanda abakunse ya calo abapwisha inshita iitali kunse ya calo.
Ifunde ili ilipya lyaisa panumafye ya milungu itatu apo ba Boris Johnson balombele ukuti kube ukucefyako imisonko pakuti imisepela nayo ingakwatako amayanda.
Balandile ukuti abakuula amayanda balikosha sana imitengo ya mayanda ukupitila mukukwata impanga lelo ukwabula ukuibomfya, elyo balombele naba May ukuti balabeko ku fibindo fyapa mayanda ayenganakako imitengo pakuti “umusebanya wa kubulisha apakwikala” mu Britain wingacepako."
Ba Corbyn ebalandile pa lyashi ilisuma pa mapange ya kuwamya imikalile, ukubikapo nokutungulula imisonko elyo nokupwisha ukufumishiwa mu mayanda "apabula icilubo".
Kabili batile bali nokupeela amabuteeko yacikaya amaka ayakulakuula amayanda ayapya.
Ba May abatile: "Uyu mwaka nalandile ukuti ndinokuipelesha pa butungulushi bwandi kukubwesulusha iciloto ca calo ca Britain - pakuti ubwikalo bwingawama ku nkulo yonse iipya.
Neci cilepilibula ukuwamya imishiika ya mayanda yesu iyafulungana.
Icalo ca Britain cikabafye lyonse icaisuka ku bantu abalefwaya ukwikalamo, ukubombelamo nokukuulamo ubwikalo.
Nangu cibefyo, tekuti cibe bwino icakuti kuti caba icayanguka kubantu abashikala mu UK, pamofye no twampani twakunse ya calo, mumusango umo wine ngabena Britain ababopmbesha mu calo cabo.
Ku bantu abengi iciloto cakuikwatila amayanda caliba ukutali sana, elyo nokubulisha kwa mucinshi pamulandu wakubulisha apakusendama nako kulekulilakofye."
Jack Ross: 'Ubukabilo bwandi ubwakubulisha bwakutungulula Scotland'
Umukalamba wa Sunderland Jack Ross atile "ubukabilo bwakwe ubwakulisha" bwakwisaba umukalamba wa Scotland pa nshita imo.
Umusambashi uwaku Scotland, uuli ne myaka 42, aletontonkanya nensansa pa mulimo wakubukulusha ibumba lyaku North-East, ililesangwa pa cifulo calenga butatu mu League One, na matoni yatatu ukufuma pamulu.
Akukile ku Stadium of Light muli luno lusuba panuma yakubwesesha ba St Mirren mu Scottish Premiership munshita yakuteya iyafumineko.
"Nalefwaisha ukuteya mwi bumba lya calo candi nga kateya.
Nalikwete akasote ka B ckabili capelele napo pene," efyo Ross aebele ba BBC Sportsound abaku Scotland.
"Lelo nakulile ninshi ndetamba ibumba lya Scotland pa Hampden inshita ishingi na batata, neci ecintu cimo icambwesesha kunuma.
Nangu cibefyo, ishuko kuti lyaisafye ngacakuti, nakwanisha ukubomba bwino mu kutungulula kwe bumba."
Abatungulwile kunuma yakwa Ross ngabakatungulula ba Sunderland pali ba Dick Advocaat, David Moyes, Sam Allardyce, Martin O'Neill, Roy Keane, Gus Poyet elyo na Paulo Di Canio.
Uwali kale umukalamba we bumba lya Alloa Athletic atile taleumfwa umwenso mukukonka panuma ya mashina ayaishibikwa pe bumba ilikulu ngeli, panuma yakukana ukwitwa kuli ba Barnsley naba Ipswich Town.
"Ukubomba kwandi ukusuma pali ino nshita kukapimwa mulipusho lyaku ‘Bushe kuti nabwesesha ili ibumba mukuteya kwa Premier League?'
Pamulandu wa mipangilwe ya fikuulwa fya ili ibumba, cishinka icakuti ili bumba lilingile ukuba mu Premier League," efyo alandile.
"Temulimo uwayanguka ukufisha ili bumba kulya, lelo nkaimona fye ukuti nabomba bwino ngacakuti nafikilisha ukutwala ibumba kulya."
Ross apwilemofye imyaka itatu mu milimo ya butungulushi, panuma ya nshita iyo abombele nga inkonkani ya ntungulushi pa Dumbarton elyo ne myeshi 15 iyakukansha ibumba lyaba Hearts.
Kabili alyafwileko ba Alloa ukufuma panshi sana ukuya pa namba 3, nokupilibula ba St Mirren ukufuma mupepi nokuwa ukubaleta mu kucimfya kwa Championship panshita yakuteya iyakonkelepo.
Kabili Ross atile aleumfwa bwino sana pali ino nshita ukucila nefyo aleumfwa ilyo aleteya muli ba Clyde, Hartlepool, Falkirk, St Mirren naku Hamilton Academical.
"Nakuba yali ninshita yakupanga ubusalo ubwakosa," aibukishe ifyo cali, pakutendeka ukutungula ibumba lya Alloa.
"Mucishinka ninjishiba ukuti umulimo wa butungulushi ewaningile, ukucila napa kuteya umupila.
Cileumfwika icakusungusha pantu nalibomba bwino, nalipangilemo ubwikalo ubusuma, nokumfwa bwino ilyo nali pamulu.
Lelo ukuteya kulaba ukwakosa inshita shimo.
Kwaliba ifintu ifyo ulingile ukupitamo cila mulungu.
Naino ine nshita ndapitamo mufya ifyo pamulandu wa masakamiko nefyakutitikisha kwa iyi ncito lelo ubutungulushi bwena buleumfwika fye bwino.
Inshita shonse nalefwaya ukubapo intungulushi kabili ilelo ndetungulula, cileumfwika icintu icawamisha nganshi ukucila ifyo naumfwapo mumweo wandi onse uwabukalamba."
Kuti mwakutika ku kulanshanya konse pa Sportsound pa bushiku bwapa Sande, 30 Sepitemba, pa mulabasa wa Radio Scotland pakati ka 12:00 na 13:00 BST
Inshita iisuma iyakunwapo aka painti nipa Cibelushi ne nshita ya 5.30pm, efyo ukufwailisha kulandile
Ukukaba kwamu lusuba nakulenga utubale twamu Britain ukutendeka ukubomba bwino ukucila ifyo ifikuulwa fyakulilamo filebomba.
Amakwebo ya tubale nayaninako pali 2.7 pesenti mu Julai - lelo ifintu tafyali bwino mu ncende shakulilamo umo amakwebo yaponene ne cipendo ca 4.8 pesenti, efyo ifipendo fyasokolwele.
Ba Peter Martin, ababomba mukabungwe kabumpandamano bwa makwebo aka CGA, akakolonganike ifi fipendo katile: "Ukukonkanyapo kwakukaba elyo nokufula kwakusendamo ulubali mumangalo ya Cikombe ca Calo ukwa calo ca England kulepilibula ukuti umweshi wa Julai wakonkele umusango umo wine uwa mweshi wafumineko uwa Juni, ilyo utubale twaile pamulu ne cipendo ca 2.8 pesenti, ukufumyakofye ukutila ifikulwa fyakulilamo fyena nafibwelelako panuma.
Ukubwelela panshi ukwa makwebo yafyakulya ukwa 1.8 pesenti mu Juni kwalibipileko mu mweshi wa Julai.
Utubale tonse utushitisha ifyakunwa twalibomba bwino sana mukupashanya ku fikuulwa fya kulilamo ifyakulya.
Utubale utushitishako nefyakulya nato twalibwelelako panshi, lelo tekufika pacipendo cakubwelela panuna ukufika ku cipendo ica fikulwa fya fyakulya fyekafyeka.
Cilemoneka kwati abantu balefwayafye ukuya mukunwa.
Ukushinguluka utubale twa bwalwa tonse amakwebo yalinina mu mishitishishe ukufika pali 6.6 pesenti muli uyu mweshi, ilyo amakwebo ya fyakulya yabwelele panshi na 3 pesenti."
Ba Paul Newman, abaku kabungwe kakufwailisha pa misngo yakuisekesha nokusunga kwa bantu aka RSM batile: "Ishi nsebo shilelangisha umubela umo wine uwamoneka ukufuma mu kupwa kwa mweshi wa Shinde.
imiceele pamo nefilecitika pamulandu wa mangalo nokulongana ukwingi efilengele sana ukuti kube ukushitisha ukwingi ukwa mishika yamu mayanda.
Cishile nge cisungusho ukutila ifikulwa fyamakwebo ifyakulilamo nafikonkanyapo ukushupikwa, nangu cibefyo ukubwelela panshi ukwa fipendo ukufika kuli 4.8 pesenti ukupashanya ku mwaka wafuminepo kukabipisha ukulunda pa mitengo yafintu iilebipilakofye.
Ukukonkanyapo kwa kukaba kwa lusuba tekuti kwise panshita iyakosa ngeyi kuli abo abashitisha ifyakulya elyo kabili ninshitafye eikalanda ngacakuti imiceele iyatalalako iyo tukwata mu mweshi wa Kasaka-ntobo kukalenga ukuti amakwebo yakacinje kubusuma."
Ukukula kwa mishitishishe mu makwebo ya fyakulya ne fyakunwa, ukubikapo na makwebo ayapya, kwafikile pali 2.7 pesenti mu mweshi wa julai, ukulangisha ukubwelela panshi ukwa fipe ifipya.
Akabungwe ka Coffer Peach Tracker akafwailisha amakwebo yamu tubale ne fikulya fyakulilamo mu calo ca UK kalakolonganya ukufwailisha kwa makwebo ukufuma ku mabumba ayali 47 ayabomba iyi milimo, umo umusangwa ubukumu bonse pamo ukufika kuli £9 billion, elyo kabili aka kabungwe ekaba icakumwenako muli aya makwebo.
Umwana umo pa bana abali 5 balakwapo akaunti yapa fitunshitunshi iyo bafisa ku bafyashi babo
Umwana umo mu bana 5 - bamo ukucepa napa myaka 11 - balikwatapo ukulanshanya kwapa fitunshitunshi uko bafika ku bafyashi nabakafundisha babo, efyo ukufwailisha kusokolwele.
Ukufwailisha pa basambi baku sekondale abali 20,000 kwasokolwele ukufula kwama peji ya "instagram ayabufi"
Ili lyashi nalileta ukusakamana ukwakuti limbi ifiletumwa pali aya mapeji fintu ifyamuselu
20 pesenti ya basambi batile balikwata akaunti iikulu iyo bengalangisha ku bafyashi
Umwana umo pa bana abali 5 - bamo ukucepa napa myaka 11 - balepanga akaunti yapa fitunshitunshi iyo basunga nge nkama ukufuma ku bakalamba.
Ukufwailisha pa basambi baku sekondale abali 20,000 kwasokolwele ukufula kwama peji ya "instagram ayabufi" - ukulanda pa kasolobelo kakubikapo ifikope aka instagram.
Ili lyashi nalileta ukusakamana ukwakuti limbi ifiletumwa pali aya mapeji fintu ifyamuselu.
20 pesenti ya basambi batile balabomfyapo akaunti “iikulu” iyabusaka iyo bengalangisha ku bafyashi babo, elyo ninshi nabakwatako nama akaunti yambi ayapambali.
Umufyashi umo uwasangile akaunti iyamubumfisolo iya mwana wakwe umukashana uuli ne myaka 13 asangile uyu mwana alepatikisha abanankwe ukuti "mulungane naine ku maka."
Uku kufwailisha, ukwacitilwe naba Digital Awareness UK elyo nakabungwe ka Headmasters’ and Headmistresses’ Conference (HMC) akamasukulu ayaibombela, kwasangile ukutila 40 ppesenti yabana abali ne myaka 11 ukufika pa 18 balikwete ama pulofailo yabili, elyo citika wa abo bana balandile ukuti balafisa ama akunti ya pambali.
Abakalamba ba kabungwe ka HMC ba Mike Buchanan batile: "Cabulanda nganshi icakuti imisepela iletunkwa mukupanga incende sha pa intaneti umo abafyashi na bakafundisha babo tekuti bashimone."
Eilidh Doyle eukaba "ishiwi lya balubilo" mu butungulushi bwa Scottish Athletics
Eilidh Doyle eusalilwe ukuba membala wa butungulushi bwa Scottish Athletics ukuba nge ntungulushi iishili pa bakalamba ba butungulushi pa kulongana kwa mwaka ukwa kabungwe kakalamba.
Doyle emuntu umo mu Scotland pali bakabutuka balubilo uwacimfyapo ifilambu ifingi mu bwangalo bwakubutuka ulubilo elyo abakumupando ba Ian Beattie balondolwele uyu mulimo nge shuko ilikalamba kuli abo abaletungulula ubu bwangalo ukuti benganonkelamo ukufuma ku bwishibilo ubukalamba ubo uyu mukashana akolongani mwisonde lyonse pa myaka ikumi iyapitapo.
"Eilidh alicindikwa nganshi mu mangalo yamu Scotland, UK elyo ne sonde lyonse kuli abo ababutuka ulubilo elyo kabili tuli ne subilo lyakuti ubwangalo bwa lubilo mu calo ca Scotland bwalanonkelamo nganshi pakumuleta mukabungwe ka butungulushi," efyo ba Beattie balandile.
Doyle atile: "Ndi uwaipekanya ukuba nge shiwi lyabangala ubwangalo bwa lubilo kabili ndesubila ukuti kuti nalundako ubukumu nokwafwilisha ukutungulula ubu bwangalo mu calo ca Scotland."
Uyu mukashna umwina America, uwacimfishe ulubilo lwama mita 200 na 400 pa Mangalo yamu 1996 mu Atlanta pa fikombe fya golide ifyama Olympic kabili incenshi yaku BBC, ashele uushingenda panuma yakucula kuli sitiloko.
Alembele pa Twitter ukutila: "Ukufika ilelo papita umweshi umo apo nakwatile ubwafya bwa sitiloko.
Nalefilwa ukwenda.
Bashing’anga batile inshitafye eikalanda ngacakuti nkabafye bwino elyo napantu ukuba bwino kukapelela.
Wali mulimo uwakosa lelo nalishilebafye bwino, nalisambile ukwenda nakabili elyo ilelo ndecita ifyakunjafwilishako ukwensh umubili!
Ndetasha sana pa mashiwi ya cikoseleshi!"
Ukusabankanya kwa cakukaminako umukaka ukulepashanya banyinefwe ku ng’ombe kwaleta ukupatulukana pa intaneti
Akampani kabombela mukukama umukaka nakaleta ukupatulukana kwa bantu pa intaneti pakusabankanya uko kapashenye ba namayo ku ng’ombe isho balekama umukaka.
Pakwisula kwa kutendeka ukwa cintu icisoselwe ukuti "icakubalilapo mwisonde lyonse icakufwala icakukaminako umukaka," akampani ka tekinoloji aka Elvie kalipanga ukusabankanya ukwaibelako mulwimbo lwa vidyo umulelangishiwa ubuntungwa ubo icakukaminako umukaka cilepeela kuli banamayo abaleonsha.
Banamyao abali 4 balangwa baleshana mwitanga umuli ifyakulya fya ng’ombe ku lwimbo ulukwete amashiwi yakutila: "Ee, ndaikama umukaka, lelo tekuti mumone umucila" elyo "ngacakuti tamulolekeshe aya te mabele ya ng’ombe, mabele ya bantu."
Ulwimbo lwakonkanyapo: "Lipompe, lipompe, ndelisha abana, lipompe, lipompe, ndekama abakashana bandi."
Nangu cibefyo, uku kusabankanya kwa makwebo, ukutuminwe pe buula lya Facebook ilya aka kampani, nakuleta ubulwi pa intaneti.
Ukufika ku cipendo ca batambile abali 77,000 elyo nefyakulandapo ukufika ku myanda iingi, iyi vidyo naipokelela amashiwi ayasankana, nabengi baletila ileyangusha ifintu “ifibi” ificitika mu makwebo yakushitisha umukaka.
"Busalo ububi sana ukubomfya ing’ombe ukusabankanya ici cibombelo.
Umuntu umo alembele ukuti, pamofye ngaifwe nasho shilemita nokukwata abana, ukufmyakofye ukuti shena shilapokwa abana mu nshiku ishinono panuma yakufyala.
Akasolobelo kakukamina umukaka aka Elvie kalekala bwino sana mukati ka bula yakwa namayo uuleonsha (Elvie/Nyina)
Umuntu umbi nao atile: "Cilemoneka icakufulunganya kuli banyina pamofye no mwana.
Lelo nomba cinshi mushingabomfesha ku kusabankanya kwa cakukaminako umukaka icabafyashi abasunga abana babo?"
Umbi nao alundilepo ukutila: "Ukusabankanya ukwafuma munshila."
Abantu bambi nabo balitungilile uku kusabankanya, elyo namayo umo atile ulwimbo "luleumfwika bwino."
"Ndetontonkanya ukuti uku kubomba ukusuma.
Naine wine kuti nakwatako kamo ngacakuti ndeonsha.
Ukukama umukaka kwalengee ukuti njumfwe kwati ndi ng’ombe.
Uku kusabankanya kuliko ukwayafya lelo nakusendelefye fintu kuli.
Ici cipe icamano," efyo umo alembele.
Umuntu umbi nao atile: "Uku kusabankanya kuleya kuli banamayo abakama umukaka (ilingi muncito shabo nangu mu fimbusu) nokuyumfwa nge "ng’ombe."
Uku tekusabankanya ukuletasha nangu ukupingula amakwebo ya mukaka."
Pampela ya vidyo ibumba lyaba namayo lyasokolola ukuti bonse bacilashana ninshi bali notwakukamina umukaka muma bula yabo.
Ilyashi ilili muli uku kusabankanya lishintilile pa mashiwi ayo banamayo abengi abakama umukaka balanda ayakuti bayumfwa kwati ni ng’ombe.
Nangu cibefyo ka Elvie Pump, takakwatata icongo, takakwata intambo nangu amatumbo elyo kekala mukati ka bulaa, ukusuminisha banamayo ukulaenda, ukwikata abana babo elyo nokuyafye kumbi ninshi balekamam umukaka.
Ba Ana Balarin, ababomfi kabili ba ECD pa Mother batile: "Ka Elvie Pump kabombelo akasuma sana icakuti kalefwaya ukusabanka ukwamaka pakutendeka ukukabomfya.

Uyu temuku wakubalilapo ilyo akabombelo ka Elvie pump kamonekela mu lyashi.

Imyanda ne Myanda iya Bana ba Baleingila mu Calo Baseshiwa mu Mutalalila Ukutwalwa ku Nkambi ye Tenti ku Mupaka wa Texas
Impendwa ya bana ba baleingila mu calo abatekwa naiya pamulu nangu cakuti ukwabuka kwapa mipaka ukwacila mweshi kwabafye cimo cine, ici nipamulandu wa fikomo ifyakosa ifyapangwa no butungulushi bwaba Trump nacikosha inshila shakupelelamo abana kubakubatungilila.
Ukulingana nefyo caba, abatungilila abengi nabo bantu baingile mucalo ukwabula ifipepala, elyo balomfw aumwenso wakuti nabo bene kuti batamfiwa mucalo ngacakuti baisa pabwelu ukutila bapele ubwafwilisho ku mwana uuli onse.
Ubu bwafya bwakosele sana mu mweshi wa Juni, ilyo abakalamba ba buteeko balandile ukuti abakupela ubwafwilisho bwakutungilila elyo nabambi abakalamba bamundupwa balingile ukuleta ififwati fya minwe yabo, elyo nefishinka fyabo fimbi ku bakalamba abalolesha ku kwingila kwamu calo.
Umulungu wapwile, ba Matthew Albence, abakalamba bamo aba kabungwe ka Immigration and Customs Enforcement, balandile kuntanshi ya Congress ukutila akabungwe kaliikatako impendwa ya bantu abaipeleshe ukuti bafwilisheko abana abaleingila mu calo abashakwete abafyashi.
Akabungwe panuna kalandile ukuti 70 pesenti ya abo bantu abaiketwe tabasangilwepo no mulandu untu bacitapo kale.
"Mupepi na 80 pesenti ya bantu abafwilisha nangu bamembala ba mayanda ayabakafwilisha baisa muli cino calo ukwabula isambu, elyo abengi pali abo babutuka imilandu ku fyalo uko bafuma.
Kanshi tulekonkanyapo ukulafwailisha abo bantu," efyo ba Albence balandile.
Mukufwaya ukupwisha ili lyashi lya bana mukwangufyanya, abakalamba bakabungwe baliletako amafunde ayakuti bamo pali aba balemonekela mu cilye panumafye ya mweshi umo uwakwikatwa kwabo, ukucila panuma ya nshiku 60, uwali emusango balebombelamo kale, ukulingana nababomfi bapa nkambi.
Abengi bakalamonekela ukupitila mu kulanshanya kwapa intaneti ukwa vidyo, pakuti bengalubulula ku milandu yabo iyakwingila mucalo kuli kapingula wa iyi milandu.
Abo abakasangwa ukuti tabalingile bakabwekeshiwamo mukwangufyanya.
Ukukokwesha kwa bana muli bucitente, kukabalenga ukuba abasakamana nokucushiwa ku mitima, icingalenga ukuti babe ababunkalwe elyo nokwesha ukufyuka, ifi ekulingana na mashiwi yababomfi abapali iyi nkambi elyo ne nsebo ishaletwapo muli iyi mibombele mu myeshi iyapitapo.
Abalandilako abana batile aya masakamiko yalekulilako pancende iikulu pamo nga Tornillo, uko ifishibilo fyakumwenako ukuti umwana alecushiwa ilingi tafiposwako amano, pamulandu wabukulu bwa ncende.
Balundilepo ukutila ukusesesha abana ku musumba wa matenti ukwabula ukubapeela inshita iyalinga iyakuipekanya elyo nokulaya ifibusa kuti kwakoseshako ukucushiwa uko bakwete nakale.
Icalo ca Syria caeba ‘abashilika’ ba calo ca US, France na Turkey ukufuma mu ncende yabo nombaline
Mukulanda ku kabungwe ka UN General Assembly, ba Foreign Minister Walid al-Moualem kabili baliyeba imbutushi sha calo ca Syria ukubwelela ku calo cabo nangu cakuti inkondo nomba naifika mu mwaka walenga 8.
Ba Moualem, ababomba panshita imoine ngaba Prime Minister batile impuka sha bashilika ba fyalo fimbi shili muncende yabo ukwabula insambu, mukabepesho kakulwisha buntala-misoka, elyo “bali nokubombelwapo ukulingana nenkonka."
"Bafwile ukufumamo nombaline elyo kabili ukwabula nefyakupindikapo”, efyo baebele akabungwe.
Ba Moualem balikomaila pakutila "inkondo yakulwisha buntala-misoka ili mukupwa" mu Syria, umo abantu ukufika kuli 360,000 balifwa ukufuma mu mwaka wa 2011, elyo nabengi balifulumuka mu mayanda yabo.
Batile umusumba wa Damascus ukakonkanyapo "ukulwisha ubu bulwi ubwashila mpaka tukafumye mu ncende sha Syria" amabumba yonse ayamunsokwe elyo "nabonse abalesangwamo ukufuma ku fyalo fimbi."
Icalo ca United States calibikamo abashilika ukufika ku cipendo ca 2,000 mu Syria, abo abalekansha nokupanda amano ku bashilika abena Kurdy nama Arab abaku Syria abashifwaya ubutungulushi bwakwa Kateeka Bashar al-Assad.
Icalo ca France calibikamo abashilika ukufika kuli 1,000 mu calo icafulunganishiwa ku nkondo.
Pa mulandu wa mbutushi, ba Moualem batile icalo ciliko bwino icakuti kuti babwela elyo kabili baliilishanya pa "fyalo fimo ifyaku kabanga" pamulandu wa "kusalanganya umwenso ku bantu" uwalengele imbutushi shiletina ukubwela kumwabo.
"Twalilomba ku bekala calo abe sonde lyonse notubungwe twa bwafwilisho ukuti bafwilisheko ukubwela kwa bantu," efyo balandile.
"Baleingishamo amashiwi ya fikansa fya calo mu lyashi ilingabafye ilyabwafwilisho."
Icalo ca United States ne cisaka ca European Union fyalisoka icalo ca Syria ukutila takwakatale akuba ubwafwilisho bwakukuula cipyacipya mpaka kukabe ukumfwana nokusuminishanya pakati kakwa Assad elyo nabantu apinkana nabo pakuti inkondo ipwe.
Abeminishi ba cisaka ca UN batile ukusuminishanya pakati ka calo ca Russia na Turkey ukwashalikishe ukwakupanga incende yakupatulwilapo abashilika muncende umwaba sana bacisanguka iya Idlib nakulenga ukuti pabeko isubilo lyakukonkanyapo ukulanshanya.
Akulanshanya kwapakati ka bena Russia nabena Turkey kwalilengele ukukanabako kwa kusansa kwabena Sirya abatungililwe ne calo ca Rusia pali iyi provinsi, uko ukwikala abantu ukufika ku cipendo ca 1 milyoni.
Lelo ba Moualem balandile ukuti ukusuminishanya kwalikwete "inshita shakupwilapo ishaishibikwa" nokulanga isubilo lyakuti ukubomba kwa bashilika kukalungama ama jihadists ukubikapo naba Nusra Front ababa mwisamba lya Al-Qaeda, "abakapwishishiwafye nakalya-nakalya."
Abeminishi ba cikasa ca UN ba Staffan de Mistura balesubila ukuti kukaba ukukumana kwa komiti iipya umukasangwa ba membala ba buteeko nabakanya ubuteeko mukupanga ipepala lya mafunde ilyakubomba panuma yakupwa kwa nkondo mu Sirya nokusuminisha ukuti kwingaba ukusala.
Ba Moualem balilandile ifikomo fyakukonka ku buteeko bwa calo ca Syria pakuti bengasangwa muli iyi komiti, nokutila imilimo ya aka kabungwe "kupituluka mu fikomo ifyaba mu lupapulo lwa calo ululipo," elyo balisokele nokuti kwikaba nangu umo uwakucilinganya iyi milimo.
Icikalenga Ukuti ba Trump Bakawine Temu ya Cibili
Ukukonkana nobu bwile, Ba Trump kuti bawina ukusala cipyapya ukwamu mwaka wa 2020 kanofye, ngefyo abengi ama liberal balesubila ukuti, ukumufumyapo ku maka ne mpasase kuti fyapwisha bwangu ukuteeka kwakwe.
Mucintu icilemoneka ukuti ecikaba "ilyashi ilyayafya nganshi ilya mipwile ya butekeshi bwa muntu!"
Pali ino nshita, takulati kube ifishibilo fya kunaka kwabaletamba.
Ukufuma mu 2014, ukupima kwa nshita iyo abantu batamba sana kwalilundapo pamiku ibili ukufika kuli 1.05 million pa CNN elyo nokulandapo imiku itatu ukufika kuli 1.6 million pa MSNBC.

Icalo ca U.S Nacipima Ukupanika ba El Salvador Pakutungilila Kwabo ukwa Calo ca China, Napanuma Ukuibwelamo
Aba cipani cama Diplomats bamwene ukuti icalo ca Dominican Republic na Panama fyalisumina kale ubutungulushi bwa musumba wa Beijing, nokukanishiwa ukunono ukufuma ku musumba wa Washington.
Ba Trump balikwete ukulanshanya ukusuma naba Kateeka ba Juan Carlos Varela abaku Panama mu Juni 2017 elyo balikwete ne hotela mu Panama mpaka abo balebomba nabo batamfishemo Akabungwe ka butungulushi bwaba Trump.
Abakalamba ba Ciputulwa ca Calo basalile ukubwesulusha abakalamba ba beminishi ba calo ca America ukufuma ku El Salvador, ku Dominican Republic elyo naku Panama pamulandu wa "masalo yakushalikisha ayakukanasumina mu butungulushi bwa Taiwan," efyalandile ba Heather Nauert, abalandilako iciputulwa, mu mashiwi ayo balandile mukutendeka kwa uno mweshi.
Lelo ukukanda kwaletontonkanishiwafye pali El Salvador, iyapokelele ukufika kuli $140 million mu ndalama sha bwafwilisho ukufuma ku calo ca America mu mwaka wa 2017, ukubikapo nokupindululu kwa kushitisha kwa miti ikola, ubuyantanshi no bwafwilisho ku makwebo.
Ifyakubakandilako ifyalandilwe, apali nokuputula kwa bwafwilisho bwa ndalama elyo nokubinda kwa fitupa fyakwendela, ngafayli ifyakosesha mu calo camu Central America umo abantu abengi tababomba elyo umwafula nokwipayana.
Panshita ilyo ukulanshanya kulecitika, abakalamba ba buteeko bwa fyalo fyamu North America na Central America nabatantalisha ukulongana kwakulolesha pa bucingo no bunonshi bwa calo ukukonkana nokulongana ukwapalako ukwacitilwe umwaka wapwile ukwamwenwe ngo lutampuko ulupya mukwesha ukucingilisha abengila mu calo ukukanaya ku calo ca United States.
Lelo ilyo cafikile pakati ka Sepitemba, abakalamba babuteeko balandile ukuti balefwaya ukulongana kukatwalile, ukupwilishisha bwino ukukandwa ukuli konse ukwa calo ca El Salvador.
Inkonkani ya ba Kateeka ba Mike Pence pali ino nshita nabaipekanya ukuyalanda pali uku kulongana, ukukabako pakati ka Lusuba-lukalamba, mucishibibilo ca butungulushi bwa ciputulwa cakwingisha ifipe muncende pa kulongana uku, efyo abeminishi balandile.
Na abeminishi batatu abaku America balibwelelemo mu mutalalila ku El Salvador, Panama na Dominican Republic ukwabula imbila ishipya ishakosa nangu ukukandwa ukufuma ku musumba wa Washington.
Abalandilako White House ba Bolton balikana ukulandapo ifili fyonse pa fishinka fya kulanshanya ifyalondolwelwe nabeminishi bakalamba abaku America batatu, ukubikapo nabeminishi babili abasumine ukulanshanya ifishinka ifyalandilwe mukulaiwa ukuti bekalumbulwa amashina.
Ama akaunti yabo yalishininkishiwe nakafwailisha uwakunse uwapalamina sana ku butungulushi kabili nao alandile mukulaiwa ukuti takalumbulwe amashina.

Graham Dorrans uwamuli ba Rangers ali nesubilo pantanshi yakushokana naba Rapid Vienna

Icilonda cape kufi ecacingilishe kateya wapakati ka cibansa Graham Dorrans ukukana monekela mu bwangalo bwa kubalilapo mukuteya kwa iyi nshita mpaka mu bwangalo ubo bawile amangwa 2-2 naba Villarreal lelo ali ne subilo lyakuti ba Rangers kuti babomfya ifyatumbwike muli uku kuteya ngecakubafwako ukucita ifikulu.

Limbi ngatwaliwinine pakulekelesha lelo, mukucimonafye, ukuwa amangwa cali cintu icisuma.
Mu cipande cakubalilapo balibomba bwino elyo naifwe twaliisabomba bwino mu cipande cabubili nokuba bwino pali bena.
Ilyo tuleya pali Cine, bukaba bushiku bumbi nabo mu calo ca Europe.

Ndesubila, kuti twaya pantanshi nomba, ukubika ifyacitike mu kuteya kwapwile kunuma yesu nokuba bakacimfya."
